revenue  n. 税收收入；财政收入；收益...a boom year at the movies, with record advertising revenue and the highest ticket sales since 1980.…电影业欣欣向荣的一年，广告及票房收入都创下1980年以来的最高纪录。
reward  n. [劳经] 报酬；报答；酬谢A bonus of up to five percent can be added to a student's final exam score as a reward for good spelling, punctuation, and grammar.作为对正确的拼写、标点和语法的奖励，多达5分的加分可以加到学生期末考试成绩中。The firm last night offered a $10,000 reward for information leading to the conviction of the killer.这家公司昨晚对能将凶手定罪的信息悬赏1万美元。Make the extra effort to impress the buyer and you will be rewarded with a quicker sale at a better price.格外卖力地给买主一个好印象，你就会被报以用更佳的价格更快地卖掉商品。The company is just starting to reap the rewards of long-term investments.这家公司正开始收获长期投资的回报。
rigorous  adj. 严格的，严厉的；严密的；严酷的The selection process is based on rigorous tests of competence and experience.挑选过程是建立在对能力和经验严格缜密的考核的基础之上的。...rigorously conducted research.…严格进行的研究。He is rigorous in his control of expenditure.他在控制开支方面一丝不苟。
sample  vt. 取样；尝试；抽样检查You'll receive samples of paint, curtains and upholstery.你将收到涂料、窗帘和座套的样品。We're giving away 2,000 free samples.我们正在赠送2000件免费样品。They took samples of my blood.他们采了我的血样。We based our analysis on a random sample of more than 200 males.我们把我们的分析基于二百多名男性的一组随机抽样。We sampled a selection of different bottled waters.我们品尝了挑选出来的各种瓶装水。...the chance to sample a different way of life.…体验一种不同生活方式的机会。
secretary  n. 秘书；书记；部长；大臣...a former Venezuelan foreign secretary.…一位前任委内瑞拉外交部长。
site  n. 地点；位置；场所I was working as a foreman on a building site.我在一个建筑工地当工头。Scientists have described the Aral sea as the site of the worst ecological disaster on earth.科学家们把咸海描绘成地球上生态环境最差的地方。...the site of Moses' tomb.…摩西墓遗址。He said chemical weapons had never been sited in Germany.他说从未在德国部署过化学武器。...controls on the siting of gas storage vessels.…对煤气储存罐选址的种种限制。It is cheaper to have extra building work done when the builder is on site, rather than bringing him back for a small job.趁建筑工人在工地上时叫他们完成额外的建筑工作要比叫他回来做一点小工便宜。There is ample car parking off site.外面有个很大的停车场。
skeptical  adj. 怀疑的；怀疑论的，不可知论的
slump  vi. 下降，衰落；倒下；大幅度下降，暴跌Net profits slumped by 41%.净利润暴跌了41%。The council's land is now worth much less than originally hoped because of a slump in property prices.由于地产价格的暴跌，委员会的土地目前大不如原来所希望的那么值钱了。...the slump of the early 1980s.…20世纪80年代初期的经济萧条时期。She slumped into a chair.她瘫倒在一张椅子上。
specialize  vi. 专门从事；详细说明；特化...a University professor who specializes in the history of the Russian empire.…一位专门研究沙俄历史的大学教授。This degree offers a major specialization in social policy alongside a course in sociology.该学位提供一门社会政策主专业课和一门社会学课程。
stimulate  vt. 刺激；鼓舞，激励America's priority is rightly to stimulate its economy.美国的首要任务自然是刺激经济。...an economy in need of stimulation.…一个需要刺激的经济。Bill was stimulated by the challenge.比尔受到该挑战的激励。It is a complex yet stimulating book.这是一本复杂却能引发兴趣的书。Exercise stimulates the digestive and excretory systems.运动刺激消化和排泄系统。...the stimulating effect of adrenaline.…肾上腺素的刺激作用。
strategy  n. 战略，策略The energy secretary will present the strategy tomorrow afternoon.能源部长将于明天下午提出该策略。I've just been explaining the basic principles of strategy to my generals.我刚才一直在向我的将军们解释战略的基本原则。
sufficient  adj. 足够的；充分的One yard of fabric is sufficient to cover the exterior of an 18-in.-diameter hatbox.一码的布料足够罩住18英寸直径帽盒的外部。Lighting levels should be sufficient for photography without flash.照明程度对无闪光灯摄影应该足够了。She recovered sufficiently to accompany Chou on his tour of Africa in 1964.她康复到足以在周的1964年非洲之旅中伴随他。
suspicious  adj. 可疑的；怀疑的；多疑的He was rightly suspicious of meeting me until I reassured him I was not writing about him.他对于见我充满疑虑，直到我向他再次保证我不是在写有关他的东西。"What is it you want me to do?" Adams asked suspiciously.“你要我去干的是什么？”亚当斯怀疑地问道。Two officers on patrol became suspicious of two men in a car.两位巡警对一辆小汽车内的两名男子起了疑心。He reported that two suspicious-looking characters had approached Callendar.他报告说两名看似可疑的人曾靠近过卡兰德。They'll question them as to whether anyone was seen acting suspiciously in the area over the last few days.他们将询问这些人过去几天是否在该地区发现行迹可疑的人。
sustain  vt. 维持；支撑，承担；忍受；供养；证实He has sustained his fierce social conscience from young adulthood through old age.他从青年时代到晚年一直保持着强烈的社会良知。Recovery can't be sustained unless more jobs are created.除非有更多的工作机会被创造出来，否则复苏无法保持下去。Every aircraft in there has sustained some damage.那里的每架飞机都遭到了一些损坏。The cash dividends they get from the cash crop would sustain them during the lean season.他们从经济作物中得到的那些现金红利能支撑他们度过歉收季节。
switch  vt. 转换；用鞭子等抽打Leona put some detergent into the dishwasher, shut the door, and pressed the switch.利昂娜在洗碗机里放了些清洁剂，关上门，然后按下开关。Estonia is switching to a market economy.爱沙尼亚正在向市场经济转变。The law would encourage companies to switch from coal to cleaner fuels.法律会鼓励各公司从用煤转向使用更清洁的燃料。The spokesman implicitly condemned the United States policy switch.这位发言人含蓄地谴责了美国政策上的转变。Within a few years the whole country will switch over to digital television.几年内全国将会换上数字电视。My mother's interest had switched to my health.我母亲的兴趣已转移到我的健康上来了。In half an hour, they'd switched the tags on every cable.半个小时内，他们换了每根电缆的标签。
temporary  adj. 暂时的，临时的His job here is only temporary.他在这儿的工作只是暂时的。Most adolescent problems are temporary.多数青春期的问题都是暂时的。The peace agreement has at least temporarily halted the civil war.该和平协议至少已暂时中止了内战。
transfer  n. 转让；转移；传递；过户Transfer the meat to a platter and leave in a warm place.把肉转到一个大浅盘中，然后搁在一个温暖的地方。Arrange for the transfer of medical records to your new doctor.安排把医疗记录转给你的新医生。The decision to transfer the investigation from the police to the district attorney's office is a mutual one.将调查从警方移交到区律师办公室的决定是共同做出的。...the transfer of power from the old to the new regimes.…从旧政权到新政权的权力移交。I was transferred to the book department.我被调到了图书部。I suspect that she is going to be transferred to Fort Meyer.我怀疑她将被调到迈耶堡。They will be offered transfers to other locations.他们将得到去其他地方的调动令。Such information is easily transferred onto microfilm.这样的信息很容易被转录到微缩胶片上。It can be connected to a PC for the transfer of information.它可以连接到个人电脑上进行信息转录。
trial  n. 试验；审讯；努力；磨炼New evidence showed the police lied at the trial.新的证据表明警方在审判时撒了谎。I have the right to a trial with a jury of my peers.我有权要求由和我一样的平民组成的陪审团参加审判。They have been treated with this drug in clinical trials.他们在临床试验中一直接受这种药物的治疗。I took the car out for a trial on the roads.我把车开出去在公路上试了一下。...the trials of adolescence.…青春期的磨难。the idea has been trialled in several schoolsMany drugs were found by trial and error.许多药物都是经过反复试验后才被发现的。He is currently on trial for drunk driving.他目前因酒后驾车而受审。The president will be drawn into a damaging battle in which his credentials will be on trial.总统将被拖入一场破坏性的斗争，他正陷入信任危机。He was found to be mentally unfit to stand trial.发现他精神状况不适合接受审判。
tumble  vi. 摔倒；倒塌；滚动；打滚；仓惶地行动A small boy tumbled off the porch.一个小男孩从门廊上摔了下去。He injured his ribs in a tumble from his horse.他从马上摔下来伤了肋骨。Profit after taxes tumbled by half to $15.8 million.税后利润猛降了一半，跌到了1580万美元。Share prices continued to tumble today on the Tokyo stock market.东京股市今天的股票价格继续暴跌。Oil prices took a tumble yesterday.石油价格昨天一阵暴跌。Waterfalls crash and tumble over rocks.瀑布在岩石上撞击翻滚。
undergo  vt. 经历，经受；忍受New recruits have been undergoing training in recent weeks.新兵们最近几周一直在接受训练。
upset  vt. 使心烦；颠覆；扰乱After she died I felt very, very upset.她死后，我感觉非常非常难过。Marta looked upset.玛尔塔看起来很沮丧。...stress and other emotional upsets.…压力和其他情感上的烦恼。The whole incident had upset me and my fiancée terribly.整个事件已使我和我的未婚妻非常烦恼。She warned me not to say anything to upset him.她警告我不要说任何让他心烦的话。Childhood illness can be upsetting for children and parents alike.童年的疾病能使孩子和父母同样苦恼。These latest comments could upset the peace negotiations which are due to begin next week.这些最新的评论可能搅乱定于下周开始的和平谈判。Markets are very sensitive to any upsets in the Japanese economic machine.市场对日本经济机器里的任何混乱都是非常敏感的。Don't upset the piles of sheets under the box.别碰乱了盒子下面的那几摞纸。Paul was unwell last night with a stomach upset.保罗昨晚胃不舒服。Larry has an upset stomach.拉里胃不舒服。
volunteer  n. 志愿者；志愿兵She now helps in a local school as a volunteer three days a week.她现在作为一名志愿者每周3天在当地一所学校帮忙。Right. What I want now is two volunteers to come down to the front.对了。我现在需要的就是两个自告奋勇者到前面来。Aunt Mary volunteered to clean up the kitchen.玛丽姨妈主动要求打扫厨房。He volunteered for the army in 1939.他在1939年自愿参军。The room was quiet; no one volunteered any further information.房间里很安静；没有人主动提供更多的信息。"They were both great supporters of Franco," Ryle volunteered.“他们俩都是佛朗哥的坚定支持者，”赖尔主动说道。They fought as volunteers with the Afghan guerrillas.他们作为志愿兵与阿富汗游击队一起战斗。
yield  vt. 屈服；出产，产生；放弃Carmen yielded to general pressure and grudgingly took the child to a specialist.卡门屈服于普遍的压力，不得已带孩子去看了位专科大夫。He may yield control.他可能放弃控制权。When entering a trail or starting a descent, yield to other skiers.进入滑道或开始下滑时，给其他滑雪者们让行。...examples of common signs like No Smoking and Yield.…像“禁止吸烟”和“让行”这样的常见标志例子。He reached the massive door of the barn and pushed. It yielded.他够着了畜棚厚重的大门推了推。门开了。Last year 400,000 acres of land yielded a crop worth $1.75 billion.去年40万英亩的土地出产了价值17.5亿美元的粮食。...improving the yield of the crop.…增加农作物的产量。It yielded a profit of at least $36 million.它带来了至少三千六百万美元的利润。...a yield of 4%.…4%的收益。The high yields available on the dividend shares made them attractive to private investors.股息股能获得的高收益使它们对私人投资者们很有吸引力。This research has been in progress since 1961 and has yielded a great number of positive results.这项研究自1961年以来一直在开展，已经取得了大量的积极成果。
absorb  vt. 吸收；吸引；承受；理解；使…全神贯注Plants absorb carbon dioxide from the air and moisture from the soil.植物从空气中吸收二氧化碳，从泥土中吸收水分。A household radiator absorbs energy in the form of electric current and releases it in the form of heat.家用暖气以电流的形式吸收能量，然后以热量的形式将其释放出去。City schools were absorbed into the countywide school district.市立学校被并入了郡学区。...footwear which does not absorb the impact of the foot striking the ground.…不能缓冲脚踏在地面上所产生的冲击力的鞋子。The banks would be forced to absorb large losses.这些银行将被迫承担那些巨大的损失。It absorbed vast amounts of capital that could have been used for investment.它消耗掉了原本可以用作投资的大量资本。Too often he only absorbs half the information in the manual.通常，他对手册里的信息只是一知半解。...a second career which absorbed her more completely than her acting ever had.…一个比其演艺事业更让她全身心投入的第二职业。
absurd  adj. 荒谬的；可笑的That's absurd.那是荒谬的。It's absurd to suggest that they knew what was going on but did nothing.暗示说他们知道怎么回事但却袖手旁观是荒谬的。Connie had a sharp eye for the absurd.康妮对荒谬之事有敏锐的眼光。Prices were still absurdly low, in his opinion.在他看来，价格依然低得荒谬。
accomplish  vt. 完成；实现；达到If we'd all work together, I think we could accomplish our goal.如果我们齐心协力，我想我们能实现我们的目标。
accumulate  vi. 累积；积聚Lead can accumulate in the body until toxic levels are reached.铅可以在体内积聚直至到达有毒的程度。
achieve  vt. 取得；获得；实现；成功There are many who will work hard to achieve these goals.有很多人会努力工作来实现这些目标。
acquaintance  n. 熟人；相识；了解；知道He exchanged a few words with the proprietor, an old acquaintance of his.他跟一位业主，他的一位老相识交谈了几句。...a writer who becomes involved in a real murder mystery through his acquaintance with a police officer.…一位通过他同一名警官的结识而卷入一起真正的谋杀谜案的作家。I first made his acquaintance in the early 1960s.我在20世纪60年代初第一次认识了他。
addict  n. 有瘾的人；入迷的人He's only 24 years old and a drug addict.他只有24岁，可已经是一个瘾君子。She is a TV addict and watches as much as she can.她是一个电视迷，看尽可能多的电视。
adequate  adj. 充足的；适当的；胜任的One in four people worldwide are without adequate homes.世界上1/4的人没有足够的住房。She is prepared to offer me an amount adequate to purchase another house.她准备好了给我一笔足以购买另一所房子的钱。Many students are not adequately prepared for higher education.很多学生没有为高等教育做足准备。
adolescent  adj. 青春期的；未成熟的It is important that an adolescent boy should have an adult in whom he can confide.一个青春期男孩应该有一个他能倾吐心声的成年人，这是很重要的。Young adolescents are happiest with small groups of close friends.年轻的青春期少年们和一小圈亲近的朋友在一起时最高兴。
adverse  adj. 不利的；相反的；敌对的（名词adverseness，副词adversely）The police said Mr. Hadfield's decision would have no adverse effect on the progress of the investigation.警方说哈德菲尔德先生的决定对于调查进展不会有任何不利的影响。Price changes must not adversely affect the living standards of the people.价格变化一定不能负面地影响人们的生活水平。
alert  vt. 警告；使警觉，使意识到We all have to stay alert.我们都必须保持警觉。The drug improved mental alertness.这种药物提高了大脑的灵敏度。The bank is alert to the danger.该银行对这种危险有警觉。There has been criticism of how his administration handled last week's terrorism alert.对他的政府对待上周恐怖主义戒备状态的方式有批评之辞。He wanted to alert people to the activities of the group.他想警告人们注意这个组织的行动。They want to be on the alert for similar buying opportunities.他们要准备应对类似的购买机会。
amplify  vt. 放大，扩大；增强；详述This landscape seemed to trap and amplify sounds.这种地形好像能聚拢和扩大声音。The music was amplified with microphones.那音乐被麦克风扩大了。...a voice that needed no amplification.…一个不需要扩音的嗓门。The mist had been replaced by a kind of haze that seemed to amplify the heat.这薄雾已经被一种热汽代替了，这似乎加重了炎热的程度。
analogy  n. 类比；类推；类似The analogy between music and fragrance has stuck.音乐与香味的类比已经深入人心了。
appease  vt. 使平息；使满足；使和缓；对…让步Gandhi was accused by some of trying to appease both factions of the electorate.甘地被一些人指责试图对两派选民都加以姑息。
array  n. 数组，阵列；排列，列阵；大批，一系列；衣服As the deadline approached she experienced a bewildering array of emotions.随着最后期限的临近，她心绪变得纷繁复杂起来。We visited the local markets and saw wonderful arrays of fruit and vegetables.我们参观了当地的市场，看到了漂亮地摆放着的水果蔬菜。
arrogant  adj. 自大的，傲慢的He was so arrogant.他是如此傲慢。That sounds arrogant, doesn't it?那听起来很傲慢，不是吗？At times the arrogance of those in power is quite blatant.有时那些当权者的傲慢很露骨。
articulate  vt. 清晰地发（音）；明确有力地表达；用关节连接；使相互连贯She is an articulate young woman.她是个善表达的年轻女子。The president has been accused of failing to articulate an overall vision in foreign affairs.总统被指责没能清楚地表述对外交事务的总体设想。He articulated each syllable.他清楚地说出了每个音节。
ascertain  vt. 确定；查明；探知Through doing this, the teacher will be able to ascertain the extent to which the child understands what he is reading.通过这样做，老师将能确定这个孩子对他正在读的内容的理解程度。Once they had ascertained that he was not a spy, they agreed to release him.一查明他不是间谍，他们就同意了释放他。
assess  vt. 评定；估价；对…征税The test was to assess aptitude rather than academic achievement.该测试将评估能力而不是学业成绩。It would be a matter of assessing whether she was well enough to travel.这将是个评估她是否身体好到可以旅行的问题。Ask them to send you information on how to assess the value of your belongings.叫他们把如何估算你的财产价值的资料寄给你。
asset  n. 资产；优点；有用的东西；有利条件；财产；有价值的人或物Our creativity in the field of technology is our greatest asset.我们在技术领域的创造力是我们最大的资本。By the end of 1989 the group had assets of $3.5 billion.到1989年底该集团已有35亿美元的资产。
assumption  n. 假定；设想；担任；采取You would be making an assumption that's not based on any fact that you could report.你会做出不以你能报道的任何事实为依据的一种假设。
authority  n. 权威；权力；当局This provided a pretext for the authorities to cancel the elections.这给当局提供了一个取消选举的借口。...the Philadelphia Parking Authority.…费城停车管理局。He's universally recognized as an authority on Russian affairs.他被公认为是俄罗斯事务的权威。A family member in a family business has a position of authority and power.家庭成员在家族企业中都有职有权。He had no natural authority and no capacity for imposing his will on others.他天生没有威信，也没有将其意志强加于他人的能力。The prison governor has refused to let him go, saying he must first be given authority from his own superiors.监狱长已拒绝释放他，说他必须首先得到上级的许可。
baffle  vt. 使…困惑；使…受挫折；用挡板控制An apple tree producing square fruit is baffling experts.一棵结方形果实的苹果树正令专家们感到困惑。I was constantly ill, with a baffling array of symptoms.我不断地生病，还伴有一大堆莫名其妙的症状。
barren  adj. 贫瘠的；不生育的；无益的；沉闷无趣的；空洞的...the Tibetan landscape of high barren mountains.…西藏荒芜的高山景观。He wants to use the water to irrigate barren desert land.他想用该水来灌溉贫瘠的沙漠土地。...an empty exercise barren of utility.…一项毫无效用的无聊训练。The room was austere, nearly barren of furniture or decoration.这个房间很简朴，几乎没有什么家具或装饰。
basement  n. 地下室；地窖They bought an old schoolhouse to live in and built a workshop in the basement.他们买了座旧校舍居住，还在地下室建了个作坊。
behave  vi. 表现；（机器等）运转；举止端正；（事物）起某种作用I couldn't believe these people were behaving in this way.我无法相信这些人竟这样行事。You have to behave.你得守规矩。Under certain conditions, electrons can behave like waves rather than particles.在某些条件下，电子能像波而不是粒子那样运动。
bias  n. 偏见；偏爱；斜纹；乖离率...his desire to avoid the appearance of bias in favour of one candidate or another.…他想避免表现出对这个或那个候选人有偏好。We mustn't allow it to bias our teaching.我们不允许它使我们的教学产生偏见。
boast  vt. 夸口说，自吹自擂说；以有…而自豪Witnesses said Furci boasted that he took part in killing them.证人们说富尔西曾吹嘘说他参与了杀人。Carol boasted about her costume.卡罗尔吹嘘着她的戏装。It is the charity's proud boast that it has never yet turned anyone away.该慈善机构自吹自擂，声称从来没有拒绝过任何人。The houses will boast the latest energy-saving technology.这些房屋将采用最新节能技术。
breakdown  n. 故障；崩溃；分解；分类；衰弱；跺脚曳步舞...the breakdown of talks between the U.S. and E.U. officials.…美国与欧盟官员会谈的失败。...the irretrievable breakdown of a marriage.…无法挽回的一场婚姻的破裂。My personal life was terrible. My mother had died, and a couple of years later I had a breakdown.我的个人生活糟透了。母亲去世了,几年后我精神崩溃了。Her old car was unreliable, so the trip was plagued by breakdowns.她的旧车性能不可靠,所以旅途被故障所困扰。The organizers were given a breakdown of the costs.组织者们被给了一份花销细目。
burst  vi. 爆发，突发；爆炸The driver lost control when a tire burst.一只轮胎爆裂时司机失去了控制。It is not a good idea to burst a blister.把水疱弄破不是个好主意。A dam burst and flooded their villages.一个大坝决堤，淹没了他们的村子。Monsoons caused the river to burst its banks.雨季使这条河决堤。The door burst open and an angry young nurse appeared.门突然开了，一个生气的年轻护士出现了。Gunmen burst into his home and opened fire.持枪歹徒闯入他家，开了枪。He burst onto the fashion scene in the early 1980s.20世纪80年代初他突然在时尚界活跃起来。...a burst of machine-gun fire.…一阵机枪射击。
chase  vt. 追逐；追捕；试图赢得；雕镂She chased the thief for 100 yards.她追了小偷100码远。He was reluctant to give up the chase.他不愿意放弃追逐。In some areas, 14 people are chasing every job.在某些地区，14个人角逐每一个岗位。There are too many schools chasing after too few students.有太多的学校争抢太少的学生。They took an invincible lead in the chase for the championship.他们在冠军角逐中遥遥领先。Women also have another reason for not chasing men too hard, of course.当然，妇女还有另一个不紧追男人的理由。The chase is always much more exciting than the conquest anyway.无论如何，追求总比征服更令人兴奋。Many farmers will then chase you off their land quite aggressively.到那时，许多农民便会毫不留情地将你逐出他们的土地。In the '70s he had been chased out of his job.在70年代他被迫离开了他的职位。They chased down the stairs into the narrow, dirty street.他们冲下楼梯，跑到狭窄肮脏的街道上。Hi everyone, we all know why we are here today, so let's cut to the chase.大家好，我们都知道今天为何来此，让我们切入主题吧。
chill  n. 寒冷；寒意；寒心Chill the fruit salad until serving time.上菜前把水果色拉冷却。These doughs can be rolled out while you wait for the pastry to chill.当你等待油酥面团冷却时，可以擀平这些生面团。The marble floor was beginning to chill me.大理石的地板开始让我感到很冷。Wade placed his chilled hands on the radiator and warmed them.韦德把他冰冷的双手放到散热器上取暖。The violence used against the students sent a chill through Indonesia.对学生使用暴力使得整个印度尼西亚不寒而栗。He caught a chill while performing at a rain-soaked open-air venue.他在一个被雨浸湿的露天场地表演时着了风寒。...chill winds, rain and choppy seas.…寒冷的风、雨以及波浪起伏的大海。September is here, bringing with it a chill in the mornings.9月到了，带来了清晨的寒意。
chip  vt. 削，凿；削成碎片...an electronic card containing a chip.…一张带有芯片的电子卡。It contains real chocolate chips.它里面含有纯正的巧克力颗粒。The cup had a small chip.这个杯子有个小缺口。He put the pile of chips in the centre of the table and drew a card.他把那堆筹码放在桌子中间，然后抽了一张牌。The blow chipped the woman's tooth.这一击把那个女人的牙齿打掉了一小块。The wagon's paint was badly chipped on the outside.这辆四轮马车外壳的油漆严重地剥落。
circulation  n. 流通，传播；循环；发行量The Daily News once had the highest circulation of any daily in the country.《每日新闻报》一度在该国所有日报中拥有最高发行量。Anyone with heart, lung, or circulation problems should seek medical advice before flying.任何有心、肺或血液循环问题的人都应该在飞行前寻求医生建议。The supply of money in circulation was drastically reduced overnight.一夜之间流通货币的供应就急剧减少了。...a society like America, with perhaps 180 million guns in circulation.…像美国这样的社会里，可能有1.8亿支枪在流通之中。
competent  adj. 胜任的；有能力的；能干的；足够的He was a loyal, distinguished and very competent civil servant.他是一个忠诚、出色、很有能力的公务员。The government performed competently in the face of multiple challenges.政府在面临多重挑战时表现得很出色。Most adults do not feel competent to deal with a medical emergency involving a child.多数成年人感到难以应付小孩医疗突发事件。
complaint  n. 抱怨；诉苦；疾病；委屈There's been a record number of complaints about the standard of service.已有对服务水准的创纪录数量的投诉。People have been reluctant to make formal complaints to the police.人们一直不愿正式向警方投诉。My main complaint is that we can't go out on the racecourse anymore.我抱怨的主要缘由是我们无法再去外面的赛道了。Eczema is a common skin complaint which often runs in families.湿疹是一种常见的皮肤病，常会遗传。
compose  vt. 构成；写作；使平静；排…的版The force would be composed of troops from NATO countries.该部队将由北约各国的军队组成。Protein molecules compose all the complex working parts of living cells.蛋白质分子构成了活细胞所有复杂的工作部件。Vivaldi composed a large number of very fine concertos.维瓦尔蒂创作了大量非常优美的协奏曲。He started at once to compose a reply to Anna.他立刻开始给安娜写回信。
compulsory  adj. 义务的；必修的；被强制的He believes that the study of history should be compulsory in school.他认为在学校里学习历史应该是强制性的。
concrete  adj. 混凝土的；实在的，具体的；有形的The posts have to be set in concrete.这些柱子必须固定在混凝土中。We sat on the concrete floor.我们坐在混凝土地板上。He merely cleared and concreted the floors.他只是清理了地板并浇上了混凝土。I had no concrete evidence.我当时没有明确而具体的证据。There were no concrete proposals on the table.没有提交讨论的具体提议。...using concrete objects to teach addition and subtraction.…用实物教加减运算。
confident  adj. 自信的；确信的I am confident that everything will come out right in time.我相信最终一切都会好起来的。Mr. Ryan is confident of success.瑞安先生对成功有信心。I can confidently promise that this year is going to be very different.我可以有信心地保证今年将大不一样。In time he became more confident and relaxed.最终他变得更加自信而从容了。She walked confidently across the hall.她自信地走过大厅。She is confident that everybody is on her side.她确信每个人都在她那一边。I can confidently say that none of them were or are racist.我可以确信地说他们当中没有人过去或现在是种族主义者。
conform  vi. 符合；遵照；适应环境The lamp has been designed to conform to new safety standards.该灯设计得符合新的安全标准。Many children who can't or don't conform are bullied.许多不守规矩的孩子受欺负。
confront  vt. 面对；遭遇；比较She was confronted with severe money problems.她面临严重的资金问题。We are learning how to confront death.我们在学习如何正视死亡。I was confronted with an array of knobs, levers, and switches.我面对着一排旋钮、控制杆和开关。She pushed her way through the mob and confronted him face to face.她从那群暴民中挤出来，与他当面对峙。They don't hesitate to open fire when confronted by police.他们一旦遭遇警察就毫不犹豫地开火。She had decided to confront Kathryn with the truth.她已决定用事实与凯瑟琳对质。I could not bring myself to confront him about it.我不能就此事让自己与他对质。
conscious  adj. 意识到的；故意的；神志清醒的He was conscious of the faint, musky aroma of aftershave.他留意到须后水那淡淡的、似麝香的芳香。She was very conscious of Max studying her.她十分清楚马克斯在仔细端详着她。I'm very conscious of my weight.我很在意自己的体重。I don't think we ever made a conscious decision to have a big family.我不认为我们曾刻意下决定要成为一大家子。Sophie was not consciously seeking a replacement after her father died.索菲在父亲去世后没有刻意地找一个代替的人。She was fully conscious throughout the surgery and knew what was going on.她在整个手术过程中神志完全清醒，知道发生了什么。He had no conscious memory of his four-week stay in the hospital.他对自己住院的4个星期记不大清了。Most people cannot consciously remember much before the ages of 3 to 5 years.多数人不能清楚地记得3到5岁之前的多少事情。
consecutive  adj. 连贯的；连续不断的The Cup was won for the third consecutive year by the Toronto Maple Leafs.这个奖杯连续第三年由多伦多枫叶队赢去了。
consistent  adj. 始终如一的，一致的；坚持的Becker was never the most consistent of players anyway.贝克尔不管怎么说从来就不是一个很稳定的球员。It's something I have consistently denied.这是我始终否认的事。This result is consistent with the findings of Garnett & Tobin.该结果与加尼特和托宾的发现相符合。A theory should be internally consistent.一套理论应当内在一致。
console  n. [计] 控制台；[电] 操纵台；支撑架"Never mind, Ned," he consoled me.“不要紧，内德”，他安慰我说。I can console myself with the fact that I'm not alone.我可以用不只我一个人的这种事实来安慰自己。The only consolation for the baseball team is that they look likely to get another chance.对这支棒球队的惟一安慰是他们看来可能会得到另一次机会。Several nurses sat before a console of flickering lights and bleeping monitors.几名护士坐在灯光闪烁、监听器嘟嘟作响的控制台前。
construct  vt. 建造，构造；创立His company recently constructed an office building in downtown Denver.他的公司最近在丹佛市中心建造了一座办公楼。The boxes should be constructed from rough-sawn timber.这些箱子应该用粗锯木材来做。He eventually constructed a huge business empire.他最终构建了一个庞大的商业王国。The novel is constructed from a series of on-the-spot reports.这部小说是由一系列现场报道构思而成的。
contention  n. 争论，争辩；争夺；论点It is my contention that death and murder always lurk as potentials in violent relationships.我的观点是，在暴力关系中总是潜伏着死亡和谋杀的可能。His case has become a source of contention between civil liberties activists and the government.他的案子已变成了公民自由活动家们和政府之间的争论缘由。
contradict  vt. 反驳；否定；与…矛盾；与…抵触She dared not contradict him.她不敢反驳他。His comments appeared to contradict remarks made earlier in the day by the chairman.他的评论好像在反驳主席当天早些时候的言论。Her version contradicted her daughter's.她的说法与她女儿的说法相矛盾。
contrary  adj. 相反的；对立的This view is contrary to the aims of critical social research for a number of reasons.许多原因证明这种观点与批判性社会研究的目的截然相反。Contrary to popular belief, moderate exercise actually decreases your appetite.与大部分人的想法相反，适度的运动实际上会降低食欲。It is not an idea around which the community can unite. On the contrary, I see it as one that will divide us.这不是一个可以让我们的组织团结起来的主意。恰恰相反，我看它会分裂我们。"People just don't do things like that."—"On the contrary, they do them all the time."“人们根本就不像那样做事。” —“然而，他们却一直在那么做。”He continued to maintain that he did nothing wrong, despite clear evidence to the contrary.他仍坚持认为自己没有做错，尽管有确凿的证据证明他做错了。
controversy  n. 争论；论战；辩论The proposed cuts have caused considerable controversy.削减的提议引起了巨大的争议。
convince  vt. 说服；使确信，使信服That weekend in Plattsburgh, he convinced her to go ahead and marry Bud.在普拉茨堡的那个周末，他说服了她嫁给巴德。Although I soon convinced him of my innocence, I think he still has serious doubts about my sanity.尽管我很快就使他相信我是清白的，但是他还是非常怀疑我精神是否正常。
coordinate  n. 坐标；同等的人或物Government officials visited the earthquake zone on Thursday morning to coordinate the relief effort.政府官员星期四上午视察了地震灾区以协调救灾工作。Coalition forces were planning a coordinated effort to attack the drug trade.联合部队正在计划共同打击毒品买卖。...a well-coordinated surprise attack.…一次完美配合的突袭。You need to coordinate legs, arms, and breathing for the front crawl.匍匐前进时，你要协调双腿、胳膊和呼吸。She'll show you how to coordinate pattern and colours.她会向你展示如何搭配款式和颜色。Tie it with fabric bows that coordinate with other furnishings.扎上和其他的饰品相配的布制蝴蝶结。Can you give me your coordinates?能给我你的坐标吗？
counterpart  n. 副本；配对物；极相似的人或物As soon as he heard what was afoot, he telephoned his German and Italian counterparts to protest.他一听到在进行中的事，马上就给德国和意大利相应人员打电话抗议。
county  n. 郡，县He arrived at the Palm Beach County courthouse with his mother.他和母亲来到了棕榈滩县法院大楼。
crash  n. 撞碎；坠毁；破产；轰隆声；睡觉His elder son was killed in a car crash a few years ago.他大儿子几年前死于一次车祸。Two people recalled hearing a loud crash about 1:30 a.m.两人回忆说大约凌晨1：30时听到一声巨响。The plane crashed mysteriously near the island of Ustica.飞机在乌斯蒂卡岛附近神秘地坠毁了。Her car crashed into the rear of a van.她的汽车撞毁了一辆面包车的尾部。The door swung inwards to crash against a chest of drawers behind it.门摆向里面，砰的一声猛力撞上了门后的五斗橱。My words were lost as the walls above us crashed down, filling the cellar with brick dust.随着上面的墙体轰隆一声倒塌下来，地窖里充满砖灰，我吓得说不出话来。When the market crashed, they assumed the deal would be cancelled.市场崩盘时，他们以为那笔交易会取消。He predicted correctly that there was going to be a stock market crash.他正确地预测到将出现股市崩溃。The computer crashed for the second time in 10 days.计算机10天内第2次死机了。
critical  adj. 鉴定的；[核] 临界的；批评的，爱挑剔的；危险的；决定性的；评论的The incident happened at a critical point in the campaign.该事件发生在运动的关键时刻。He says setting priorities is of critical importance.他说确定轻重缓急至关重要。Economic prosperity depends critically on an open world trading system.经济繁荣关键取决于一个开放的世界贸易体系。The German authorities are considering an airlift if the situation becomes critical.德国当局正在考虑如果形势危急时进行空运。Moscow is running critically low on food supplies.莫斯科的食品供应正严重匮乏。Ten of the injured are said to be in critical condition.据说伤者中有十人情况危急。She was critically ill.她病情危急。His report is highly critical of the trial judge.他的报道对承审法官是高度批判的。She spoke critically of Lara.她以批评的口吻谈到拉腊。We need to become critical text-readers.我们需要成为批判性的文本阅读者。Wyman watched them critically.怀曼批判地注视着他们。The film met with considerable critical and public acclaim.这部电影深得评论和公众的赞扬。
crude  adj. 粗糙的；天然的，未加工的；粗鲁的Standard measurements of blood pressure are an important but crude way of assessing the risk of heart disease or strokes.标准的血压测量是评估心脏病或中风风险的一种重要却粗略的方法。The donors can be split – a little crudely – into two groups.捐献者们可以分成–大致地–两个组。...crude wooden boxes.…粗制的木盒子。...a crudely carved wooden form.…一件粗糙的木头雕刻。Must you be quite so crude?你一定要这样粗鲁吗？He hated it when she spoke so crudely.他讨厌她说话那么粗鲁。
deceive  v. 欺骗；行骗He has deceived and disillusioned us all.他欺骗了我们所有人, 令我们所有人失望至极。Do not be deceived by claims on food labels like "light" or "low fat."不要被食品标签上像“少脂”或“低脂”的字样误导。
decisive  adj. 决定性的；果断的，坚定的...his decisive victory in the presidential elections.…他在这次总统选举中的决定性胜利。The plan was decisively rejected by Congress three weeks ago.这个计划三周前被国会关键性地否决了。He should give way to a younger, more decisive leader.他应该让位给一位更年轻、更果断的领导者。"I'll call for you at ten," she said decisively.“我10点来接你，”她果断地说。
deduce  vt. 推论，推断；演绎出Alison cleverly deduced that I was the author of the letter.艾莉森聪明地推断出我是这封信的作者。The date of the document can be deduced from references to the Civil War.该文件的日期可以从其对内战的提及处推算出来。
deem  vt. 认为，视作；相信French and German were deemed essential.法语和德语被认为是必需的。He says he would support the use of force if the UN deemed it necessary.他说如果联合国认为有必要，他就支持动用武力。
demonstrate  vt. 证明；展示；论证The study also demonstrated a direct link between obesity and mortality.这项研究也证明了肥胖和死亡率之间的直接关系。They are anxious to demonstrate to the voters that they have practical policies.他们急于向选民证明他们有切实可行的政策。Have they, for example, demonstrated a commitment to democracy?例如，他们展现了对民主的奉献吗？Some 30,000 angry farmers arrived in Brussels yesterday to demonstrate against possible cuts in subsidies.昨天大约三万名愤怒的农民到布鲁塞尔游行示威，反对可能的补贴削减。In the cities vast crowds have been demonstrating for change.在各城市，已经有大量的群众举行示威游行要求变革。A selection of cosmetic companies will be there to demonstrate their new products.一些化妆品公司会在那里展示他们的新产品。
depress  vt. 压抑；使沮丧；使萧条I must admit the state of the country depresses me.我必须承认国家的形势令我沮丧。The stronger U.S. dollar depressed sales.更坚挺的美元使销售量下降。
deprive  vt. 使丧失，剥夺They've been deprived of the fuel necessary to heat their homes.他们无法得到住房取暖必需的燃料。
descend  vi. 下降；下去；下来；遗传；屈尊Things are cooler and more damp as we descend to the cellar.我们往地窖中下得越深，里面就越冷、越潮湿。Some 3,000 city officials will descend on Capitol Hill on Tuesday to lobby for more money.大约三千名市政官员将于周二突访美国国会山，为争取更多经费游说。He was ultimately overthrown and the country descended into chaos.他最终被推翻，国家陷入了混乱。We're not going to descend to such methods.我们不会堕落到使用这些方式的份上。
deteriorate  vi. 恶化，变坏There are fears that the situation might deteriorate into full-scale war.人们担心局势会恶化为全面战争。...concern about the rapid deterioration in relations between the two countries.…对两国关系迅速恶化的担忧。
disguise  vt. 掩饰；假装；隐瞒You'll have to travel in disguise.你将不得不乔装出行。She disguised herself as a man so she could fight on the battlefield.她女扮男装以便能上战场打仗。The extremists entered the building disguised as medical workers.极端分子们假扮成医务人员，进入了大楼。He made no attempt to disguise his agitation.他无意掩饰他的不安。The proposal is a thinly disguised effort to revive the price controls of the 1970s.这项提议是恢复20世纪70年代物价控制的一种几乎不加掩饰的努力。
disperse  vt. 分散；使散开；传播The oil appeared to be dispersing.油看上去正在扩散。Police fired shots and used tear gas to disperse the demonstrators.警察开枪并使用了催泪瓦斯来驱散示威人群。
displace  vt. 取代；置换；转移；把…免职；排水These factories have displaced tourism as the country's largest source of foreign exchange.这些工厂已经取代了旅游业而成为该国最大的外汇来源。More than 600,000 people were displaced by the tsunami.超过60万人被海啸搞得背井离乡。
disrupt  vt. 破坏；使瓦解；使分裂；使中断；使陷于混乱Anti-war protesters disrupted the debate.反战示威者们扰乱了辩论。
distribute  vt. 分配；散布；分开；把…分类Students shouted slogans and distributed leaflets.学生们高呼口号，散发传单。We didn't understand how difficult it was to distribute a national paper.我们不明白配销一份全国性的报纸有多么困难。Distribute the topping evenly over the fruit.将浇头均匀地浇在水果上。
divert  vt. 转移；使…欢娱；使…转向We diverted a plane to rescue 100 passengers.我们改变飞机航线以拯救100名乘客。Abington Memorial Hospital has been diverting trauma patients to other hospitals because it does not have enough surgeons.由于缺乏足够的外科医生，阿宾顿纪念医院一直在将外伤病人转到其他医院。A wave of deadly bombings has forced the United States to divert funds from reconstruction to security.一系列致命的炸弹袭击迫使美国将资金从重建转向安全防御。He instructed the switchboard staff to divert all Laura's calls to him.他通知接线员把劳拉打来的所有电话都转给他。They want to divert the attention of the people from the real issues.他们想把人民的注意力从真正的问题上转移开。
divorce  vt. 使离婚，使分离；与…离婚Numerous marriages now end in divorce.现在许多婚姻都以离婚而告终。He and Lillian had got divorced.他和莉莲离婚了。I am absolutely furious that he divorced me to marry her.我实在很生气他和我离婚娶了她。...this divorce of Christian culture from the roots of faith.…基督教文化与信仰根源的分离。Good management in the police cannot be divorced from accountability.警政的良好管理离不开问责制。Democracy cannot be divorced from social and economic progress.民主离不开社会和经济的进步。
drain  vi. 排水；流干Miners built the tunnel to drain water out of the mines.矿工们开掘了隧道以将水排出矿井。Now the focus is on draining the water.现在的焦点是排水。The authorities have mobilized vast numbers of people to drain flooded land and build or repair dikes.当局动员了大批民众为遭受洪灾的地区排涝并修建或修复堤坝。Drain the pasta well, arrange on four plates and pour over the sauce.把意大利面条沥干水，摆放在4个盘子里，倒上调味品。Harry felt the colour drain from his face.亨利感到脸上没有了血色。My emotional turmoil had drained me.困惑焦灼的情绪使我心力交瘁。I began to suffer from headaches, which left me feeling completely drained.我开始感到头痛，它使我感到精疲力竭。The state's finances have been drained by drought and civil disorder.国家财政已经被旱灾和内乱消耗殆尽了。Tony built his own house and laid his own drains.托尼盖了自己的房子,铺设了自己的排水管道。...an ultramodern printing plant, which has been a big drain on resources.…一个消耗大量资源的超级现代化印刷厂。They were aware that their public image was rapidly going down the drain.他们意识到自己的公众形象正被迅速地破坏掉。
drift  n. 漂流，漂移；趋势；漂流物We proceeded to drift on up the river.我们继续在河上漂流着。We need to offer young people drifting into crime an alternative set of values.我们需要给误入犯罪歧途的年轻人提供另一套价值观。You've been drifting from job to job without any real commitment.你频频换工作，全无恒心。As rural factories lay off workers, people drift toward the cities.随着乡镇企业裁员，人们陆续移向城市。Cool summer dance sounds are drifting from the stereo indoors.屋内立体声音响飘出美妙的夏季舞曲。The snow, except where it drifted, was only calf-deep.除了被风吹积起来的地方外，积雪只深及小腿。...the drift toward the cities.…向城市的流动。A nine-year-old boy was trapped in a snow drift.一个9岁的男孩陷在雪堆里了。Grace was beginning to get his drift.格雷斯开始抓住他的主旨了。
dubious  adj. 可疑的；暧昧的；无把握的；半信半疑的This claim seems to us to be rather dubious.这项声明在我们看来相当不可信。Carter was dubiously convicted of shooting three white men in a bar.卡特很有嫌疑地被宣叛在一家酒吧射杀了3名白人。My parents were a bit dubious about it all at first but we soon convinced them.起初我父母亲对此尚心存疑虑，但很快我们便说服了他们。He eyed Coyne dubiously.他怀疑地注视着科因。
economical  adj. 经济的；节约的；合算的...plans to trade in their car for something smaller and more economical.…用他们的车抵价购买更小且更经济型轿车的计划。Services could be operated more efficiently and economically.可以更有效、更经济地提供服务。...ideas for economical housekeeping.…节俭持家的一些想法。His gestures were economical, his words generally mild.他的手势简练，言语通常是温和的。
eject  vt. 喷射；驱逐，逐出Officials used guard dogs to eject the protesters.官员们用护卫犬驱走抗议者。...the ejection and manhandling of hecklers at the meeting.…对会上起哄者的驱逐和推搡。He aimed his rifle, fired a single shot, then ejected the spent cartridge.他用步枪瞄准，开了一枪，接着排出了空弹壳。The pilot ejected from the plane and escaped injury.飞行员从飞机里弹出，没有受伤。
elaborate  adj. 精心制作的；详尽的；煞费苦心的...an elaborate research project.…一项复杂的研究项目。...elaborate efforts at the highest level to conceal the problem.…最高层企图掩饰这个问题的百般努力。It was clearly an elaborately planned operation.这显然是一次经过周密策划的行动。He is known for his elaborate costumes.他以其繁丽的服装著称。His task was to elaborate policies that would make a market economy compatible with a clean environment.他的任务是周密地制定能够让市场经济适合于无污染的环境的政策。...the elaboration of specific policies and mechanisms.…对具体政策和机制的周密制定。A spokesman declined to elaborate on a statement released late yesterday.发言人拒绝对昨天晚些时候发表的一份声明作出更多说明。
elastic  adj. 有弹性的；灵活的；易伸缩的Make a mask with long ears and attach a piece of elastic to go around the back of the head.做一个带长耳朵的面具，安上一条松紧带绕过后脑。Beat it until the dough is slightly elastic.反复捶打，直到面团略有弹性。
elbow  n. 肘部；弯头；扶手He slipped and fell, badly bruising an elbow.他滑倒了，严重挫伤了一只胳膊肘。They also claim that the security team elbowed aside a steward.他们还声称治安队把一名乘务员推到了一边。Non-state firms gradually elbow aside the inefficient state-owned ones.非国有企业逐渐排挤掉了那些低效率的国有企业。
elevate  vt. 提升；举起；振奋情绪等；提升…的职位He was elevated to the post of president.他被提拔到总裁的职位。The elevation of the assistant coach to the head coaching position within only 9 months was a surprise.这位助理教练仅仅在9个月内就被提拔到总教练的位置是件令人惊讶的事。Don't elevate your superiors to superstar status.不要把你的上级抬高到超级明星的地位。Emotional stress can elevate blood pressure.情绪紧张会使血压升高。A few times a day, elevate feet above heart level.一天几次把脚抬到高过心脏的位置。I built a platform to elevate the bed.我搭了一个台子把床抬高了。
elicit  vt. 抽出，引出；引起Mr. Norris said he was hopeful that his request would elicit a positive response.诺里斯先生说他希望他的要求会引起积极的回应。My letters to her have elicited no response.我写给她的信没有得到回应。
eligible  adj. 合格的，合适的；符合条件的；有资格当选的Almost half the population are eligible to vote in today's election.将近一半的居民有资格在今天的选举中投票。The rules covering eligibility for benefits changed in the 1980s.关于社会救济金合格条件的规定在20世纪80年代发生了变化。He's the most eligible bachelor in Japan.他是日本最令人中意的单身汉。
enclose  vt. 围绕；装入；放入封套The rules state that samples must be enclosed in two watertight containers.条例规定样品必须用两个不漏水的容器封装起来。Enclose the flower in a small muslin bag.把这花用一个小棉袋包起来。I have enclosed a cheque for £100.我信里附上了一张$100的支票。
endow  vt. 赋予；捐赠；天生具有You are endowed with wealth, good health and a lively intellect.你天生赋有财富、健康，和敏锐的智力。Herbs have been used for centuries to endow a whole range of foods with subtle flavours.香草几个世纪以来一直被用来赋予各种食品细腻的味道。The ambassador has endowed a $1 million public-service fellowships programme.大使资助了一个100万美元的公共服务奖学金项目。
endure  vt. 忍耐；容忍The company endured heavy financial losses.公司承受了沉重的财务损失。Somehow the language endures and continues to survive.由于某种原因，这种语言持续生存下来了。This chance meeting was the start of an enduring friendship.这次偶然的相遇是一段持久友情的开始。
enforce  vt. 实施，执行；强迫，强制Boulder was one of the first cities in the nation to enforce a ban on smoking.博尔德是该国率先施行禁烟令的城市之一。They struggled to limit the cost by enforcing a low-tech specification.他们通过强制执行一种低技术规范来竭力限制成本。
enormous  adj. 庞大的，巨大的；凶暴的，极恶的The main bedroom is enormous.主卧室大极了。It was an enormous disappointment.这是件令人极为失望的事。This book was enormously influential.这本书影响极大。
ensue  vi. 跟着发生，接着发生；继起If the Europeans did not reduce subsidies, a trade war would ensue.如果欧洲不减少补贴，贸易战将随即爆发。
enterprise  n. 企业；事业；进取心；事业心There are plenty of small industrial enterprises.有很多小型的工业企业。Horse breeding is indeed a risky enterprise.养马的确是一项有风险的事业。He is still involved in voluntary work promoting local enterprise.他仍从事志愿工作推动当地创业。...the spirit of enterprise worthy of a free and industrious people.…与一个自由勤劳的民族相称的开拓精神。
equip  vt. 装备，配备They try to equip their vehicles with gadgets to deal with every possible contingency.他们尽量给他们的车辆配备各种小装置以应付任何可能的突发状况。Owners of restaurants have to equip them to admit disabled people.餐馆老板们必须给餐馆配备接纳残疾人的设施。Relative poverty, however, did not prevent Martin from equipping himself with an excellent education.然而相对的贫穷并没有妨碍马丁接受良好教育。
erase  vt. 抹去；擦除They are desperate to erase the memory of that last defeat.他们急于抹去上次失败的记忆。An intruder broke into the campaign headquarters and managed to erase 17,000 names from computer files.一名入侵者闯入作战指挥部，设法删除了电脑文件中的17000个名字。
exception  n. 例外；异议Few guitarists can sing as well as they can play; Eddie, however, is an exception.很少有吉他手唱歌能唱得跟弹得一样好，而艾迪是个例外。The law makes no exceptions.法律不搞例外。Marketing is applied to everything these days, and books are no exception.现在市场营销用于任何事物，图书也不例外。He also took exception to having been spied on.他也厌恶被暗中监视。Yesterday was a day off for everybody, with the exception of Lorenzo.昨天每个人休一天假，洛伦佐除外。The vehicles are without exception old, rusty and dented.这些车辆无一例外地破旧、锈迹斑斑且有撞痕。
exert  vt. 运用，发挥；施以影响He exerted considerable influence on the thinking of the scientific community on these issues.他对科学界在这些问题上的思考施加了相当大的影响。Do not exert yourself unnecessarily.不要无谓地耗费自己的精力。He clearly found the physical exertion exhilarating.他明显发现体力消耗令人愉悦。
exquisite  adj. 精致的；细腻的；优美的，高雅的；异常的；剧烈的The Indians brought in exquisite beadwork to sell.印地安人带了精美的珠饰来销售。...exquisitely crafted dollshouses.…制作精美的玩具小屋。
extract  vt. 提取；取出；摘录；榨取...the traditional method of pick and shovel to extract coal.…用锄和铲采煤的传统方法。Citric acid can be extracted from the juice of oranges, lemons, limes or grapefruit.柠檬酸可以从橙汁、柠檬汁、酸橙汁或柚子汁中提取。Petroleum engineers plan and manage the extraction of oil.石油工程师们规划并管理石油的提炼。He extracted a small notebook from his hip pocket.他从臀后口袋拿出了一本小笔记簿。A dentist may decide to extract the tooth to prevent recurrent trouble.牙医可能会决定拔掉这颗牙，以防复发。In those days, dentistry was basic. Extractions were carried out without anaesthetic.那时牙科学刚起步，拔牙是在没有麻药的情况下进行的。He sought to extract the maximum political advantage from the cut in interest rates.他力图从利息削减中谋取最大的政治利益。He made the mistake of trying to extract further information from our director.他犯了想从我们主任那里探取进一步信息的错误。I've simply extracted a few figures.我只是摘取了一些数据。Britain's trade figures can no longer be extracted from export-and-import documentation at ports.英国的贸易数字再也不能从各港口的进出口文件中摘取了。This material has been extracted from "Collins Good Wood Handbook."该资料摘自《柯林斯良木手册》。Read this extract from an information booklet about the work of an airline cabin crew.阅读这个航空公司机务员工作信息手册的选段。Blend in the vanilla extract, lemon peel, and walnuts.调和香草精、柠檬皮和核桃。
faculty  n. 科，系；能力；全体教员He was drunk and not in control of his faculties.他喝醉了，控制不了他的各项机能。The faculty agreed on a change in the requirements.全体教员同意改变要求。How can faculty improve their teaching so as to encourage creativity?全体教员怎样才能改进教学以便激发创造力？
faithful  adj. 忠实的，忠诚的；如实的；准确可靠的She had been faithful to her promise to guard this secret.她一直信守诺言保守着这个秘密。He spends his time making speeches at factories or gatherings of the Party faithful.他花时间在工厂或者在该党忠实拥护者的集会上发表演讲。He has since 1965 faithfully followed and supported every twist and turn of government policy.他从1965年起忠实地追随并支持政府政策的每一次重大转变。I'm very faithful when I love someone.当我爱一个人时我是非常忠贞的。Colin Welland's screenplay is faithful to the novel.科林·韦兰的电影剧本是忠实于小说原文的。When I adapt something I translate from one meaning to another as faithfully as I can.我在改编的时候，我用尽量忠实于原文的方式把一种含义翻译为另一种。
fatal  adj. 致命的；重大的；毁灭性的；命中注定的It would be fatal for the nation to overlook the urgency of the situation.国家若忽视这一局势的紧迫性，后果将会非常严重。He made the fatal mistake of compromising early.他犯了妥协早了的致命错误。Failure now could fatally damage his chances in the future.现在的失败能严重地毁掉他将来的机会。...the fatal stabbing of a police sergeant.…对一名警官的致命一刺。The dead soldier is reported to have been fatally wounded in the chest.报道说死去的那名士兵胸部受到了致命伤。
favo  None
format  n. 格式；版式；开本I had met with him to explain the format of the programme and what we had in mind.我已经同他见过面，解释了这个节目的程式和我们的想法。His latest album is available on all formats.他的最新专辑有各种格式可以买到。...a menu that includes the choice to format a disk.…一个包括格式化磁盘选项的菜单。When text is saved from a Web page, it is often very badly formatted with many short lines.文本从网页上另存时版式通常会变乱，出现很多短行。
foundation  n. 基础；地基；基金会；根据；创立Best friends are the foundation of my life.良友们是我生活的基础。The issue strikes at the very foundation of our community.这个问题严重影响到我们社会的基础。...the National Foundation for Educational Research.…全国教育研究基金会。The allegations were without foundation.这些指控没有根据。Use foundation and/or face powder afterwards for an even skin tone.随后使用粉底霜和（或）粉饼以使皮肤色调均匀。
generate  vt. 使形成；发生；生殖；产生物理反应The labour secretary said the reforms would generate new jobs.劳动部长说这些改革将带来新的工作。The company, New England Electric, burns coal to generate power.新英格兰电力公司燃烧煤来发电。
grip  n. 紧握；柄；支配；握拍方式；拍柄绷带She gripped the rope.她紧紧抓住绳子。His strong hand eased the bag from her grip.他强有力的手使她把紧握的包松开。The president maintains an iron grip on his country.总统保持着对国家的铁腕统治。The entire community has been gripped by fear.整个社区已被恐惧笼罩着。The nation is gripped by the dramatic story.整个国家都被这个戏剧性的故事所吸引。The film turned out to be a gripping thriller.这部电影原来是一部扣人心弦的惊险片。...a new way of reinforcing rubber which gives car tyres a better grip.…一种增强橡胶使汽车轮胎抓力加强的新方法。The administration's first task is to come to grips with the economy.该政府首要的任务是认真着手处理经济问题。Part of me was very frightened and I consciously had to get a grip on myself.我其实非常害怕，但又不得不有意识地控制住自己。He wondered if perhaps he was getting old and losing his grip.他怀疑自己或许在变老，对事情感到力不从心。Shakur loses his fragile grip on reality and starts blasting away at friends and foes alike.沙库尔丧失了对现实脆弱的控制力，无论对朋友还是敌人都开始猛烈抨击起来。
guarantee  n. 保证；担保；保证人；保证书；抵押品Surplus resources alone do not guarantee growth.仅有富足的资源并不能确保发展。A famous old name on a firm is not necessarily a guarantee of quality.公司的老字号并不一定能保证质量。Most states guarantee the right to free and adequate education.大多数州都保证免费和适当教育的权利。We guarantee that you will find a community with which to socialize.我们保证你将找到一个可以社交的团体。The editors can give no guarantee that they will fulfil their obligations.这些编辑不能保证他们将履行职责。Whatever a guarantee says, when something goes wrong, you can still claim your rights from the shop.不管保修单上怎么说，当产品出现故障时，你仍然可以去商店维护自身的权益。Some builders guarantee their work.一些建筑商为他们的工作担保。All Dreamland's electric blankets are guaranteed for three years.所有“梦乡”牌的电热毯都保质3年。Males between 18 and 20 had to leave a deposit as a guarantee of returning to do their military service.18岁至20岁的男性必须留下押金作为回来服兵役的担保。
guard  n. 守卫；警戒；护卫队；防护装置Gunmen guarded homes near the cemetery with shotguns.枪手携带猎枪守卫着公墓附近的住宅。Marines with rifles guarded them.持步枪的海军陆战队士兵看守他们。The prisoners overpowered their guards and locked them in a cell.囚犯们制服了卫兵，并把他们锁在一个牢房里。We have a security guard around the whole area.我们在整个地区周围配有保安人员。He closely guarded her identity.他严密地保守她的身份。...the chin guard of my helmet.…我头盔上的下巴防护罩。Charm the audience and catch them off guard.让观众陶醉，然后出其不意使他们大吃一惊。The ANC could not afford to lower its guard until everything had been carried out.在所有任务完成之前，非洲人国民大会丝毫不敢放松警惕。You can't let your guard down.你不能掉以轻心。The police have questioned him thoroughly, and he'll be on his guard.警察已仔细盘问了他，因此他会保持警惕。Police were on guard at Barnet town hall.警察在巴尼特市政厅值守。One young policeman stood guard outside the locked embassy gates.一名年轻的警察在大门紧闭的使馆外站岗。Three men were arrested and one was under guard in a hospital.有三人被捕，一人在医院里受到监视。
hamper  vt. 妨碍；束缚；使困累The bad weather hampered rescue operations.恶劣的天气阻碍了救助行动。...a luxury food hamper.…一个豪华的食物礼品篮。...a picnic hamper.…一个野炊篮子。He tossed his damp towel into the laundry hamper.他把湿毛巾抛入洗衣篮里。
harsh  adj. 严厉的；严酷的；刺耳的；粗糙的；刺目的...the harsh desert environment.…严酷的沙漠环境。...the harshness of their living conditions.…他们生活条件之艰苦。He said many harsh and unkind things about his opponents.他说了许多关于他对手的严厉且残酷的话。She's been told that her husband is being harshly treated in prison.她被告知她丈夫正在监狱里遭受严酷的对待。Tropical colours may look rather harsh in our dull northern light.热带丛林的色彩在我们暗淡的北极光下也许会显得很刺眼。As the wine ages, it loses its bitter harshness.随着葡萄酒变陈，酒中的苦涩味就会消失。It's a pity she has such a loud harsh voice.可惜她有这么一种响亮刺耳的声音。Chris laughed harshly.克里斯大笑，声音刺耳。The harsh truth is that luck plays a big part in who will live or die.残酷的现实是，运气在很大程度上决定着谁生谁死。
heighten  vt. 提高；增高；加强；使更显著The move has heightened tension in the state.这一举动加剧了该州的紧张局势。Cross's interest heightened.克罗斯的兴趣增强了。
heritage  n. 遗产；传统；继承物；继承权The historic building is as much part of our heritage as the paintings.这座历史建筑和这些绘画作品一样也是留给我们的遗产的组成部分。
hop  v. 单足跳跃〔跳行〕I hopped down three steps.我单脚跳下3级台阶。"This really is a catching rhythm, huh?" he added, with a few little hops.“这节奏可真有感染力，是吧？”他补充说道，单脚小步跳了几下。A small brown fawn hopped across the trail in front of them.一只小棕鹿在他们面前蹦跳着穿过了小路。The rabbit got up, took four hops and turned around.兔子直起身子，蹦跳了4下，然后转过身。My wife and I were the first to arrive and hopped on board.我和妻子是最先到达并跳上车的。It is a three-hour drive but can be reached by a 20-minute hop in a private helicopter.这段路程开车需要3个小时，而乘坐私人直升飞机20分钟就可以到达。
humanity  n. 人类；人道；仁慈；人文学科They face charges of committing crimes against humanity.他们面临犯有反人类罪的指控。He was under discussion and it made him feel deprived of his humanity.他受到议论，这使他觉得自己被剥夺了人格。Her speech showed great maturity and humanity.她的演讲表现出高度的成熟和博爱。The number of students majoring in the humanities has declined by about half.主修人文学科的学生数量已经下降了近一半。
ignite  vt. 点燃；使燃烧；使激动The bombs ignited a fire which destroyed some 60 houses.炸弹引起了一场火灾，烧毁了大约六十间房屋。There was one teacher who really ignited my interest in words.曾经有一位老师真正激起了我对文字的兴趣。
illustrate  vt. 阐明，举例说明；图解The example of the United States illustrates this point.美国的例子表明了这一点。The situation illustrates how vulnerable the president is.这个情况显示总统是多么地不堪一击。Let me give another example to illustrate this difficult point.让我举另一个例子来阐明这个难点。Here, by way of illustration, are some extracts from our new catalogue.这里引为例证的是摘自我们新目录的部分内容。She went on to art school and is now illustrating a book.她接着上了美术学校，现在正在给一本书画插图。...the world of children's book illustration.…儿童书籍插图的世界。
impart  vt. 给予（尤指抽象事物），传授；告知，透露The ability to impart knowledge and command respect is the essential qualification for teachers.传授知识并博得尊敬的能力对老师们来说是基本的条件。She managed to impart great elegance to the unpretentious dress she was wearing.她努力为自己朴素的衣着增添几分优雅。
incentive  n. 动机；刺激There is little or no incentive to adopt such measures.几乎或根本没有鼓励来采取这样的措施。
incidentally  adv. 顺便；偶然地；附带地"I didn't ask you to come. Incidentally, why have you come?"“我没有叫你来。顺便问一下，你为什么来呢？”The letter mentioned my great aunt and uncle only incidentally.信里只是附带地提到我的叔祖母和叔祖父。
indispensable  adj. 不可缺少的；绝对必要的；责无旁贷的She was becoming indispensable to him.对他来说她正变得不可或缺。
industrial  adj. 工业的，产业的；从事工业的；供工业用的；来自勤劳的...industrial machinery and equipment.…工业机械及设备。...leading western industrial countries.…主要的西方工业发达国家。
industrialize  vt. 使工业化Energy consumption rises as countries industrialize.能源消耗随着各国工业化而增加。Industrialization began early in Spain.工业化很早就在西班牙开始了。
inflict  vt. 造成；使遭受（损伤、痛苦等）；给予（打击等）...the damage being inflicted on industries by the recession.…经济衰退给工业造成的损失。
ingenious  adj. 有独创性的；机灵的，精制的；心灵手巧的...a truly ingenious invention.…一项的确新颖的发明。
innocent  adj. 无辜的；无罪的；无知的He was sure that the man was innocent of any crime.他确信此人是清白无罪的。They seemed so young and innocent.他们看上去如此少不更事。She had always regarded Greg as a hopeless innocent where women were concerned.她过去一直认为格雷格在关于女人方面是一个不可救药的无知者。The baby gurgled innocently on the bed.那个婴儿在床上天真地咯咯笑。All those wounded were innocent victims.所有受伤的人都是无辜的受害者。It was probably an innocent question, but Michael got flustered anyway.那也许是个没有恶意的问题，但迈克尔还是变得紧张不安。
innovation  n. 创新，革新；新方法They produced the first vegetarian beanburger – an innovation which was rapidly exported.他们制造出第一个素式豆堡包–一种被迅速销往国外的新食品。We must promote originality, inspire creativity and encourage innovation.我们必须提倡独创性，激发创造力，鼓励创新。
inspire  vt. 激发；鼓舞；启示；产生；使生灵感Our challenge is to motivate those voters and inspire them to join our cause.我们的艰巨任务是要激励那些投票者并鼓励他们加入我们的事业。In the 1960s, the electric guitar virtuosity of Jimi Hendrix inspired a generation.20世纪60年代，吉米·亨德里克斯演奏电吉他的精湛技巧激发了一代人的热情。The book was inspired by a real person, namely Tamara de Treaux.这本书是受一个叫塔玛拉·德特罗的人启发而写成的。...Mediterranean-inspired ceramics in bright yellow and blue.…源自地中海风格灵感的明黄色和蓝色瓷器。The car's performance is effortless and its handling is precise and quickly inspires confidence.这辆车开起来毫不费劲且精确到位，能很快激起驾驶员的信心。
instantaneous  adj. 瞬间的；即时的；猝发的Death was not instantaneous because none of the bullets hit the heart.因为没有一颗子弹射中心脏，所以没有即刻死亡。Airbags inflate instantaneously on impact to form a cushion between the driver and the steering column.安全气囊在碰撞时立刻膨胀，在司机和方向盘之间形成一个缓冲。
institution  n. 制度；建立；（社会或宗教等）公共机构；习俗...financial institutions.…金融机构。Larry has been in an institution since he was four.拉里从4岁起就在孤儿院生活。I believe in the institution of marriage.我相信婚姻制度。There was never an official institution of censorship in Albania.阿尔巴尼亚从来就没有正式建立过审查制度。
insulate  vt. 隔离，使孤立；使绝缘，使隔热People should insulate their homes to conserve energy.人们应该使住房隔冷以保存能量。Is there any way we can insulate our home from the noise?有什么办法能使我们家隔音吗？In order to make it safe, the element is electrically insulated.为安全起见，该元件做了绝缘处理。They wonder if their community is no longer insulated from big city problems.他们想知道他们的社区是否不再与那些大城市的问题隔离。They lived in happy insulation from brutal facts.他们生活在幸福中，与残酷事实相隔绝。
integral  adj. 积分的；完整的，整体的；构成整体所必须的Rituals, celebrations, and festivals form an integral part of every human society.仪式、庆典和节日是每个人类社会不可缺少的组成部分。
integrate  vt. 使…完整；使…成整体；求…的积分；表示…的总和He didn't integrate successfully into the Italian way of life.他没有成功融入到意大利的生活方式中去。Integrating the kids with the community is essential.使孩子们融入这个社区是非常必要的。He thinks we are living in a fully integrated, supportive society.他认为我们生活在一个完全融合、互相帮助的社会。The Marine Corps was the last service to integrate.美国海军陆战队是最后合并的部队。...a black honour student in Chicago's integrated Lincoln Park High School.…在芝加哥混合种族的林肯公园高中上学的一位黑人优等学生。Writing about a topic helps you integrate new knowledge with what you already know.围绕某一题目写作有助于你将新知识和已有知识结合起来。...historic landmarks that integrate with the community.…与社区融为一体的历史性里程碑。There is, he said, a lack of an integrated national transportation policy.他说目前缺乏一个整体的全国运输政策。
intelligible  adj. 可理解的；明了的；仅能用智力了解的The language of Darwin was intelligible to experts and non-experts alike.达尔文的语言对专家和平常人来说都容易理解。
interval  n. 间隔；间距；幕间休息The process is repeated after a short interval of time.该程序间隔很短时间就重复一次。...during the interval of the musical "Steppin' Out."…在音乐剧《影舞追梦》的幕间休息期间。Fraser did not perform until after the interval.弗雷泽直到中场休息之后才出场。She woke him for his medicines at intervals throughout the night.整个晚上她不时叫醒他，让他吃药。Several red and white barriers marked the road at intervals of about a mile.每隔1英里左右就有一些红白相间的路障来标示道路。
interview  n. 接见，采访；面试，面谈The interview went well.面试很顺利。When Wardell was interviewed, he was impressive, and on that basis, he was hired.当沃德尔接受面试时，他给人印象深刻，因此他被雇用了。The trouble began when Allan gave an interview to the Chicago Tribune last month.麻烦开始于艾伦上个月接受《芝加哥论坛报》的采访。I'd interviewed him often in the past.我过去经常采访他。The police interviewed the driver, but had no evidence to go on.警察询问了司机，但没有得到继续调查的证据。
invest  vt. 投资；覆盖；耗费；授予；包围Many people don't like to invest in stocks.许多人不喜欢投资股票。I'm tired of watching you invest our money in insane projects.我看够了你将我们的钱投到一些荒唐的项目上。The company has invested a six-figure sum in an electronic order-control system which is used to keep stores stocked.这家公司已经耗资6位数购买了电子定单控制系统来为商店进货。...the need to invest in new technology.…这种投资于新技术的需要。Government agencies must invest more funds in training and development programmes.政府机构必须将更多的资金投入到培训和开发项目中。I would rather invest time in Rebecca than in the kitchen.我宁愿把时间花在丽贝卡身上，也不愿花在厨房里。The constitution invested him with certain powers.宪法赋予了他一些权力。
investigate  v. 调查；研究They're still investigating the accident.他们还在调查这个事故。He ordered an investigation into the affair.他下令对此事进行调查。
isolate  vt. 使隔离；使孤立；使绝缘This policy could isolate the country from the other permanent members of the United Nations Security Council.这项政策可能会将这个国家从联合国安理会的其他常任理事国中孤立出来。They are finding themselves increasingly isolated within the teaching profession.他们发现自己在教育界中越来越孤立。She seemed determined to isolate herself from everyone, even him.她似乎决心要与每个人，甚至是他割断联系。His radicalism and refusal to compromise isolated him.他的激进和拒绝让步使他受到了孤立。Our anxieties can also be controlled by isolating thoughts, feelings and memories.我们的焦虑也可以通过对思想、感情和记忆分别进行考虑来加以控制。We can use genetic engineering techniques to isolate the gene that is responsible.我们可以用遗传工程技术将起作用的基因离析出来。Patients will be isolated from other people for between three days and one month after treatment.治疗之后，患者将被与他人隔离3天到1个月。Hayley contracted tuberculosis and had to be put in an isolation ward.海利感染了肺结核而不得不被送进一个隔离病房。
jeopardize  vt. 危害；使陷危地；使受危困He has jeopardized his future career.他损害了他的前程。
label  vt. 标注；贴标签于He peered at the label on the bottle.他注视着瓶子上的标签。It requires foreign frozen-food imports to be clearly labelled.它要求外国进口冷冻食品要粘贴明确的标签。The produce was labelled "Made in China."该产品上贴有“中国制造”的标签。It won't be labelled in any way as a military expedition.它无论如何也称不上是一次军事远征。It does not matter whether these duties are labelled "duties" or "tasks".这些义务被称作“义务”还是“任务”都无关紧要。
lawsuit  n. 诉讼（尤指非刑事案件）；诉讼案件The dispute culminated last week in a lawsuit against the government.这场针对政府诉讼案的争论在上星期达到了高潮。
leap  vi. 跳，跳跃He leaped in the air and waved his fists to the fans as he ran out of the stadium.他跑出体育馆，跳起来向他的崇拜者们挥舞着拳头。Frederick leaped 22 feet, 7¼ inches on his second attempt.弗雷德里克第2次试跳跳了22英尺7.25英寸。The suspect took a leap out of a third-storey window.那个犯罪嫌疑人从三楼的窗口跳了出去。The two men leaped into the jeep and roared off.那两个人飞快地跳上吉普车呼啸而去。The car leaped forward.汽车突然向前冲去。The result has been a giant leap in productivity.其结果就是生产力的大幅度提高。...the leap in the unemployed from 35,000 to 75,000.…失业人数从3.5万人猛增到7.5万人。Bush's approval rating leaped to an astounding 88 percent.布什的支持率令人吃惊地剧增到了88%。
lease  n. 租约；租期；租赁物；租赁权He took up a 10-year lease on the house.他为这房子签了10年的租约。He went to Toronto, where he leased an apartment.他去了多伦多，在那里租了一套公寓。She hopes to lease the building to students.她希望把大楼租给学生。
legal  adj. 法律的；合法的；法定的；依照法律的He vowed to take legal action.他发誓要诉诸法律行动。...the legal system.…法律制度。It could be a bit problematic, legally speaking.从法律上说，可能是有点问题。What I did was perfectly legal.我做的事情完全合法。
lest  conj. 唯恐，以免；担心I was afraid to open the door lest he should follow me.我当时害怕打开那个门惟恐他跟踪我。And, lest we forget, Einstein wrote his most influential papers while working as a clerk.而且，为了不使我们忘记，爱因斯坦在做小职员的时候写了他最有影响的论文。
liable  adj. 有责任的，有义务的；应受罚的；有…倾向的；易…的Only a small minority of the mentally ill are liable to harm themselves or others.只有极少数的精神病人很有可能伤害到自己或他人。She will grow into a woman particularly liable to depression.她将变成一个特别易于消沉的女人。The airline's insurer is liable for damages to the victims' families.航空公司投保的保险公司为遇难者家庭的损失负法律责任。The company does not accept liability for fragile, valuable or perishable articles.公司对于易碎、贵重或易腐烂的物品不负责任。
linger  vi. 徘徊；苟延残喘；磨蹭The scent of her perfume lingered on in the room.她的香水味在房间里久久不散。He was ashamed. That feeling lingered, and he was never comfortable in church after that.他很惭愧。这种感觉持续着，此后他在教堂里就再没有自在过。Customers are welcome to linger over coffee until around midnight.顾客们可以慢慢品味咖啡到午夜。
loan  n. 贷款；借款The country has no access to foreign loans or financial aid.该国得不到外国贷款或财政援助。The president wants to make it easier for small businesses to get bank loans.总统想使小公司能更容易地获得银行贷款。I am in need of a loan of a bike for a few weeks.我需要借辆自行车来用几周。He had kindly offered to loan us all the plants required for the exhibit.他友好地主动提出了借给我们展览会所需的全部植物。It is common practice for clubs to loan out players to sides in the lower divisions.将球员借给下级球队是俱乐部的惯例。...impressionist paintings on loan from the National Gallery.…从国家美术馆借来的印象派画作。
magnify  vt. 放大；赞美；夸大This version of the Digges telescope magnifies images 11 times.这种型号的迪格斯望远镜能将图像放大11倍。A lens would magnify the picture so it would be like looking at a large TV screen.透镜会把图像放大，这样就会像看大电视屏幕。Poverty and human folly magnify natural disasters.贫穷和人类的愚蠢加剧自然灾难。They do not grasp the broad situation and spend their time magnifying ridiculous details.他们没有把握大局而把时间花费在夸大荒谬的细节上。
majority  n. 多数；成年The majority of my patients come to me from out of town.我的多数病人来自市区外。Surveys indicate that supporters of the treaty are still in the majority.调查显示该条约的支持者仍占多数。Members of parliament approved the move by a majority of ninety-nine.国会议员们以99票的多数批准了该提案。...her continuing disagreement with the majority view.…她与多数人观点的持续不一致。...a citizen of Russia who has reached the age of majority.…一个已成年的俄罗斯公民。
mature  adj. 成熟的；充分考虑的；到期的；成年人的You will learn what to expect as your child matures physically.当你的孩子身体发育成熟时，你将知道会发生什么。When the trees matured they were cut.当这些树长成时，它们就会被砍掉。They have matured way beyond their age.他们已经成熟得远远超过了他们的年龄。They are emotionally mature and should behave responsibly.他们在情感上是成熟的，应该负责任地行事。Unlike wine, brandy matures only in wood, not glass.和葡萄酒不同，白兰地只能在木质容器里酿成，玻璃容器不行。Grate some mature cheddar cheese.磨碎一些酿熟的切达干酪。These bonuses will be paid when your savings plan matures in ten years' time.当你的储蓄计划在10年后到期时，这些红利将会被支付。...a man of mature years who had been in the job for longer than most of the members could remember.…一个成年男子，从事这项工作的时间已经长得大部分成员都记不清了。
maximum  n. [数] 极大，最大限度；最大量Under planning law the maximum height for a fence or hedge is 6 feet.根据规划法，栅栏或树篱的最高高度为6英尺。The law provides for a maximum of two years in prison.法律规定监禁最长两年。I need the maximum amount of information you can give me.我需要你所能给我的最大的信息量。It was achieved with minimum fuss and maximum efficiency.它以最少的慌乱和最高的效率被做到了。We need an extra 6 grams a day maximum.我们一天最多还需要6克。
minor  adj. 未成年的；次要的；较小的；小调的；二流的She is known in Italy for a number of minor roles in films.她因担任电影中一些配角而闻名意大利。Sarah had been plagued continually by a series of minor illnesses since her mid teens.自从十四五岁起萨拉就一直小病不断。The approach has virtually ended cigarette sales to minors.这一作法实际上已经终止了向未成年人出售香烟。...the unfinished sonata movement in F minor.…未完成的F小调奏鸣曲乐章。
misfortune  n. 不幸；灾祸，灾难She seemed to enjoy the misfortunes of others.她似乎很喜欢幸灾乐祸。
mislead  vt. 误导；带错It's this legend which has misled scholars.正是这个传奇故事误导了学者们。
momentum  n. 势头；[物] 动量；动力；冲力This campaign is really gaining momentum.这场运动确实势头正猛。
multiply  vt. 乘；使增加；使繁殖；使相乘Such disputes multiplied in the eighteenth and nineteenth centuries.此类争论在18世纪和19世纪大大增加。These creatures can multiply quickly.这些生物能迅速大量繁殖。What do you get if you multiply six by nine?6乘以9得多少？
muscle  n. 肌肉；力量Keeping your muscles strong and in tone helps you to avoid back problems.保持强壮有力的肌肉有助于防范背疾。Eisenhower used his muscle to persuade Congress to change the law.艾森豪威尔施展了他的影响力来说服国会修改该法律。The Fair Trade Commission has of late been flexing its muscles, cracking down on cases of corruption.公平交易委员会最近一展雄威，对腐败案件进行了严惩。He stood without moving a muscle, unable to believe what his eyes saw so plainly.他一动也不动地站着，不敢相信自己的眼睛。
negotiate  vt. 谈判，商议；转让；越过It is not clear whether the president is willing to negotiate with the Democrats.尚不清楚总统是否愿意与民主党人进行谈判。When you have two adversaries negotiating, you need to be on neutral territory.在你让敌对双方谈判时，你应该采取中间立场。The local government and the army negotiated a truce.该地方政府和军方谈判达成了休战协定。Western governments have this week urged him to negotiate and avoid force.西方国家政府本周已敦促他进行谈判并且避免使用武力。Frank Mariano negotiates the desert terrain in his battered pickup.弗兰克·马里亚诺驾驶他那辆破旧的敞篷小货车成功地穿越了沙漠地区。I negotiated the corner on my motorcycle and pulled to a stop.我骑着摩托车顺利地绕过弯道，停了下来。
nominate  vt. 推荐；提名；任命；指定This week one of them will be nominated by the Democratic Party for the presidency of the United States.本周他们中的一人将被民主党提名为美国总统职位的候选人。The Security Council can nominate anyone for secretary-general.安全理事会可以提名任何人为秘书长。In 1967 Johnson nominated Thurgood Marshall to the Supreme Court.1967年，约翰逊任命瑟古德·马歇尔为最高法院法官。She was nominated by the president as ambassador to Barbados.她被总统任命为驻巴巴多斯大使。Practically every film he made was nominated for an Oscar.他制作的每部电影几乎都获得了奥斯卡提名。
numerous  adj. 许多的，很多的Sex crimes were just as numerous as they are today.当时的性犯罪与现在一样多。
offend  vt. 冒犯；使…不愉快He apologizes for his comments and says he had no intention of offending the community.他为自己的评论道歉，并且说他无意冒犯那个团体。In the great effort not to offend, we end up saying nothing.为了尽量不冒犯人，我们最终什么也没说。She is terribly offended, angered and hurt by this.她被此深深地触犯、触怒并伤害了。In Western countries girls are far less likely to offend than boys.在西方国家，女孩们远不像男孩们那样容易犯罪。
offspring  n. 后代，子孙；产物Eleanor was now less anxious about her offspring than she had once been.这时，埃莉诺已不像以前那样为子女担忧了。
oppose  vt. 反对；对抗，抗争Mr. Taylor was not bitter toward those who had opposed him.泰勒先生并不仇恨那些曾经反对过他的人。
option  n. [计] 选项；选择权；买卖的特权He's argued from the start that the US and its allies are putting too much emphasis on the military option.他从一开始就争论说美国及其盟国过于看重军事这个选项。Criminals are given the option of going to jail or facing public humiliation.罪犯们被给予进监狱或面对公众羞辱的选择权。Each bank has granted the other an option on 19.9% of its shares.每家银行都已把自己股份的19.9%的期权给予另一家银行。Several options are offered for the student's senior year.好几门选修课开给毕业班的学生。I am keeping my options open; I can decide in a few months.我保留选择的权利；我可以几个月后再作出决定。
outdate  vt. 使过时；使废弃；使陈旧
overall  adj. 全部的；全体的；一切在内的...the overall rise in unemployment.…失业人数的总体上升。Overall I was disappointed.总的来说，我感到失望。...a man in white overalls....一个穿白色防护服的男人。
overflow  vi. 溢出；泛滥；充溢Pour in some of the broth, but not all of it, because it will probably overflow.倒入部分肉汤，不要全部，因为很可能会溢出来。The rivers overflowed their banks.那些河里的水漫过了河岸。Schreiber addressed an auditorium overflowing with journalists.施赖伯向挤满了新闻记者的观众席致辞。The kitchen garden was full to overflowing with fresh vegetables.菜园里长满了新鲜的蔬菜。
overtake  vt. 赶上；压倒；突然来袭Lung cancer has now overtaken breast cancer as a cause of death for women in the U.S.肺癌作为一种美国女性死亡原因现已超过了乳腺癌。Something like panic overtook me in a flood.一种类似恐慌的感觉在一次洪水中压倒了我。
overturn  vt. 推翻；倾覆；破坏The motorcycle veered out of control, overturned and smashed into a wall.摩托车转向失去了控制，翻倒在地，然后猛地撞到一面墙上。Alex jumped up so violently that he overturned his glass of wine.亚历克斯跃起得太猛，以至于打翻了他的那杯葡萄酒。When the courts overturned his decision, he backed down.当法院推翻了他的决定时，他让步了。
package  n. 包，包裹；套装软件，[计] 程序包I tore open the package.我撕开了那个包裹。...a package of doughnuts.…一包炸面圈。...a package of measures to help the film industry.…一揽子帮助电影业的措施。The beans are then ground and packaged for sale as ground coffee.咖啡豆接着被磨碎、包装，以研磨咖啡销售。A city is like any product, it has to be packaged properly to be attractive to the consumer.一座城市就像任何产品一样，需要适当地加以包装来吸引消费者。...package tours to Egypt.…去埃及的包价旅游。
panic  n. 恐慌，惊慌；大恐慌An earthquake has hit the capital, causing damage to buildings and panic among the population.一场地震袭击了首都，造成建筑物的损坏和人们的惊慌。There was a moment of panic as it became clear just how vulnerable the nation was.随着国家如此脆弱变得明显，出现了一阵恐慌局面。I'm in a panic about getting everything done in time.我处于一阵要把一切及时安排就绪的恐慌中。Guests panicked and screamed when the bomb exploded.炸弹爆炸的时候，客人们惊慌失措，惊声尖叫。The unexpected and sudden memory briefly panicked her.这突如其来的记忆使她一时惊慌失措。
parallel  n. 平行线；对比Readers familiar with military conflict will find a vague parallel to the Vietnam War.熟悉军事冲突的读者们会发现一个和越南战争大致相似的事件。It's an ecological disaster with no parallel anywhere else in the world.这是一场世界其他任何地方均无等同的生态灾难。Detailed study of folk music from a variety of countries reveals many close parallels.对不同国家的民乐的详细研究表明它们有很多相似之处。There are significant parallels with the 1980s.与20世纪80年代有显著的相似之处。Often there are emotional reasons paralleling the financial ones.经济原因的常常伴有情感原因。His remarks paralleled those of the president.他的评论与总统的评论相同。...parallel talks between the two countries' foreign ministers.…两国外长之间相似的谈话。Their instincts do not always run parallel with ours.他们的直觉并不总是与我们的同步。...seventy-two ships, drawn up in two parallel lines.…72艘船，停靠成两条平行线。Remsen Street is parallel with Montague Street.雷姆森大街与蒙塔古大街是平行的。...the area south of the 38th parallel.…38度纬线以南的地区。
patriot  n. 爱国者It has been suggested the founders were not true patriots but men out to protect their own interests.有人指出创建者并非真正的爱国者，而是一些维护自己利益的人。
pension  n. 退休金，抚恤金；津贴；膳宿费...struggling by on a pension.…靠养老金艰难度日。
perceive  vt. 察觉，感觉；理解；认知Students must perceive for themselves the relationship between success and effort.学生们必须自己去认识到成功与努力之间的关系。Stress is widely perceived as contributing to coronary heart disease.压力普遍被认为能造成冠心病。
permanent  adj. 永久的，永恒的；不变的Heavy drinking can cause permanent damage to the brain.饮酒过量可能造成永久性脑损伤。...a permanent solution to the problem.…一个解决该问题的永久性办法。His confidence had been permanently affected by the ordeal.他的信心已永久地被这次磨难影响了。...a permanent state of tension.…长期的紧张状态。They feel under permanent threat.他们感觉处在持续不断的威胁之下。...the heavy, permanently locked gate.…这扇厚重的、长年锁着的大门。At the end of the probationary period you will become a permanent employee.试用期结束后，你将成为终身雇员。...permanently employed lifeguards.…终身雇用的救生员。They had no permanent address.他们没有固定的地址。Her hair had had a permanent, but had grown out.她的头发曾经烫卷过，但又长出新的了。
permeate  vt. 渗透，透过；弥漫Bias against women permeates every level of the judicial system.对妇女的偏见全面影响司法体系的各个层面。The smell of roast beef permeated the air.烤牛肉的气味弥漫在空气中。
perpetual  adj. 永久的；不断的；四季开花的；无期限的...the creation of a perpetual union.…一个永久性工会的创立。They were all perpetually starving.他们一直都在挨饿。I thought her perpetual complaints were going to prove too much for me.我觉得她那永无休止的抱怨会让我吃不消的。He perpetually interferes in political affairs.他不断地干涉政治事务。
phase  n. 月相This autumn, 6000 residents will participate in the first phase of the project.今年秋季，6000名居民将参与这项计划的第一阶段。The crisis is entering a crucial, critical phase.危机正进入一个至关重要的决定性阶段。
pitch  vi. 倾斜；投掷；搭帐篷；坠落Simon pitched the empty bottle into the lake.西蒙把空瓶子投进湖里。We passed long, hot afternoons pitching a baseball.我们以打棒球来消磨一个个漫长的炎热午后。The movement took him by surprise, and he pitched forward.突然的移动让他猝不及防，向前跌倒。Alan staggered sideways, pitched head-first over the low wall and fell into the lake.艾伦两侧摇晃着，一头栽过矮墙，掉进湖里。They were being pitched into a new adventure in which they would have to fight the whole world.他们当时正被胁迫参与到一次不得不与整个世界抗衡的新冒险中。He raised his voice to an even higher pitch.他将嗓门提得更高了。His cry is pitched at a level that makes it impossible to ignore.他哭声之大让人不可能置若罔闻。His voice was pitched high, the words muffled by his crying.他的嗓门提得很高，说的话都被他的叫喊声压得听不清了。While this is very important material I think it's probably pitched at too high a level for our students.尽管这是个很重要的材料，但我认为它的难度太大，不适合我们的学生。The public's feelings were at a high pitch of indignation.公众的愤怒情绪达到了极点。My agent has pitched the idea to my editor in New York.我的代理人已向我在纽约的编辑力荐这个想法。...a football pitch.…一个足球场。He was the fastest thing I ever saw on a baseball field.他是我见过的在棒球场上跑得最快的家伙。The president speaks in New York today, making another pitch for his economic programme.总统今天在纽约发表讲话，再一次游说他的经济计划。
pitch  vi. 倾斜；投掷；搭帐篷；坠落Simon pitched the empty bottle into the lake.西蒙把空瓶子投进湖里。We passed long, hot afternoons pitching a baseball.我们以打棒球来消磨一个个漫长的炎热午后。The movement took him by surprise, and he pitched forward.突然的移动让他猝不及防，向前跌倒。Alan staggered sideways, pitched head-first over the low wall and fell into the lake.艾伦两侧摇晃着，一头栽过矮墙，掉进湖里。They were being pitched into a new adventure in which they would have to fight the whole world.他们当时正被胁迫参与到一次不得不与整个世界抗衡的新冒险中。He raised his voice to an even higher pitch.他将嗓门提得更高了。His cry is pitched at a level that makes it impossible to ignore.他哭声之大让人不可能置若罔闻。His voice was pitched high, the words muffled by his crying.他的嗓门提得很高，说的话都被他的叫喊声压得听不清了。While this is very important material I think it's probably pitched at too high a level for our students.尽管这是个很重要的材料，但我认为它的难度太大，不适合我们的学生。The public's feelings were at a high pitch of indignation.公众的愤怒情绪达到了极点。My agent has pitched the idea to my editor in New York.我的代理人已向我在纽约的编辑力荐这个想法。...a football pitch.…一个足球场。He was the fastest thing I ever saw on a baseball field.他是我见过的在棒球场上跑得最快的家伙。The president speaks in New York today, making another pitch for his economic programme.总统今天在纽约发表讲话，再一次游说他的经济计划。
plea  n. 恳求，请求；辩解，辩护；借口，托辞Mr. Nicholas made his emotional plea for help in solving the killing.尼古拉斯先生发出了令人感动的呼吁，恳求帮助破解这桩杀人案。The judge questioned him about his guilty plea.法官就他的认罪答辩对他提出质疑。We will enter a plea of not guilty.我们将进行无罪抗辩。Phillips murdered his wife, but got off on a plea of insanity.菲利普斯谋杀了自己的妻子，但以精神错乱为由逃脱了罪责。
plead  vt. 借口；为...辩护；托称The lady pleaded with her daughter to come back home.那位女士恳求她的女儿回家。He was kneeling on the floor pleading for mercy.他正跪在地板上请求宽恕。Morris had pleaded guilty to robbery.莫里斯已经承认犯有抢劫罪。He appeared before the committee to plead his case.他出现在委员会上为他的案子辩护。Mr. Giles pleads ignorance as his excuse.贾尔斯先生以不知情作为他的借口。
pop  n. 流行音乐；汽水；砰然声；枪击...the perfect combination of Caribbean rhythms, European pop, and American soul.…加勒比旋律、欧洲流行乐及美国灵乐的完美结合。...a life-size poster of a pop star.…一张如真人大小的流行歌星海报。...a can of pop.…一听碳酸饮料。Each corn kernel will make a loud pop when cooked.每颗玉米粒炒熟的时候都会发出很响的爆裂声。He untwisted the wire off the champagne bottle, and the cork popped and shot to the ceiling.他拧开香槟瓶子上的铁丝，瓶塞砰的一声冲到了天花板上。My eyes popped at the sight of the rich variety of food on show.我瞪大眼睛看着各色各样的食物展品。Marianne got a couple of mugs from the cupboard and popped a teabag into each of them.玛丽安娜从碗柜中拿出了几个杯子，把茶袋迅速地放入每个杯子中。I looked at Pop and he had big tears in his eyes.我看了看爸爸，他眼里噙着大滴的泪珠。
pop  n. 流行音乐；汽水；砰然声；枪击...the perfect combination of Caribbean rhythms, European pop, and American soul.…加勒比旋律、欧洲流行乐及美国灵乐的完美结合。...a life-size poster of a pop star.…一张如真人大小的流行歌星海报。...a can of pop.…一听碳酸饮料。Each corn kernel will make a loud pop when cooked.每颗玉米粒炒熟的时候都会发出很响的爆裂声。He untwisted the wire off the champagne bottle, and the cork popped and shot to the ceiling.他拧开香槟瓶子上的铁丝，瓶塞砰的一声冲到了天花板上。My eyes popped at the sight of the rich variety of food on show.我瞪大眼睛看着各色各样的食物展品。Marianne got a couple of mugs from the cupboard and popped a teabag into each of them.玛丽安娜从碗柜中拿出了几个杯子，把茶袋迅速地放入每个杯子中。I looked at Pop and he had big tears in his eyes.我看了看爸爸，他眼里噙着大滴的泪珠。
