denounce  vt. 谴责；告发；公然抨击；通告废除German leaders all took the opportunity to denounce the attacks and plead for tolerance.德国领导人们都藉此机会谴责这些攻击，并且恳请宽容。They were at the mercy of informers who might at any moment denounce them.他们完全受那些随时可能告发他们的告密者的支配。
density  n. 密度The region has a very high population density.这一地区人口密度很高。Jupiter's moon Io, whose density is 3.5 grams per cubic centimetre, is all rock.木星的卫星木卫一全是岩石，其密度为每立方厘米3.5克。
depart  vi. 离开；出发，起程；违反；去世Flight 43 will depart from Denver at 11:45 a.m. and arrive in Honolulu at 4:12 p.m.43号航班将于上午11:45从丹佛起飞，并于下午4:12到达檀香山。In the morning Mr. McDonald departed for Sydney.麦克唐纳先生早上起程去了悉尼。Why is it in this country that we have departed from good educational sense?为什么我们这个国家偏离了良好的教育观念？
deport  vt. 驱逐出境；举止；放逐...a government decision earlier this month to deport all illegal immigrants.…本月早些时候政府一项驱逐所有非法移民的决定。...thousands of migrants facing deportation.…面临被驱逐出境的数以千计的移民。
descend  vi. 下降；下去；下来；遗传；屈尊Things are cooler and more damp as we descend to the cellar.我们往地窖中下得越深，里面就越冷、越潮湿。Some 3,000 city officials will descend on Capitol Hill on Tuesday to lobby for more money.大约三千名市政官员将于周二突访美国国会山，为争取更多经费游说。He was ultimately overthrown and the country descended into chaos.他最终被推翻，国家陷入了混乱。We're not going to descend to such methods.我们不会堕落到使用这些方式的份上。
desirable  adj. 令人满意的；值得要的Prolonged negotiation was not desirable.拖得很长的谈判是不受欢迎的。...the desirability of democratic reform.…民主改革的可取性。...the young women of his own age whom his classmates thought most desirable.…与他同龄的、在他的同学们看来最性感的年轻女子。He had not at all overrated Veronica's desirability.他丝毫没有高估韦罗妮卡的性感。
despair  n. 绝望；令人绝望的人或事I looked at my wife in despair.我绝望地看着妻子。"Oh, I despair sometimes," he says in mock sorrow.“哦，我有时会绝望。”他假装悲伤地说。He wished to earn a living through writing but despaired of doing so.他原想通过写作谋生，但却对此绝望了。
destined  adj. 注定的；命定的；去往…的Any economic strategy based on a weak dollar is destined to fail.任何基于疲软的美元之上的经济策略都注定会失败。...products destined for Saudi Arabia.…运往沙特阿拉伯的产品。
destiny  n. 命运，定数，天命We are masters of our own destiny.我们是自己命运的主人。Is it destiny that brings people together, or is it accident?是定数，还是偶然，将人们带到一起？
destructive  adj. 破坏的；毁灭性的；有害的，消极的...the awesome destructive power of nuclear weapons.…核武器可怕的毁怀性力量。
devise  vt. 设计；想出；发明；图谋；遗赠给We devised a scheme to help him.我们想出了一个计划来帮助他。
diagnose  vt. 诊断；断定The soldiers were diagnosed as having flu.这些士兵被诊断为患了流感。Susan had a mental breakdown and was diagnosed with schizophrenia.苏珊精神崩溃，被诊断为精神分裂。
dilute  adj. 稀释的；淡的If you give your baby juice, dilute it well with cooled, boiled water.喂婴儿果汁要用凉开水充分稀释。The liquid is then diluted.然后液体就变稀了。There was a clear intention to dilute black voting power.削弱黑人选举权的意图是显而易见的。...a dilute solution of bleach.…稀释了的漂白液。
dim  adj. 暗淡的，昏暗的；模糊的，看不清的；悲观的，怀疑的She stood waiting in the dim light.她站在昏暗的灯光下等待着。Two lamps burned dimly.两盏油灯昏暗地燃烧着。The room was dim and cool and quiet.这房间昏暗、阴冷且安静。Pete's flashlight picked out the dim figures of Bob and Chang.皮特的手电筒照射出鲍勃和常的蒙胧身影。The shoreline could be dimly seen.海岸线隐约可见。It seems that the '60s era of social activism is all but a dim memory.60年代的社会激进主义时代似乎只剩下模糊的记忆。Christina dimly recalled the procedure.克里斯蒂娜隐约地记起了那个步骤。The prospects for a peaceful solution are dim.找到和平解决方案的前景渺茫。Sometimes he thought George was a bit dim.有时他觉得乔治有点儿笨。Dim the lighting – it is unpleasant to lie with a bright light shining in your eyes.把灯光调暗–在刺眼的灯光下躺着不舒服。Their economic prospects have dimmed.他们的经济前景变得暗淡了。Their memory of what happened has dimmed.他们对所发生的事的记忆变得模糊了。
discard  vt. 抛弃；放弃；丢弃Read the manufacturer's guidelines before discarding the box.先阅读制造商的说明书再把盒子丢掉。
discrete  adj. 离散的，不连续的...instruction manuals that break down jobs into scores of discrete steps.…将这些工作分解为多个分立步骤的说明书。
dismay  n. 沮丧，灰心；惊慌Local politicians have reacted with dismay and indignation.当地政客们作出了恐慌和愤慨的反应。The committee was dismayed by what it had been told.该委员会被所告知的情况搞得焦虑不安。He was dismayed at the cynicism of the youngsters.他对年轻人们的愤世嫉俗感到伤心焦虑。
disorder  n. 混乱；骚乱...a rare nerve disorder that can cause paralysis of the arms.…一种罕见的能导致手臂瘫痪的神经紊乱疾病。Six months ago America's worst civil disorder in more than 100 years erupted in the city of Los Angeles.6个月前，美国100多年来最严重的市民骚乱在洛杉矶市爆发了。The emergency room was in disorder.急救室一片混乱。
dispose  vt. 处理；处置；安排
disregard  vt. 忽视；不理；漠视；不顾He disregarded the advice of his executives.他对主管们的建议置之不理。Whoever planted the bomb showed a total disregard for the safety of the public.不论谁安置了炸弹都显示出对公众安全的全然漠视。
distinctive  adj. 有特色的，与众不同的...the distinctive odour of chlorine.…氯气的特殊气味。...the distinctively fragrant taste of elderflowers.…接骨木花奇特的香味。
distort  vt. 扭曲；使失真；曲解The media distorts reality; it categorizes people as all good or all bad.媒体歪曲事实，将人分为十足的好人和坏蛋。These figures give a distorted view of the significance for the local economy.这些数据对当地经济的重要性给出了歪曲的看法。A painter may exaggerate or distort shapes and forms.画家可能会夸大或扭曲形状与形式。Sound was becoming more and more distorted through the use of hearing aids.由于使用助听器，声音变得越来越失真。
distract  vt. 转移；分心Tom admits that playing video games sometimes distracts him from his homework.汤姆承认玩电子游戏有时让他做家庭作业时分心。Don't let yourself be distracted by fashionable theories.别让自己被新潮的理论给分心了。
distress  n. 危难，不幸；贫困；悲痛Jealousy causes distress and painful emotions.嫉妒会引发悲伤和痛苦的情绪。He expressed concern that the ship might be in distress.他对船可能处在危急状态表示忧虑。The idea of Toni being in danger distresses him enormously.想到托尼仍处在危险当中就使他忧心忡忡。
diverse  adj. 不同的；多种多样的；变化多的The building houses a wide and diverse variety of antiques.这栋楼里摆放着大量各式各样的古董。Albert Jones' new style will inevitably put him in touch with a much more diverse and perhaps younger audience.艾伯特·琼斯的新风格无疑将使他接触更多形形色色的、或许更年轻的观众。
dividend  n. 红利；股息；[数] 被除数；奖金The first quarter dividend has been increased by nearly 4 percent.第一季度的股息增加了近4％。Steps taken now to maximize your health will pay dividends later on.现在采取措施充分重视你的健康将来就会有回报。
division  n. [数] 除法；部门；分配；分割；师（军队）；赛区...the unification of Germany, after its division into two states at the end of World War Two.…德国在二战结束时分裂成两个国家，之后又统一了。The current division of labour between workers and management will alter.劳资双方目前的劳动分配将会改变。I taught my daughter how to do division at the age of six.我女儿6岁时，我就教她怎样做除法。The division between the prosperous west and the impoverished east remains.富裕的西部和贫穷的东部之间的对立依然存在。...the bank's Latin American division.…该银行的拉丁美洲部。Several armoured divisions are being moved from Germany.几个装甲师正从德国调来。Chico State reached the NCAA Division II national finals last season.奇科加州大学上个赛季进入了全国大学体育协会乙级全国决赛。
domestic  adj. 国内的；家庭的；驯养的；一心只管家务的...over 100 domestic flights a day to 30 leading U.S. destinations.…每天飞往美国30个主要目的地的100多个国内航班。...a plan for sharing domestic chores.…一份分担家务的计划。...domestic appliances.…家用电器。It was a scene of such domestic bliss.这是一幕家庭美满的场景。...a domestic cat.…一只家猫。
dominant  adj. 显性的；占优势的；支配的，统治的...a change which would maintain his party's dominant position in Scotland.…巩固他的政党在苏格兰支配地位的一场变革。
doom  n. 厄运；死亡；判决；世界末日...his warnings of impending doom.…他对即将到来的厄运发出的警告。Why are people so full of gloom and doom?人们的心里为什么满是悲观失望？That argument was the turning point for their marriage, and the one which doomed it to failure.那次争吵是他们婚姻的一个转折点，它注定了他们婚姻的失败。
dread  n. 恐惧；可怕的人（或物）I'm dreading Christmas this year.我害怕今年的圣诞节。I dreaded coming back, to be honest.老实说，我很害怕回来。She thought with dread of the cold winters to come.想到寒冬即将到来，她就感到恐惧。I dread to think what will happen in the case of a major emergency.我不敢想像万一出现重大紧急情况会怎么样。
dropout  n. 中途退学；辍学学生...long-haired, dope-smoking dropouts.…蓄着长发，吸着大麻的离经叛道之人。...high-school dropouts.…中学辍学生。The dropout rate among students is currently one in three.学生的辍学率目前是1/3。
duplicate  vt. 复制；使加倍His task will be to duplicate his success overseas here at home.他的任务将是在国内复制他在海外的成功。The tight race is almost a duplicate of the elections in Georgia and South Dakota last month that pitted a Republican challenger against a Democratic incumbent.这次紧张的竞选几乎是上个月在佐治亚州和南达科他州选举的翻版，由一个共和党的挑战者竞争一个现任的民主党人。...a business which duplicates video tapes for the film makers.…一家为电影制片人复制录像带的企业。I'm on my way to Switzerland, but I've lost my card. I've got to get a duplicate.我在去瑞士的路上，但是我的卡丢了。我得弄张补发卡。He let himself in with a duplicate key.他用一把另配的钥匙打开门进去了。
electrical  adj. 有关电的；电气科学的...shipments of electrical equipment.…电器设备的运输。...electrically powered vehicles.…电动车。...lighting and other electrical systems on the new runway.…新跑道上的照明和其他电力系统。...brief pulses of electrical energy.…短暂的电能脉冲。...electrically charged particles.…带电的粒子。...company representatives from the electrical industry.…来自电力行业的公司代表。
embed  vt. 栽种；使嵌入，使插入；使深留脑中One of the bullets passed through Andrea's chest before embedding itself in a wall.其中一颗子弹穿过安德烈亚的胸膛然后嵌入一面墙中。The fossils at Dinosaur Cove are embedded in hard sandstone.恐龙湾中的化石嵌在坚硬的砂岩中。This agreement will be embedded in a state treaty to be signed soon.这项协议将被纳入到一份即将被签署的国家条约中。I think that hatred of the other is deeply embedded in our society.我觉得对异己的憎恨在我们的社会中根深蒂固。
embody  vt. 体现，使具体化；具体表达Jack Kennedy embodied all the hopes of the 1960s.杰克•肯尼迪体现了20世纪60年代的全部希望。For twenty-nine years, Checkpoint Charlie embodied the Cold War.29年来，查理检查站具体象征了冷战。The proposal has been embodied in a draft resolution.这项提议已经被包含在一份决议草案中。
emerge  vi. 浮现；摆脱；暴露Richard was waiting outside the door as she emerged.当她出现的时候，理查德正等候在门外。She then emerged from the courthouse to thank her supporters.于是她从法院大楼出来向支持者们表示感谢。There is growing evidence that the economy is at last emerging from recession.有越来越多的迹象表明经济将最终摆脱萧条。...the growing corruption that has emerged in the past few years.…过去几年中暴露出来的日趋严重的腐败。It soon emerged that neither the July nor August mortgage payment had been collected.很快显示的是7月和8月的抵押款都没有被收取。Vietnam has emerged as the world's third-biggest rice exporter.越南已立足成为世界第三大稻米出口国。...the new republic that emerged in October 1917.…1917年10月成立的新共和国。
emit  vt. 发出，放射；发行；发表The new device emits a powerful circular column of light.这个新装置发出一束强烈的环形光柱。Whitney blinked and emitted a long, low whistle.惠特尼眨了眨眼，吹出了一声长而低沉的口哨。
emphasize  vt. 强调，着重But it's also been emphasized that no major policy changes can be expected to come out of the meeting.但是也强调，这次会议预期不会做出重大政策改变。
engagement  n. 婚约；约会；交战；诺言He had an engagement at a restaurant at eight.他8点钟在一家餐馆有一个约会。I've broken off my engagement to Arthur.我已经解除了于阿瑟的订婚约定。We spoke every night during our engagement.我们订婚期间每晚都交谈。The constitution prohibits them from military engagement on foreign soil.宪法禁止他们在外国领土上的军事交战。
entertain  vt. 娱乐；招待；怀抱；容纳They were entertained by top singers, dancers and celebrities.他们饶有兴趣地看了顶级歌手、舞蹈演员和名流们的演出。To generate new money the sport needs to be more entertaining.想生更多的财，这项运动得更有娱乐性。I don't like to entertain guests anymore.我不再喜欢招待客人。He loves to entertain.他喜欢宴客。...a cosy area for entertaining and relaxing.…一个宴客与休闲的舒适场所。How foolish I am to entertain doubts.我心存疑虑是多么愚蠢啊。
envisage  vt. 正视，面对；想像He envisages the possibility of establishing direct diplomatic relations in the future.他设想将来建立直接外交关系的可能性。
epidemic  adj. 流行的；传染性的A flu epidemic is sweeping through Moscow.一场流感正席卷莫斯科。...an epidemic of serial killings.…连环谋杀的盛行。
equation  n. 方程式，等式；相等；[化学] 反应式The equation is simple: research breeds new products.这个情况是简单的：研究孕育新产品。The party fears the equation between higher spending and higher taxes.该党害怕增加开支和增高税收之间的相互制衡。
evoke  vt. 引起，唤起；博得...the scene evoking memories of those old movies.…唤起对那些老电影的记忆的场景。
evolve  vt. 发展；进化；使逐步形成；推断出The bright plumage of many male birds was thought to have evolved to attract females.许多雄鸟的鲜艳羽毛被认为是为吸引雌鸟而进化来的。Birds are widely believed to have evolved from dinosaurs.鸟类普遍被认为是从恐龙进化而来的。...a tiny airline which eventually evolved into Pakistan International Airlines.…最终发展成为巴基斯坦国际航空公司的一家小型航空公司。Popular music evolved from folk songs.流行音乐由民歌演变而来。
excess  n. 超过，超额；过度，过量；无节制An excess of house plants in a small apartment can be oppressive.在一套狭小公寓里放过多的室内植物会给人压抑感。After cooking the fish, pour off any excess fat.烹调完鱼后，倒掉多余的油。Make sure that you don't have to pay expensive excess charges.确保你不需要支付昂贵的额外费用。The value of the company is well in excess of $2 billion.该公司的价值远超过20亿美元。I was reasonably fit, played a lot of tennis, and didn't smoke or drink to excess.我那时很健康，常打网球，不过度抽烟或喝酒。
exclaim  vi. 呼喊，惊叫；大声叫嚷"He went back to the lab," Inez exclaimed impatiently.“他回实验室了，”伊内兹不耐烦地叫道。
exclusive  adj. 独有的；排外的；专一的It used to be a private, exclusive club, and now it's open to all New Yorkers.它曾是一家高档的私人俱乐部，而现在它对所有纽约人开放。Our group will have exclusive use of a 60-foot boat.我们组将有一条专用的60英尺的船。He told the magazine in an exclusive interview: "All my problems stem from drinking."他在一次独家采访中告知那家杂志：“我所有的问题源于饮酒。”Some papers thought they had an exclusive.一些报社以为他们有一条独家报道。...the average cost of a three-course dinner exclusive of tax, tip and beverage.…不含税、小费和酒水费用的3道菜晚餐的平均花费。They both have learned that ambition and successful fatherhood can be mutually exclusive.他们都明白了事业心与做个成功的父亲是互相排斥的。
execution  n. 执行，实行；完成；死刑
exempt  vt. 免除；豁免Men in college were exempt from military service.在校男大学生免服兵役。South Carolina claimed the power to exempt its citizens from the obligation to obey federal law.南卡罗来纳州宣称有权使其公民免除遵守联邦法律的义务。...the exemption of employer-provided health insurance from taxation.…雇主提供的医疗保险的税项免除。
expire  vi. 期满；终止；死亡；呼气He had lived illegally in the United States for five years after his visitor's visa expired.访问签证到期后他在美国非法居住了5年。
extend  vt. 延伸；扩大；推广；伸出；给予；使竭尽全力；对…估价The caves extend for some 12 miles.这些洞穴延伸约12英里。The main stem will extend to around 12 ft, if left to develop naturally.如果让其自然生长，主干会延伸到12英尺左右。A table extended from the front of her desk to create a T-shaped seating arrangement.一张桌子从她的办公桌前端伸出，形成T型的座位排列。The normal cyclone season extends from December to April.正常的飓风季节从12月持续到4月。The service also extends to wrapping and delivering gifts.这项服务还包括包装及递送礼物。The talks will extend to the church, human rights groups, and other social organizations.这些会谈将涉及教会、人权组织和其他的社会组织。This year they have introduced three new products to extend their range.今年他们已引入了3种新产品以扩大他们的范围。The building was extended in 1500.该建筑于1500年扩建。...a table that extends to accommodate extra guests.…一张能伸展以容纳更多客人的桌子。They have extended the deadline by twenty-four hours.他们已经将最后期限延长了24小时。It might be possible to extend the technique to other crop plants.把该技术扩延到其它农作物上也许是可能的。The man extended his hand: "I'm Chuck."这位男士伸出了他的手：“我是查克。”
extinct  adj. 灭绝的，绝种的；熄灭的At the current rate of decline, many of the rain forest animals could become extinct in less than 10 years.按照目前的下降速度，许多雨林动物不到十年就会绝种。Herbalism had become an all but extinct skill in the Western world.草药医术在西方世界几乎已成了一项绝迹的技术。Its tallest volcano, long extinct, is Olympus Mons.它最高的火山是已死很久的奥林匹斯山。
extraordinary  adj. 非凡的；特别的；离奇的；特派的We've made extraordinary progress as a society in that regard.我们社会在那方面已经取得了巨大进步。The task requires extraordinary patience and endurance.这项工作需要非凡的耐心和毅力。She's extraordinarily disciplined.她特别遵守纪律。What an extraordinary thing to happen!发生了多么非同寻常的事啊！Apart from the hair, he looked extraordinarily unchanged.除了头发，他看上去真是一点也没变。The U.S. has called for an extraordinary emergency meeting of the UN Human Rights Commission to examine the crisis.美国已要求召开一次联合国人权委员特别紧急会议来调查这次危机。
fabricate  vt. 制造；伪造；装配All four claim that officers fabricated evidence against them.4人全部声称官员们伪造了不利于他们的证据。She described the interview as a "complete fabrication."她把这次采访描述为“纯属虚构”。
facet  n. 面；方面；小平面The caste system shapes nearly every facet of Indian life.种姓制度几乎决定了印度生活的各个方面。
facilitate  vt. 促进；帮助；使容易The new airport will facilitate the development of tourism.新机场将促进旅游业的发展。
farewell  n. 告别，辞别；再见；再会They said their farewells there at the cafe.他们在咖啡馆那儿道了别。
fascinate  vt. 使着迷，使神魂颠倒Politics fascinated Franklin's father.政治让富兰克林的父亲着迷。
feasible  adj. 可行的；可能的；可实行的She questioned whether it was feasible to stimulate investment in these regions.她质问在这些地区刺激投资是否可行。The committee will study the feasibility of setting up a national computer network.委员会将研究建立一个国家计算机网络的可行性。
feminine  adj. 女性的；妇女（似）的；阴性的；娇柔的...male leaders worrying about their women abandoning traditional feminine roles.…担心他们的女人会抛弃传统女性角色的男性领导人。I've always been attracted to very feminine women who are not overpowering.我总是被那些不强悍的女人味十足的女人所吸引。
fertilizer  n. [肥料] 肥料；受精媒介物；促进发展者...farming without any purchased chemical, fertilizer or pesticide.…不使用任何购买的化学品、肥料或杀虫剂的耕作。
finance  n. 财政，财政学；金融The fund has been used largely to finance the construction of federal prisons.该基金大部分已用于资助联邦监狱的建造。A United States delegation is in Japan seeking finance for a major scientific project.1个美国代表团正在日本为一个重大科研项目寻求资助。...a major player in the world of high finance.…高层金融界的大腕。The report recommends an overhaul of public finances.这份报告建议对公共财政进行彻底检视。Be prepared for unexpected news concerning your finances.对关于你财务状况的意外消息要做好准备。
finite  adj. 有限的；限定的...a finite set of elements.…有限的一组元素。Only a finite number of situations can arise.只有有限的几种情况可能会出现。
flare  vt. 使闪耀；使张开；用发光信号发出；使外倾...a ship which had fired a distress flare.…一艘发出了遇险信号弹的船。Camp fires flared like beacons in the dark.篝火突然熊熊燃烧起来，像黑暗中的灯塔。Don't spill too much fat on the barbecue as it could flare up.不要在烤肉上浇太多的油，因为它可能会突然烧起来。Even as the president appealed for calm, trouble flared in several American cities.即使在总统呼吁大家保持冷静时，美国几座城市里仍在爆发骚乱。Dozens of people were injured as fighting flared up.数十人由于战斗激化而负伤。Tempers flared and harsh words were exchanged.人们大动肝火，对骂起来。
flip  vt. 掷；轻击He didn't flip on the headlights until he was two blocks away.直到过了两个街区后，他才打开前灯。Then he walked out, flipping the lights off.接着他走了出去，随手把灯关掉。He was flipping through a magazine in the living room.他在起居室里快速翻阅一本杂志。The plane then flipped over and burst into flames.这时飞机翻了个个儿，接着就燃烧了起来。I pulled a coin from my pocket and flipped it.我从口袋里掏出一枚硬币，把它投掷出去。
flutter  vi. 飘动；鼓翼；烦扰Her chiffon skirt was fluttering in the night breeze.她的薄绸裙在晚风中飘动。...a butterfly fluttering its wings.…一只拍动着翅膀的蝴蝶。...a flutter of white cloth.…白布的飘动。The paper fluttered to the floor.纸飘落到地板上。
forecast  vt. 预报，预测；预示...a forecast of a 2.25 percent growth in the economy.…2.25%经济增长的预报。He delivered his election forecast.他作了他的选举预报。They forecast a humiliating defeat for the president.他们预言总统蒙受羞辱的一次失败。
foretell  vt. 预言；预示；预告...prophets who have foretold the end of the world.…预言了世界末日的先知们。
forge  n. 熔炉，锻铁炉；铁工厂The prime minister is determined to forge a good relationship with the country's new leader.该首相决意与该国的新领袖建立良好的关系。They agreed to forge closer economic ties.他们同意建立更密切的经济联系。He admitted seven charges including forging passports.他承认了包括伪造护照在内的7项罪名。They used forged documents to leave the country.他们利用伪造的文件离开了这个国家。...the most prolific art forger in the country.…该国最大的艺术品伪造者。
formula  n. [数] 公式，准则；配方；婴儿食品...a peace formula.…一项和平方案。He developed a mathematical formula describing the distances of the planets from the Sun.他提出了一个描述各行星与太阳之间距离的数学公式。Glucose and fructose have the same chemical formula but have very different properties.葡萄糖和果糖具有相同的化学分子式但有很不同的特性。After he was officially pronounced the world's oldest man, he offered this simple formula for a long and happy life.在他被正式宣布为世界上最老的人之后，他提供了这一长寿和幸福生活的简单方法。
formulate  vt. 规划；用公式表示；明确地表达Little by little, he formulated his plan for escape.他一点一点地构想出了他的逃跑计划。I was impressed by the way he could formulate his ideas.我对他表述自己想法的独特用词印象深刻。
forum  n. 论坛，讨论会；法庭；公开讨论的广场Members of the council agreed that was an important forum for discussion.理事会成员们一致认为那是一个用于讨论的重要论坛。
foster  vt. 培养；养育，抚育；抱（希望等）Little Jack was placed with foster parents.小杰克被安置在养父母家。She has since gone on to find happiness by fostering more than 100 children.她此后又通过收养一百多个孩子找到了快乐。He said that developed countries had a responsibility to foster global economic growth to help new democracies.他说发达国家有一种促进全球经济增长以帮助新兴民主国家的责任。
fragile  adj. 脆的；易碎的The fragile economies of several southern African nations could be irreparably damaged.几个南部非洲国家脆弱的经济可能会无可挽救地被摧垮。By mid-1988 there were clear indications of the extreme fragility of the Right-wing coalition.到1988年年中有明显的迹象表明右翼联盟极度脆弱。He leaned back in his fragile chair.他向后靠在他那把不结实的椅子上。Older drivers are more likely to be seriously injured because of the fragility of their bones.年纪较大的司机因骨骼易碎而更可能会受重伤。
fringe  n. 边缘；穗；刘海The jacket had leather fringes.这件上衣饰有皮流苏。...black townships located on the fringes of the city.…位于该城市边缘的黑人居住区。The party remained on the fringe of the political scene until last year.直到去年该党还一直处于政治舞台的外围。My fringe was cut short, but the rest of my hair was long.我的刘海剪得短,但其余的头发长。The monarchists are a small fringe group who quarrel fiercely among themselves.君主制拥护者们是个边缘性小团体，内部争吵激烈。
fulfil  vt. 履行；完成；实践；满足President Kaunda fulfilled his promise of announcing a date for the referendum.卡翁达总统实现了他的关于宣布投票公决日期的诺言。Without them you will not be able to fulfil the tasks you have before you.没有他们你将不能完成你面前的任务。The war was the biggest thing in her life and nothing after that quite fulfilled her.那场战争是她一生中最重大的事，在那之后没有什么颇使她感到满足过。She has courageously continued to lead a fulfilled life.她已勇敢地继续过一种心满意足的生活。
furnish  vt. 提供；供应；装备Many proprietors try to furnish their hotels with antiques.许多企业主尽可能用古董装饰他们的旅馆。They'll be able to furnish you with the rest of the details.他们将能够给你提供其余的细节。
galaxy  n. [天] 星系；银河系（the Galaxy）；一群显赫的人Astronomers have discovered a distant galaxy.天文学家们发现了一个遥远的星系。The Galaxy consists of 100 billion stars.银河系由1千亿颗恒星组成。
generosity  n. 慷慨，大方；宽宏大量There are stories about his generosity, the massive amounts of money he gave to charities.关于他的慷慨有些传闻，说他向慈善机构捐献巨款。
given  adj. 赠予的；沉溺的；规定的In chess there are typically about 36 legal moves from any given board position.在国际象棋中，从棋盘的任何一个特定方格通常都可以移动大致36步。Write down the sort of thing you would like to do, given the opportunity.如果有机会，请写下你想做的那类事。Usually, I am sensible with money, as I have to be, given that I don't earn that much.我花钱通常是很明智的。考虑到自己挣得不多，必须这样做。Given the uncertainty over Leigh's future I was left with little other choice.考虑到莉前途未卜，我几乎没有选择余地。
gleam  n. 微光；闪光；瞬息的一现His black hair gleamed in the sun.他的黑头发在阳光下闪闪发光。There was a gleam of hope for a peaceful settlement.和平解决曾有一线希望。
gossip  n. 小道传闻；随笔；爱说长道短的人He spent the first hour talking gossip.他头一个小时尽在说人闲话。There has been much gossip about the possible reasons for his absence.关于他缺席的原因已经有多种传闻。We spoke, debated, gossiped into the night.我们交谈、争论、闲聊到夜间。Eva gossiped with Sarah.伊娃与萨拉闲聊。He was a vicious gossip.他是个可恶的饶舌者。
govern  vt. 管理；支配；统治；控制They go to the polls on Friday to choose the people they want to govern their country.他们周五去投票站选出他们希望来治理国家的人。Marine insurance is governed by a strict series of rules and regulations.海上保险受一系列严格的规章条例所制约。
gracious  adj. 亲切的；高尚的；和蔼的；雅致的She is a lovely and gracious woman.她是个可爱而和蔼的女人。She closed with a gracious speech of thanks.她以彬彬有礼的致谢辞作结。Hospitality at the presidential guest house was graciously declined.总统套房里的款待被婉言谢绝了。He drove through the gracious suburbs with the swimming pools and tennis courts.他开车穿过了建有游泳池和网球场的舒适的城郊。Good gracious, look at that specimen, will you?天哪，你看看那个家伙，好吗？
grieve  vt. 使悲伤，使苦恼He's grieving over his dead wife and son.他因丧妻失子而悲痛不已。I didn't have any time to grieve.我没有时间去悲伤。
groan  vi. 呻吟；抱怨；发吱嘎声Slowly, he opened his eyes. As he did so, he began to groan with pain.他慢慢地睁开眼睛，并开始痛苦地呻吟。They glanced at the man on the floor, who began to groan.他们扫了一眼地板上那个开始呻吟的男子。She heard him let out a pitiful, muffled groan.她听到他发出一声可怜、压抑的呻吟。"My leg – I think it's broken," Eric groaned.“我的腿–我想是断了，”埃里克呻吟着说。His parents were beginning to groan about the price of college tuition.他的父母开始抱怨大学的学费。Listen sympathetically to your child's moans and groans about what she can't do.要充满同情地去倾听孩子对她不能做的事而发的牢骚和抱怨。The timbers groan and creak and the floorboards shift.木料吱嘎作响，地板也跟着动。The bar counter groans under the weight of huge plates of the freshest fish.酒吧柜台上堆满了大盘大盘最新鲜的鱼。Consumers were groaning under the weight of high interest rates.消费者受着高利率的重压。
halt  vi. 停止；立定；踌躇，犹豫They halted at a short distance from the house.他们停在离房子不远处。Striking workers halted production at the auto plant yesterday.昨天，汽车厂的罢工工人完全停止了生产。the haltThe Russian government had called a halt to the construction of a new project in the Rostov region.俄罗斯政府已经决定停止在罗斯托夫地区的一个新工程的修建。The lift creaked to a halt at the ground floor.电梯嘎吱一声停在了底楼。Her political career came to a halt in December 1988.她的政治生涯于1988年12月彻底结束了。
heap  n. 堆；许多；累积...a heap of bricks.…一堆砖。Mrs. Madrigal heaped more carrots onto Michael's plate.马德里加尔太太往迈克尔的盘子里放了更多的胡萝卜。Off to one side, the militia was heaping up wood for a bonfire.在一侧，民兵们正在堆起木柴，准备生起篝火。The head of the navy heaped scorn on both the methods and motives of the conspirators.这位海军首领对密谋分子的做法和动机都给予了极大的蔑视。You have heaps of time.你有很多时间。
hemisphere  n. 半球...the depletion of the ozone layer in the northern hemisphere.…北半球臭氧层的消耗。
hesitate  vi. 踌躇，犹豫；不愿The telephone rang. Catherine hesitated, debating whether to answer it.电话响了。凯瑟琳迟疑着，考虑是否接听。Asked if he would go back, Mr. Searle said after some hesitation, "I'll have to think about that."当被问及他是否愿意回去时，瑟尔先生迟疑了一下后说：“我得考虑一下。”Some parents hesitate to take these steps because they suspect that their child is exaggerating.一些家长迟迟不肯采取这些措施，因为他们怀疑自己的孩子在夸大其词。In the event of difficulties, please do not hesitate to contact our Customer Service Department.如有困难，请不要迟疑，与我们的客户服务部联系。
hierarchy  n. 层级；等级制度Like most other American companies with a rigid hierarchy, workers and managers had strictly defined duties.像大多数其他等级制度森严的美国公司一样，工人和管理人员都有严格界定的职责。The church hierarchy today feels the church should reflect the social and political realities of the country.教会统治集团如今感到教会应该反映国家的社会现实和政治现实。
highlight  vt. 突出；强调；使显著；加亮Last year Collins wrote a moving ballad which highlighted the plight of the homeless.去年柯林斯写了一首感人的叙事诗，突出描写了无家可归者的苦境。Highlight the chosen area by clicking and holding down the left mouse button.通过点击鼠标左键并摁住以突出显示所选区域。...a match that is likely to prove one of the highlights of the tournament.…可能是本届锦标赛最精彩的赛事之一。
hike  vi. 远足；徒步旅行；上升The site is reached by a 30-minute hike through dense forest.要花30分钟徒步穿过密林才能到达那个地方。You could hike through the Fish River Canyon – it's entirely up to you.你可以远足穿越菲什干河大峡谷–这全由你自己决定。...some harder, more strenuous hiking on cliff pathways.…在悬崖峭壁的小路上进行的更艰难、更费力的长途行走。...a sudden 1.75 percent hike in interest rates.…利率突涨1.75%。It has now been forced to hike its rates by 5.25 percent.它现在被迫将其税率提高5.25%。The insurers have started hiking up premiums by huge amounts.保险公司已经开始大幅度地提高保险费。
hinge  n. 铰链，折叶；关键，转折点；枢要，中枢The top swung open on well-oiled hinges.盖子在上好油的折叶上一下子弹开了。
hoist  n. 起重机；升起，吊起Hoisting my suitcase on to my shoulder, I turned and headed toward my hotel.我把手提箱扛到肩膀上，转身朝旅馆走去。A twenty-foot steel pyramid is to be hoisted into position on top of the tower.一座20英尺高的钢制金字塔将被吊到塔顶该放的位置上。He uses a hydraulic hoist to unload two empty barrels.他用一架液压起重机卸下两只空桶。A group forced their way through police cordons and hoisted their flag on top of the disputed monument.一群人强行冲破警方警戒线，把他们的旗帜升到了那座有争议的纪念碑的顶部。
horizon  n. [天] 地平线；视野；眼界；范围In the distance, the dot of a boat appeared on the horizon.远处小黑点般的一条小船出现在地平线上。As your horizons expand, these new ideas can give a whole new meaning to life.随着你的眼界不断开阔，这些新观念将给你的生活赋予崭新的意义。With breast cancer, as with many common diseases, there is no obvious breakthrough on the horizon.就乳腺癌来说，如同许多常见病一样，目前还看不到明显的突破。
hospitality  n. 好客；殷勤Every visitor to Georgia is overwhelmed by the kindness, charm, and hospitality of the people.来到佐治亚州的每一个人都为当地人的善良、魅力和好客感动不已。...corporate hospitality tents.…公司为客人提供饮料食品等招待服务的帐篷。
hostile  adj. 敌对的，敌方的；怀敌意的Many people felt he would be hostile to the idea of foreign intervention.许多人觉得他会反对外来干预。The West has gradually relaxed its hostile attitude to this influential state.西方对这个有影响力的国家的敌对态度已趋缓和。Drinking may make a person feel relaxed and happy, or it may make her hostile, violent, or depressed.喝酒可以使一个人感到放松和愉快，也可以让人变得不友善、粗暴或沮丧。...some of the most hostile climatic conditions in the world.…世界上最不利的一些气候条件。Soon after he arrived, Kingfisher launched a hostile bid for Dixons.金费希尔到任之后不久就开始了对迪克森斯公司的恶意收购投标。The city is encircled by a hostile army.该市被敌军包围。
hover  vi. 盘旋，翱翔；徘徊Beautiful butterflies hovered above the wild flowers.美丽的蝴蝶在野花上方盘旋。Judith was hovering in the doorway.朱迪丝在门口徘徊。She hovered on the brink of death for three months as doctors battled to save her.3个月来在医生们奋力挽救她的生命的过程中，她一直处在死亡的边缘。In September 1989 the exchange rate hovered around 140 yen to the dollar.在1989年9月，汇率一直在140日元比1美元左右徘徊。
humble  adj. 谦逊的；简陋的；（级别或地位）低下的；不大的He gave a great performance, but he was very humble.他的表演很精彩，但他却很谦逊。"I'm a lucky man, undeservedly lucky," he said humbly.“我是个幸运的人，不该这么幸运，”他谦虚地说。Spyros Latsis started his career as a humble fisherman in the Aegean.斯派罗斯·拉齐斯最初的职业是爱琴海的一名地位低微的渔夫。There are restaurants, both humble and expensive, that specialize in noodles.既有普通的也有昂贵的专营面条的餐馆。It is, in my humble opinion, perhaps the best steak restaurant in the city.以我之拙见，它也许是该市最好的牛排馆。So may I humbly suggest we all do something next time.那么我可否愚拙地提议下次我们大家都做点什么。Anson was forced to eat humble pie and publicly apologize to her.安森被迫认错并公开向她道歉。Honda won fame in the 1980s as the little car company that humbled the industry giants.20世纪80年代，本田作为一家小型汽车公司因一举击垮行业巨头而声名鹊起。Ted's words humbled me.特德的一席话使我自感惭愧。Giving up an addiction is a humbling experience.戒掉一种嗜好是一次令自尊心受挫的经历。
identical  adj. 同一的；完全相同的The three bombs were virtually identical.这3个炸弹几乎一模一样。...nine identically dressed female dancers.…9个着装相同的女舞蹈演员。
ignorant  adj. 无知的；愚昧的People don't like to ask questions for fear of appearing ignorant.人们不喜欢问问题，生怕显得自己无知。I met some ignorant people who called me all kinds of names.我碰见了一些粗鲁人，他们用各种名称叫我。
immigrant  adj. 移民的；迁入的...illegal immigrants.…非法移民。
immune  adj. 免疫的；免于……的，免除的About 93 percent of U.S. residents are immune to measles either because they were vaccinated or they had the disease as a child.大约93%的美国居民对麻疹是免疫的，他们要么因为接种过疫苗，要么就是小时候得过麻疹。Birds in outside cages develop immunity to airborne bacteria.养在户外笼子里的鸟对空气传播的病毒有免疫力。Higher education is no longer immune to state budget cuts.高等教育不再受州预算削减的影响。People with diplomatic passports are immune from criminal prosecution.持有外交护照者享有刑事起诉豁免权。The police are offering immunity to witnesses who help identify the murderers.警方对帮助他们指认杀人凶手的证人免予起诉。
imperative  adj. 必要的，不可避免的；紧急的；命令的，专横的；势在必行的；[语]祈使的It was imperative that he act as naturally as possible.至关重要的是他要尽可能地自然行事。The most important political imperative is to limit the number of U.S. casualties.政治上的当务之急是控制美国的伤亡人数。
impetus  n. 动力；促进；冲力The impetus for change came from lawyers.促进转变的动力来自于律师们。
implement  vt. 实施，执行；实现，使生效The government promised to implement a new system to control financial loan institutions.政府许诺要实施新的制度来控制金融贷款机构。Very little has been achieved in the implementation of the peace agreement signed last January.去年1月份签署的和平协议的执行几乎没有什么进展。...writing implements.…书写用具。
inaugurate  vt. 创新；开辟；开创；举行开幕典礼；举行就职典礼The new president will be inaugurated on January 20th.新总统将在1月20日正式就任。...the inauguration of the new Governor.…新任州长的就职典礼。A Mafia Museum was inaugurated in Corleone.一座黑手党博物馆在科莱奥内举行落成典礼。They later attended the inauguration of the University.他们后来参加了该大学的成立典礼。Pan Am inaugurated the first scheduled international flight.泛美航空开创了第一个定期的国际航班。
incline  vi. 倾斜；倾向；易于He came to a halt at the edge of a steep incline.他停步在一个陡坡的边上。Jack inclined his head very slightly.杰克微微点了点头。...the factors that incline us toward particular beliefs.…使我们倾向于特定信念的种种因素。Those who fail incline to blame the world for their failure.那些失败者往往会将其失败归咎于社会。
incur  vt. 招致，引发；蒙受The government had also incurred huge debts.政府也已承受了大笔债务。
independent  adj. 独立的；单独的；无党派的；不受约束的Your questions should be independent of each other.你们的问题应该是相互间毫无关联的。We're going independent from the university and setting up our own group.我们将从大学独立出去，成立我们自己的集团。...several people working independently in different areas of the world.…在世界不同地区独立工作的几个人。Phil was now much more independent of his parents.菲尔现在不大依赖他的父母了。...helping disabled students to live and study as independently as possible.…帮助残疾学生尽可能不依赖地生活和学习。Papua New Guinea became independent from Australia in 1975.巴布亚新几内亚1975年脱离澳大利亚而独立。...an independent television station.…一家独立的电视台。There were calls in Congress for an independent inquiry.国会中有对一次独立调查的呼吁。There's been a late surge of support for an independent candidate.对一位独立候选人的支持最近有骤然的增多。Mr. Vassiliou, standing as an independent, succeeded in convincing a significant number of voters of his argument.瓦西里欧先生以无党派人士身份成功地说服了大量选民支持他的观点。
indirect  adj. 间接的；迂回的；非直截了当的Businesses are feeling the indirect effects from the recession that's going on elsewhere.企业正感受到其他地区经济不景气造成的间接影响。Drugs are indirectly responsible for the violence.毒品间接对暴力负有责任。He took an indirect route back home.他选择了一条迂回的路线回家。His remarks amounted to an indirect appeal for economic aid.他的话等于是一个对经济援助拐弯抹角的请求。He referred indirectly to the territorial dispute.他拐弯抹角地提到了领土争端。
infinite  adj. 无限的，无穷的；无数的；极大的...an infinite variety of landscapes.…极其多样的地形地貌。With infinite care, John shifted position.约翰小心翼翼地换了位置。His design was infinitely better than anything I could have done.他的设计比我所能设计的不知要好上多少倍。...an infinite number of atoms.…无数个原子。A centimetre can be infinitely divided into smaller units.一厘米能被无穷尽地分为更小的单位。
inflation  n. 膨胀；通货膨胀；夸张；自命不凡...rising unemployment and high inflation.…上涨的失业率和高通胀。
infringe  vt. 侵犯；违反；破坏The film exploited his image and infringed his copyright.该影片利用了他的肖像，侵犯了他的肖像权。They rob us, they infringe our rights, they kill us.他们劫掠我们，他们侵犯我们的权利，他们屠杀我们。
inhabit  vt. 栖息；居住于；占据The valley is inhabited by the Dani tribe.这个山谷里居住着丹尼部落。...the people who inhabit these islands.…居住于这些岛屿的人们。
inherent  adj. 固有的；内在的；与生俱来的，遗传的Stress is an inherent part of dieting.要节食必定会经受压力。Man is not inherently violent.人类并非生来就暴力。
inherit  vt. 继承；遗传而得He has no son to inherit his land.他没有儿子来继承他的土地。The Endara government inherited an impossibly difficult situation from its predecessors.恩达拉政府从其前任手里接过了一个极为困难的局面。We inherit from our parents many of our physical characteristics.我们从父母的遗传中得到许多体貌特征。Her children have inherited her love of sports.她的孩子们从她那里继承了对体育运动的爱好。
inhibit  vt. 抑制；禁止The high cost of borrowing is inhibiting investment by industry in new equipment.高昂的借贷成本正抑制行业对新设备的投资。Officers will be inhibited from doing their duty.官员们将被阻止履行其职责。
initiative  n. 主动权；首创精神；新方案；倡议Local initiatives to help young people have been inadequate.当地对年轻人的扶助法案一直不够完善。We have the initiative; we intend to keep it.我们拥有主动权；我们想要保持主动权。She was disappointed by his lack of initiative.她对他缺乏主动性感到失望。If they reject or ignore the initiative, the public will vote on it in November.如果他们拒绝或无视公民立法提案程序，公众将于11月对它进行投票表决。We are the only power willing to take the initiative in the long struggle to end the war.在旨在结束战争的长期斗争中，我们是惟一愿意首先采取行动的国家。
instal  vt. 安装；使就任；设置
instance  n. 实例；情况；建议In sub-Saharan Africa today, for instance, gross investment accounts for roughly 15% of national income.例如，在如今的撒哈拉以南的非洲国家，总投资大约占国民收入的15％。...an investigation into a serious instance of corruption.…对一例严重腐败事件的调查。In the first instance your child will be seen by an ear, nose and throat specialist.你的孩子首先要由耳鼻喉专家诊查。
insurance  n. 保险；保险费；保险契约；赔偿金The house was a total loss and the insurance company promptly paid us the policy limit.房屋被定为全损，保险公司按保险限额迅速赔付了我们。Attentive proofreading is the only insurance against the kind of omissions described in this section.仔细校对是避免本节提到的那种遗漏问题的惟一预防措施。
intelligent  adj. 智能的；聪明的；理解力强的Susan's a very bright and intelligent woman who knows her own mind.苏珊是一个非常聪明伶俐而且清楚自己想法的女人。They are incapable of thinking intelligently about politics.他们在考虑政治问题时缺乏头脑。Intelligent computers will soon be an indispensable diagnostic tool for every doctor.智能计算机很快将会成为每位医生必不可少的诊断工具。
intensive  adj. 加强的；集中的；透彻的；加强语气的...after several days and nights of intensive negotiations.…在几个日夜的集中谈判之后。Caitlin's parents opted to educate her intensively at home.凯特林的父母选择在家对她进行强化教育。...intensive methods of rearing poultry.…集约饲养家禽的方法。Will they farm the rest of their land less intensively?他们会在耕种其余土地时不这么集约吗？
intent  n. 意图；目的；含义The rebels are obviously intent on keeping up the pressure.反叛分子显然决心继续施加压力。She looked from one intent face to another.她看着一张张专注的面孔。He listened intently, then slammed down the phone.他专注地听着，然后猛地把电话放下。The timing of this strong statement of intent on arms control is crucial.发表这项意图实施军备控制的强硬声明的时机至关重要。To all intents and purposes he was my father.他实际上可以称得上是我的父亲。
intermittent  adj. 间歇的；断断续续的；间歇性After three hours of intermittent rain, the game was abandoned.雨断断续续地下了3个小时之后，比赛被取消了。The talks went on intermittently for three years.会谈断断续续地进行了3年。
intervene  vi. 干涉；调停；插入The situation calmed down when police intervened.警察干预后，局势平静了下来。Hernandez intervened and told me to stop it.贺尔南德兹插话，不让我再说下去。The mailboat arrived on Friday mornings unless bad weather intervened.除非受到恶劣天气的干扰，邮船于星期五上午到达。
intricate  adj. 复杂的；错综的，缠结的...the production of carpets with highly intricate patterns.…图案复杂精细的地毯的制作。...intricately carved sculptures.…一些精雕细刻的雕塑。
intrigue  n. 阴谋；诡计；复杂的事；私通...political intrigue.…政治阴谋。The novelty of the situation intrigued him.那种新奇的情景激起了他的好奇心。
pathetic  adj. 可怜的，悲哀的；感伤的；乏味的...a pathetic little dog with a curly tail.…一只可怜的卷尾小狗。The small group of onlookers presented a pathetic sight.那一小群旁观者显出一幅可怜的样子。She was pathetically thin.她那时瘦弱得可怜。What pathetic excuses.多么无力的借口！Don't be so pathetic.别那么差劲。Five women in a group of 18 people is a pathetically small number.18个人中5位女性是个小得可怜的数目。
patrol  n. 巡逻；巡逻队；侦察队Prison officers continued to patrol the grounds within the jail.狱警们继续在监狱内的场地里巡逻。He failed to return from a patrol.他没能从一次巡逻中回来。The army is now on patrol in Srinagar and a curfew has been imposed.军队现在在斯利那加巡逻，宵禁也已实行。Guerrillas attacked a patrol with hand grenades.游击队用手榴弹袭击了一支巡逻队。
penalty  n. 罚款，罚金；处罚One of those arrested could face the death penalty.那些被捕之人其中的一个可能会面临死刑。Referee Michael Reed had no hesitation in awarding a penalty.裁判迈克尔·里德毫不犹豫地判了罚球。Why should I pay the penalty for somebody else's mistake?我为什么要为别人的错误而接受惩罚呢？
penetrate  vt. 渗透；穿透；洞察X-rays can penetrate many objects.X射线能穿透很多物体。The thick walls prevented penetration by debris from the hurricane.一堵堵厚墙阻挡了飓风带来的碎片的穿透。...the continuing failure of women to penetrate the higher levels of engineering.…女性跻身工程业较高层级的连续失败。The CIA had requested our help to penetrate a drug ring operating out of Munich.中情局曾要求我们协助打入在慕尼黑外活动的一个贩毒团伙。...the successful penetration by the KGB of the French intelligence service.…克格勃向法国情报机构的成功渗入。There have been around 15 attempts from outside Idaho to penetrate the market.已有约十五次从爱达荷州以外打入该市场的企图。...import penetration across a broad range of heavy industries.…横跨广泛重工业领域的进口渗入。
persist  vi. 存留，坚持；持续，固执Contact your doctor if the cough persists.如果持续咳嗽，就与医生联系。Why do people persist in begging for money in the street?为什么人们非要在街上讨钱呢？He urged the United States to persist with its efforts to bring about peace.他敦促美国坚持努力实现和平。
perspective  n. 观点；远景；透视图He says the death of his father 18 months ago has given him a new perspective on life.他说１８个月前他父亲的去世使他对人生产生了新的看法。...two different perspectives on the nature of adolescent development.…关于青春期发育特点的两种不同观点。Remember to keep things in perspective.记住要正确地看待事物。I let things get out of perspective.我没能正确地看待事物。
petition  n. 请愿；请愿书；祈求；[法] 诉状People feel so strongly that we recently presented the government with a petition signed by 4,500 people.人们感受如此强烈，以至我们最近向政府提交了一份由4500人签名的请愿书。His lawyers filed a petition for all charges to be dropped.他的律师们提出申请要求撤销所有指控。...couples petitioning for divorce.…申请离婚的几对夫妇。All the attempts to petition Congress had failed.所有向国会提出请求的努力都已失败了。
pierce  vt. 刺穿；洞察；响彻；深深地打动One bullet pierced the left side of his chest.一颗子弹射入了他的左胸。I'm having my ears pierced on Saturday.我星期六要去扎耳洞。...health risks from needles used in piercing and tattooing.…穿孔和纹身中使用针而带来的健康风险。...barefoot girls with braids and piercings.…梳着辫子、扎有耳洞的赤脚姑娘们。
pirate  n. 海盗；盗版；侵犯专利权者In the nineteenth century, pirates roamed the seas.19世纪，海盗很猖獗。Computer crimes include data theft and pirating software.计算机犯罪包括数据窃取和盗版软件。New technology makes it possible to make pirated copies of music and movies.新技术使制作盗版音乐和影片成为可能。Pirate copies of the DVD are already being sold.该DVD的盗版已经有售了。
polish  n. 磨光，擦亮；擦亮剂；优雅，精良The still air smelled faintly of furniture polish.久未流通的空气中有股淡淡的家具漆的气味。Each morning he shaved and polished his shoes.每天早晨他都刮胡子、擦皮鞋。He gave his counter a polish with a soft duster.他用柔软的抹布将柜台擦得亮亮的。...a highly polished floor.…一块擦得很亮的地板。The opera lacks the polish of his later work.这部歌剧缺少他后期作品中所具有的上乘境界。They just need to polish their technique.他们只需要改进一下自己的技艺。Polish up your writing skills on a one-week professional course.上一周的专业课程来增强你的写作技能。
poll  n. 投票；民意测验；投票数；投票所Polls show that the European treaty has gained support in Denmark.民意测验显示，欧洲条约已经在丹麦获得支持。We are doing a weekly poll on the president, and clearly his popularity has declined.我们正在对总统进行每周一次的民意测验，很显然他的受欢迎度已经下降了。More than 18,000 people were polled.18000多人接受了民意测验。Audiences were going to be polled on which of three pieces of contemporary music they liked best.听众将就3首现代乐曲中最喜欢哪一首接受民意调查。Incumbent officeholders are difficult to defeat at the polls.现任官员很难在选举中被击败。Voters are due to go to the polls on Sunday to elect a new president.选民们按计划将于周日前往投票站选举新总统。The result showed he had polled enough votes to force a second ballot.结果显示他获得了足够的选票来促使第二轮选举。
portray  vt. 描绘；扮演In 1975 he portrayed the king in a Los Angeles revival of "Camelot."1975年他在洛杉矶重演的戏剧《卡米洛特》中扮演国王。The film portrays a culture of young people who live in lower Manhattan.这部电影描绘了在下曼哈顿地区生活的青年人文化。...complaints about the way women are portrayed in ads.…不满于广告中对妇女的刻画方式。
postpone  vt. 使…延期；把…放在次要地位；把…放在后面He decided to postpone the expedition until the following day.他决定将探险活动推迟到第二天。
preach  vt. 说教；讲道；鼓吹；传道；反复灌输At High Mass the priest preached a sermon on the devil.在大弥撒仪式上，牧师布了一次有关魔鬼的道。The bishop preached to a crowd of several hundred local people.主教向一群几百名当地人布道。He said he was trying to preach peace and tolerance to his people.他说他正试图向他的人民宣扬和平与宽容。Health experts are now preaching that even a little exercise is far better than none at all.如今，健康专家宣扬说，即使少量的运动也比一点不运动要好得多。"Don't preach at me," he shouted.“不要对我说教，”他喊道。
precaution  n. 预防，警惕；预防措施Could he not, just as a precaution, move to a place of safety?难道他不能就当是一种防范搬到一个安全的地方去吗？
predecessor  n. 前任，前辈He maintained that he learned everything he knew from his predecessor.他坚称他所知道的一切都是从他的前任那儿学到的。Although the car is some 2 inches shorter than its predecessor, its boot is 20 percent larger.尽管这款汽车比其上一代产品短2英寸，但它的行李箱大了20%。
pregnant  adj. 怀孕的；富有意义的Lena got pregnant and married.莉娜怀了孕并结了婚。There was a long, pregnant silence, which Mrs. Madrigal punctuated by reaching for the cheque.马德里加尔太太伸手去拿那支票，打破了那一阵长时间的、耐人寻味的沉默。
prejudice  n. 偏见；侵害There was a deep-rooted racial prejudice long before the two countries went to war.早在两国交战之前就有了根深蒂固的种族偏见。There is widespread prejudice against workers over 45.对年龄超过45岁的工人有普遍的偏见。I think your upbringing has prejudiced you.我认为你的教养使你抱有偏见。The report was held back for fear of prejudicing his trial.因为担心会使他的审判带有偏见，该报告没有公开。Her study was not in any way intended to prejudice the future development of the college.她的研究绝对无意损害该学院的未来发展。
prescribe  vi. 规定；开药方The physician examines the patient then diagnoses the disease and prescribes medication.内科医生检查了病人，然后对疾病作出诊断，并开出药方。She took twice the prescribed dose of sleeping tablets.她服用了所开剂量两倍的安眠药。...article II of the constitution, which prescribes the method of electing a president.…规定总统选举办法的宪法第二条。
preside  vi. 主持，担任会议主席The PM returned to Downing Street to preside over a meeting of his inner cabinet.首相回到唐宁街去主持一场核心内阁会议。
presume  vt. 假定；推测；擅自；意味着I presume you're here on business.我想你是来这儿出差的吧。"Had he been home all week?"—"I presume so."“他整个星期都在家吗？”—“我想是。”They're resentful that outsiders presume to meddle in their affairs.他们对外人擅自干预他们的事务怨恨不已。The legal definition of "know" often presumes mental control.“知情”的法律界定通常以思维控制力为前提。
pretend  vi. 假装，伪装，佯装I pretend that things are really okay when they're not.我在情况不好的时候假装一切真地没事。Sometimes the boy pretended to be asleep.有时候那个男孩子假装睡着了。She can sunbathe and pretend she's in Cancun.她会进行日光浴并假装她是在坎昆。We do not pretend that the past six years have been without problems for us.我们不假称过去的6年对我们来讲是没有问题的。
preview  n. 预览；试映；事先查看He had gone to see the preview of a play.他去看过一出戏的预演。
previous  adj. 以前的；早先的；过早的She has a teenage daughter from a previous marriage.她有个出自前一次婚姻的十几岁的女儿。It was a surprisingly dry day after the rain of the previous week.这是继前一周的降雨之后出奇干燥的一天。
primitive  adj. 原始的，远古的；简单的，粗糙的...studies of primitive societies.…对原始社会的研究。...primitive whales.…原始鲸。Primitive humans needed to be able to react like this to escape from dangerous animals.原始人们需要能够像这样反应以逃脱危险的动物。The conditions are primitive by any standards.这些条件以任何标准衡量都是简陋的。
principal  adj. 主要的；资本的The principal reason for my change of mind is this.我改变主意的最重要原因就是这个。...the country's principal source of foreign exchange earnings.…该国最重要的外汇交易收入来源。Donald King is the principal of Dartmouth High School.唐纳德·金是达特茅斯中学的校长。
probability  n. 可能性；机率；[数] 或然率Without a transfusion, the victim's probability of dying was 100%.不输血的话，该患者的死亡概率是100%。The probabilities of crime or victimization are higher with some situations than with others.犯罪或实施伤害的概率在有些情况下比其他情况下要大一些。If you've owned property for several years, the probability is that values have increased.如果你已拥有财产几年了，很可能价值已经增涨了。Formal talks are still said to be a possibility, not a probability.正式谈判据说仍有可能，但不是很可能。The Republicans had better get used to the fact that in all probability, they are going to lose.共和党人最好习惯他们很可能会失败的事实。
probe  n. 探针；调查The more they probed into his background, the more inflamed their suspicions would become.他们越深入调查他的背景，对他的怀疑就会越强烈。For three years, I have probed for understanding.3年来我一直在寻求理解。...a federal grand-jury probe into corruption within the FDA.…联邦大陪审团对食品及药品管理局内部腐败的一次调查。The surgeon would pick up his instruments, probe, repair, and stitch up again.外科医生会拿起器械进行探查、修复，然后再缝合。Dr. Amid probed around the sensitive area.阿米德医生在敏感部位周围做了探查。...a fibre-optic probe.…一根光纤探针。A flashlight beam probed the underbrush only yards away from their hiding place.一束手电光搜索了离他们藏身之处仅几码远的低矮灌丛。
proceed  vi. 开始；继续进行；发生；行进He proceeded to tell me of my birth.他接着给我讲了我的出生。The group proceeded with a march they knew would lead to bloodshed.这群人继续进行他们知道会导致流血事件的一次游行。The ideas were not new. Their development had proceeded steadily since the war.这些想法并不新。它们的发展自开战以来一直在稳步地继续。The proceeds of the concert went to charity.音乐会的收入给了慈善机构。
prominent  adj. 突出的，显著的；杰出的；卓越的...the children of very prominent or successful parents.…非常知名或成功的人士们的孩子们。Here the window plays a prominent part in the design.这里，窗户在设计中有着突出的作用。Trade will figure prominently in the second day of talks in Washington.贸易在华盛顿会谈的第二天将成为突出的议题。
promising  adj. 有希望的，有前途的A school has honoured one of its brightest and most promising former students.一所学校给其培养过的最聪明、最有前途的学生中的一位颁了奖。
prone  adj. 俯卧的；有…倾向的，易于…的For all her experience as a television reporter, she was still prone to camera nerves.尽管有丰富的做电视记者的经验，她仍然倾向于在镜头前紧张。...the most injury-prone rider on the circuit.…赛车道上最容易受伤的车手。Bob slid from his chair and lay prone on the floor.鲍勃从椅子上滑下来，面朝下躺在了地板上。
proportion  n. 比例，占比；部分；面积；均衡A large proportion of the dolphins in that area will eventually die.那个地区的很大一部分海豚最终都会死去。The proportion of women in the profession had risen to 17.3%.从事那个职业的女性比例已经增长到17.3%。Women's bodies tend to have a higher proportion of fat to water.女性体内往往有更高的脂肪与水的比值。In the tropics plants grow to huge proportions.在热带，植物长得很高大。The pressure in the cylinders would go up in proportion to the boiler pressure.汽缸内的压力会与锅炉的压力成比例上升。Children tend to have relatively larger heads than adults in proportion to the rest of their body.与身体其余部位相比，孩子头部所占比例往往比成人大。The punishment was out of all proportion to the crime.惩罚和罪行完全不成比例。
propose  vt. 建议；打算，计划；求婚Hamilton proposed a change in the traditional debating format.汉密尔顿建议对传统的辩论形式作一个改变。It's still far from clear what action the government proposes to take over the affair.尚不清楚政府打算采取什么行动接手这件事。He has proposed a resolution limiting the role of U.S. troops.他提出了一项限制美军作用的决议。He proposed to his girlfriend over a public-address system.他在有线广播系统上向女友求婚。
protest  vi. 抗议；断言They were protesting soaring prices.他们在抗议不断飞涨的物价。The opposition now seems too weak to stage any serious protests against the government.反对党现在似乎太弱小，无力针对政府组织什么重大的抗议。The Mexican president cancelled a trip to Texas in protest at the state's execution of a Mexican national.墨西哥总统取消了得克萨斯之行，以抗议该州对一名墨西哥侨民的处决。When we tried to protest that Mo was beaten up they didn't believe us.当我们坚持说莫遭到了毒打时，他们都不相信。"I never said any of that to her," he protested.“我从来没有对她说过那种话，”他断然否认。
provided  conj. 假如；倘若The other banks are going to be very eager to help, provided that they see that he has a specific plan.如果他有一个具体的计划，其他的银行才会非常渴望提供资助。
provocative  adj. 刺激的，挑拨的；气人的He has made a string of outspoken and sometimes provocative speeches in recent years.他最近几年做了一系列直言不讳的、有时带有挑衅的演说。Some adolescents might be more sexually mature and provocative than others.有些青少年可能比其他人在性方面是更成熟、更挑逗的。
proximity  n. 接近，[数]邻近；接近；接近度，距离；亲近Part of the attraction is Darwin's proximity to Asia.达尔文港的部分吸引力在于她与亚洲比邻。He became aware of the proximity of the Afghans.他开始意识到那些阿富汗人的接近。
publication  n. 出版；出版物；发表The guide is being translated into several languages for publication near Christmas.这本指南正被翻译成好几种语言，准备在圣诞节前后出版。They have started legal proceedings against two publications which spoke of an affair.他们已开始对提及一件绯闻的两本出版物进行法律诉讼。A spokesman said: "We have no comment regarding the publication of these photographs."一位发言人说: “关于这些照片的公开，我们无可奉告。”
publicity  n. 宣传，宣扬；公开；广告；注意Much advance publicity was given to the talks.会谈之前做了大量的宣传。...government publicity campaigns.…政府的宣传活动。The case has generated enormous publicity in Brazil.这起犯罪事件已在巴西引起了公众的极大关注。
punctual  adj. 准时的，守时的；精确的He's always very punctual. I'll see if he's here yet.他一向很准时。我要看看他是不是已经来了。My guest arrived punctually.我的客人准时到了。
quench  vt. 熄灭，[机] 淬火；解渴；结束；冷浸He stopped to quench his thirst at a stream.他停在一条小溪边喝水解渴。
raid  n. 袭击；突袭；搜捕；抢劫The guerrillas raided banks and destroyed a police barracks and an electricity substation.游击队员们突袭了多家银行，摧毁了一个警察营房和一座变电站。The rebels attempted a surprise raid on a military camp.反叛者们曾经试图对兵营发动一场突然袭击。Police raided their headquarters and other offices.警察突击搜查了他们的总部和其他办公场所。They were arrested early this morning after a raid on a house by thirty armed police.他们于今天凌晨，在30名武装警察突击搜查了一所住宅后被捕。
random  adj. [数] 随机的；任意的；胡乱的The survey used a random sample of two thousand people across the Midwest.这项调查使用的是对中西部地区2000人的随机取样。...interviews with a randomly selected sample of 30 girls aged between 13 and 18.…对随机抽取的30名年龄在13至18岁之间的女孩的访谈。...random violence against innocent victims.…对无辜受害者的随意攻击。...drinks and magazines left scattered randomly around.…随意四处散落的饮料和杂志。We received several answers, and we picked one at random.我们收到了好几个答案，就随机地拣选了一个。Three African-Americans were killed by shots fired at random from a minibus.3名非洲裔美国人被从一辆小型公共汽车中胡乱射出的子弹打死了。
ratio  n. 比率，比例The adult to child ratio is one to six.成人与儿童之比是1比6。
rational  adj. 合理的；理性的He's asking you to look at both sides of the case and come to a rational decision.他是在要求你看到问题的两面，然后做出理性的决定。It can be very hard to think rationally when you're feeling so vulnerable and alone.在你感到如此脆弱和孤单的时候很难理性地思考问题。Did he come across as a sane, rational person?他看上去是不是一个头脑清醒而理智的人？
rebel  vi. 反叛；反抗；造反...fighting between rebels and government forces.…叛军与政府军之间的战斗。The rebels want another 1% cut in interest rates.反对派希望能再降低1%的利率。Voters rebelled against high property taxes.投票者们反对高额财产税。She had been a rebel at school.她在学校时就是个叛逆者。The child who rebels is unlikely to be overlooked.叛逆的孩子不太可能被忽视。
rebound  n. 回弹；篮板球His shot in the 21st minute of the game rebounded from a post.他在比赛21分钟时的射门从球门柱上弹了回来。Mia realized her trick had rebounded on her.米娅意识到她的伎俩反而害了自己。
recession  n. 衰退；不景气；后退；凹处The oil price increases sent Europe into deep recession.石油价格的上涨使欧洲陷入严重的经济衰退。
reciprocal  adj. 互惠的；相互的；倒数的，彼此相反的They expected a reciprocal gesture before more hostages could be freed.他们期望在更多的人质被释放之前有互惠的表示。
reckon  vt. 测算，估计；认为；计算Toni reckoned that it must be about three o'clock.托尼想一定是3点钟左右了。The market is reckoned to be worth $1.4 bn in the U.S. alone.这个市场仅在美国的价值估计就有14亿美元。
reclaim  vt. 开拓；回收再利用；改造某人，使某人悔改In 1986, they got the right to reclaim South African citizenship.1986年，他们得到了恢复南非公民身份的权利。The good news for the industry was that investors don't seem to be in any hurry to reclaim their money.对该行业来说，好消息是投资者们似乎不急于要求收回他们的钱。The Netherlands has been reclaiming farmland from water.荷兰一直在围海造田。The diamond towns are gradually being reclaimed by the desert.那些开采钻石的小镇逐渐被沙漠重新吞噬了。
recruit  n. 招聘；新兵；新成员The police are trying to recruit more black and Hispanic officers.警方正试图招收更多的黑人和西班牙裔的警官。She set up her stand to recruit students to the Anarchist Association.她搭了一个摊位招募学生加入无政府主义者协会。A bomb exploded at an army recruiting office.一枚炸弹在一个征兵办公室爆炸了。...a new recruit to the LA Police Department.…洛杉矶警察局的一名新警员。
recur  vi. 复发；重现；采用；再来；循环；递归...a theme that was to recur frequently in his work.…一个将在他的作品中多次出现的主题。
reel  vi. 卷；眩晕；蹒跚地走；退缩...a 30-metre reel of cable.…一卷30米长的电缆。He was reeling a little. He must be very drunk.他有点踉跄。他一定醉得很厉害。I'm still reeling from the shock of hearing about it.我现在仍然因为听到这个消息而震惊不已。His mind reeled at the question.他的脑子被这个问题搅混了。
referee  n. 裁判员；调解人；介绍人Vautrot has refereed in two World Cups.沃特罗特已经在两届世界杯比赛中担任过裁判。
reform  n. 改革，改良；改正The party embarked on a programme of economic reform.这个政党开始了一个经济改革的计划。...his plans to reform the country's economy.…他改革国家经济的计划。When his court case was coming up, James promised to reform.当他的案件即将被审理时，詹姆斯承诺要改过自新。...a reformed alcoholic.…一个改过自新的酗酒者。
refugee  n. 难民，避难者；流亡者，逃亡者A political refugee from Cameroon has moved into our neighbourhood.一个喀麦隆的政治难民已经搬进了我们小区。
refund  vi. 退还；偿还，归还Face it – you'll just have to take those cowboy boots back and ask for a refund.面对现实吧–你不过是要把那些牛仔靴拿回去，要求退款。We guarantee to refund your money if you're not delighted with your purchase.如果你对购买的商品不满意，我们保证退款。
reign  vi. 统治；支配；盛行；君临Last night confusion reigned about how the debate, which continues today, would end.昨晚，这场在今天继续进行的辩论将如何结束的问题令人困惑。...Henry II, who reigned from 1154 to 1189.…1154年至1189年在位统治的亨利二世。...Queen Victoria's reign.…维多利亚女王的统治时期。
reinforce  vt. 加强，加固；强化；补充I hope this will reinforce Indonesian determination to deal with this kind of threat.我希望这会加强印度尼西亚对付这类威胁的决心。The delegation hopes to reinforce the idea that human rights are not purely internal matters.代表团希望巩固人权不完全是国家内政的观念。Eventually, they had to reinforce the walls with exterior beams.最后，他们不得不用外梁来加固那些墙壁。Both sides have been reinforcing their positions after yesterday's fierce fighting.在昨天的激战后，双方一直在增援各自的阵地。
relay  vi. 转播；接替Britain's prospects of beating the United States in the relay looked poor.英国队在接力赛中战胜美国队的希望看上去不大。The satellite will be used mainly to relay television programmes.这颗卫星将主要用来转播电视节目。She relayed the message, then frowned.她转告了那个消息，然后皱了皱眉。
reliance  n. 信赖；信心；受信赖的人或物...the country's increasing reliance on foreign aid.…这个国家日益依赖外来援助。
render  vt. 致使；提出；实施；着色；以…回报It contained so many errors as to render it worthless.太多的错误使之变得毫无价值。
resemble  vt. 类似，像Some of the commercially produced venison resembles beef in flavour.一些商业化生产的鹿肉味道像牛肉。
resign  vt. 辞职；放弃；委托；使听从A hospital administrator has resigned over claims he lied to get the job.一位医院主管因为有人声称他的职位是骗来的而辞职了。Mr Robb resigned his position last month.罗布先生上个月辞去了他的职位。Pat and I resigned ourselves to yet another summer without a boat.帕特和我将就着又过了一个没有船的夏天。
respectable  adj. 值得尊敬的；人格高尚的；相当数量的He came from a perfectly respectable middle-class family.他来自一个非常体面的中产阶级家庭。If she divorced Tony, she would lose the respectability she had as Mrs. Tony Tatterton.如果她和托尼离婚，她将会失去作为托尼•塔特顿太太的体面。...investments that offer respectable and highly attractive rates of return.…提供不错的、极具吸引力的回报率的投资。
restore  vt. 恢复；修复；归还The army has recently been brought in to restore order.该军队最近被调来恢复秩序。His visit is expected to lead to the restoration of diplomatic relations.他的访问预计会导致外交关系的恢复。We will restore her to health but it may take time.我们会让她恢复健康，但这或许需要时间。I owe the restoration of my hearing to this remarkable new technique.我把我听力的复原归功于这项非凡的新技术。...experts who specialize in examining and restoring ancient parchments.…专门研究和修复古羊皮纸手稿的专家们。I specialized in the restoration of old houses.我擅长旧房的修复。The following day their horses and goods were restored to them.第二天他们的马匹和货物被归还给了他们。
restrain  vt. 抑制，控制；约束；制止Wally gripped my arm, partly to restrain me and partly to reassure me.沃利抓住了我的胳膊，部分是想制止我，部分是想安慰我。She was unable to restrain her desperate anger.她无法抑制她那不顾一切的愤怒。The radical 500-day plan was very clear on how it intended to try to restrain inflation.这项激进的500天计划在其想要如何试图限制通货膨胀上是非常清晰的。
resume  n. 摘要；[管理] 履历，简历After the war he resumed his duties at Wellesley College.那场战争之后，他恢复了在韦尔斯利学院的任职。It is premature to speculate about the resumption of negotiations.考虑谈判的恢复还太早。"I changed my mind," Blanche said, resuming her seat.“我改主意了，”布兰奇说，返回到她的座位上。

retort  n. 反驳，顶嘴；曲颈瓶"You can't smoke in here," Shaw said.—"Don't worry, it's not tobacco," he retorted.“你不能在这儿吸烟，”肖说道。—“别担心，这不是烟叶，”他反驳道。His sharp retort clearly made an impact.他的尖锐反驳显然起了作用。
retrospect  n. 回顾，追溯In retrospect, I wish that I had thought about alternative courses of action.回想起来，我真希望自己当初考虑过其他的行动方案。
revelation  n. 启示；揭露；出乎意料的事；被揭露的真相...the seemingly everlasting revelations about his private life.…有关他私生活的似乎永无休止的披露。...following the revelation of his affair with a former secretary.…在他和前任秘书的风流韵事被揭露之后。Degas's work had been a revelation to her.德各斯的工作曾是她的一大发现。
revenge  n. 报复；复仇The attackers were said to be taking revenge on the 14-year-old, claiming he was a school bully.攻击者被称是在报复一名14岁男孩，称他是学校一霸。The paper accused her of trying to revenge herself on her former lover.这家报纸指责她企图报复她以前的情人。

rival  n. 对手；竞争者The world champion finished more than two seconds ahead of his nearest rival.这位世界冠军领先离他最近的对手两秒多钟冲过终点。The area is famous for its wonderfully fragrant wine which has no rivals in the Rhone.这一地区以其极为醇香的葡萄酒而闻名，这种酒在罗纳河流域没有可匹敌者。Cassette recorders cannot rival the sound quality of CDs.盒式磁带录音机在音质上无法与CD相媲美。
roar  n. 咆哮；吼；轰鸣A police car roared past.一辆警车呼啸而过。The engine roared, and the vehicle leapt forward.引擎轰鸣，车子猛地向前驶去。...the roar of traffic.…车辆的轰鸣声。Max threw back his head and roared with laughter.马克斯把头向后一甩，哄然大笑。There were roars of laughter as he stood up.他站起来时出现阵阵哄堂大笑。"I'll kill you for that," he roared.“我要为此杀了你，” 他吼道。During the playing of the national anthem the crowd roared and whistled.奏国歌时，人群又吼又吹口哨。There was a roar of approval.响起了一片表示赞成的喊叫声。The lion roared once, and sprang.狮子吼了一声，跳了起来。...the roar of lions in the distance.…远处的狮吼声。
rot  n. 腐烂；腐败；腐坏If we don't unload it soon, the grain will start rotting in the silos.如果我们不马上卸货，这些粮食在仓中将开始腐烂。Investigations had revealed extensive rot in the beams under the ground floor.检测显示一楼下面的横梁已经有大面积的腐烂。In many schools, the rot is beginning to set in. Standards are falling all the time.在许多学校，情况正在逐步恶化，水准在不断降低。Most governments simply leave the long-term jobless to rot.大多数政府只能任由长期失业者颓废下去。
rupture  n. 破裂；决裂；疝气He died of an abdominal infection caused by a rupture of his stomach.他死于由一次胃穿孔引发的腹部感染。His stomach might rupture from all the acid.他的胃可能会因为所有这些酸而穿孔。While playing badminton, I ruptured my Achilles tendon.打羽毛球的时候，我把跟腱撕裂了。He ruptured himself playing football.他因踢足球而发了疝气。Certain petrol tanks in trucks can rupture and burn in a collision.卡车内的某些油箱会在一次碰撞中爆裂起火。The incidents have not yet caused a major rupture in the political ties between countries.这些事件尚未造成各国间政治联系的严重破裂。Brutal clashes between squatters and police yesterday ruptured the city's governing coalition.昨天私自占地者与警察的野蛮冲突使这座城市的执政联盟破裂。
sacrifice  n. 牺牲；祭品；供奉The priest sacrificed a chicken.牧师献祭了一只鸡。...animal sacrifices to the gods.…献给众神的动物祭品。She sacrificed family life to her career.她为了她的事业牺牲了家庭生活。Kitty Aldridge has sacrificed all for her first film.姬蒂•奥尔德里奇为了她的第一部电影牺牲了一切。She made many sacrifices to get Anita a good education.为了让安尼塔受到良好教育，她做出了很多牺牲。
saddle  n. 鞍，鞍状物；车座；拖具Why don't we saddle a couple of horses and go for a ride?为什么我们不给几匹马配上鞍骑着转转？I want to be gone from here as soon as we can saddle up.我想一配好鞍就离开这儿。
scarce  adj. 缺乏的，不足的；稀有的Food was scarce and expensive.食物匮乏而且昂贵。Jobs are becoming increasingly scarce.工作职位变得越来越少。It probably would be a good idea if you made yourself scarce.如果你溜走倒可能是个好主意。
scramble  vt. 攀登；使混杂，仓促凑成；扰乱Tourists were scrambling over the rocks looking for the perfect camera angle.旅行者们爬上岩石，寻找最完美的拍摄角度。Ann threw back the covers and scrambled out of bed.安掀开被子，急忙下了床。More than three million fans are expected to scramble for tickets.预计会有三百万以上的歌迷抢购门票。...the scramble for jobs.…工作的竞争。Make the toast and scramble the eggs.烤面包，炒鸡蛋。...scrambled eggs and bacon.…炒蛋和熏咸肉。The system lets you encrypt or scramble the data that's sent between machines.这个系统可以让你对机器间互发的数据作加密或扰频处理。

seal  n. 密封；印章；海豹；封条；标志He sealed the envelope and put on a stamp.他封好信封，贴了张邮票。Write your letter and seal it in a blank envelope.写好你的信，然后将其封入一个空信封。She filled the containers, sealed them with a cork, and stuck on labels.她装满那些容器，用塞子封了口，然后贴上了标签。A woman picks them up and seals them in plastic bags.一位女士拣起它们，然后把它们封入各塑料袋中。When assembling the pie, wet the edges where the two crusts join, to form a seal.捏合馅饼时，弄湿两块面皮封合的边缘，以形成一个封口。Check seals on fridges and freezers regularly.定期检查冰箱和冰柜的密封装置。The seal on the box broke when it fell from its hiding-place.盒子从隐藏处掉下时上面的封口破了。...a supply of note paper bearing the presidential seal.…一批盖有总统印章的便条纸。The soldiers were deployed to help paramilitary police seal the border.这些士兵们被调去协助准军事警察封锁边境。Police and troops sealed off the area after the attack.警察和军队在袭击发生后封锁了该地区。McLaren are close to sealing a deal with Renault.麦克拉伦即将和雷诺尔特达成一笔交易。A general election will be held which will seal his destiny one way or the other.一场将左右他命运的大选即将举行。

slide  n. 滑动；幻灯片；滑梯；雪崩She slid the door open.她把门滑开了。I slid the wallet into his pocket.我把那钱包滑进了他的口袋。He slid into the driver's seat.他悄悄地坐到了司机的座位上。She had slid into a depression.她不知不觉地抑郁寡欢起来。The dollar continued to slide.美元继续下跌。...the dangerous slide in oil prices.…石油价格危险的下跌。...a slide show.…幻灯片放映。...a drop of blood on a slide.…载物玻璃片上的一滴血。...two young children playing on a slide.…在玩滑梯的两个年幼的孩子。
smash  vt. 粉碎；使破产；溃裂Someone smashed a bottle.有人打碎了一个瓶子。A crowd of youths started smashing windows.一群年轻人开始打碎窗户。The demonstrators used trucks to smash through embassy gates.示威者们用卡车撞破大门闯进大使馆。The bottle smashed against a wall.那瓶子撞到了一面墙上。Their attempts to clean up politics and smash the power of party machines failed.他们整治政治和搞垮党派组织权力的企图失败了。
snatch  n. 抢夺；抓举；小量Mick snatched the cards from Archie's hand.米克一把夺过阿彻手里的牌。He snatched up the telephone.他一把抓起了电话。If your bag is snatched, let it go.如果你的包被抢走，就随它去吧。I snatched a glance at the mirror.我乘机瞥了一眼镜子。The American came from behind to snatch victory by a mere eight seconds.美国队后来居上，仅以8秒钟的优势赢得了胜利。I heard snatches of the conversation.我听到几段零星的谈话。
solo  n. 独奏；独唱；独奏曲He had just completed his final solo album.他刚刚完成他最后一张个人专辑。...Daniel Amokachi's spectacular solo goal.…丹尼尔•阿莫卡奇精彩的个人进球得分。Charles Lindbergh became the very first person to fly solo across the Atlantic.查尔斯•林白成为第一个单独飞越大西洋的人。The original version featured a guitar solo.原版以吉他独奏为特色。
sore  adj. 疼痛的，痛心的；剧烈的，极度的；恼火的，发怒的；厉害的，迫切的It's years since I've had a sore throat like I did last night.我已经好多年没有像昨晚那样嗓子痛了。The result is that they are now all feeling very sore at you.结果是他们现在都很生你的气。Our backs and hands were covered with sores and burns from the ropes.我们的背和手到处是绳索导致的伤口和灼伤。The continuing presence of American troops on Korean soil remains a very sore point with these students.美国军队继续驻留在韩国领土依然是令这些学生极其恼怒的事情。
sparkle  n. 闪耀；火花；活力The jewels on her fingers sparkled.她手指上的珠宝闪闪发光。His bright eyes sparkled.他明亮的双眼炯炯有神。...the sparkle of coloured glass.…彩色玻璃的闪光。...sparkles of light.…光的闪烁She sparkles, and has as much zest as a person half her age.她聪慧而有朝气，且有着与比她年龄小一半的人一样多的热情。There was little sparkle in their performance.他们的表演平庸而了无生气。He is sparkling and versatile in front of the camera.他在摄影机前聪颖机智、多才多艺。
spectrum  n. 光谱；频谱；范围；余象She'd seen his moods range across the emotional spectrum.她见过他在各种情感间的情绪变化。Politicians across the political spectrum have denounced the act.政界圈各派政客都谴责了这种行为。
spice  n. 香料；情趣；调味品；少许...herbs and spices.…各种香草和香料。They spiced their conversations and discussions with intrigue.他们通过设谜为他们的谈话和讨论增加乐趣。Her publisher wants her to spice up her stories with sex.她的出版商想要她用色情给她的故事增添趣味。
spite  n. 不顾；恶意；怨恨Josef Krips at the State Opera hired her in spite of the fact that she had never sung on stage.国家歌剧院的约瑟夫•克里普斯雇佣了她，尽管她从未在台上演唱过。The blunt comment made Richard laugh in spite of himself.那率直的评论使得理查德不由自主地笑了起来。I refused her a divorce, out of spite I suppose.我拒绝了她离婚的要求，我想是出于怨恨。Pantelaras was giving his art collection away for nothing, to spite Marie and her husband.潘特拉拉斯将他的艺术收藏品无偿赠送了，存心惹怒玛丽和她的丈夫。
split  vt. 分离；使分离；劈开；离开；分解In a severe gale the ship split in two.在一次强劲的大风中那艘船断成了两半。If the chicken is fairly small, you may simply split it in half.要是鸡不太大，你把它分成两半就行。Yet it is feared the Republican leadership could split over the agreement.然而人们担心共和党领导层可能会因该协议而出现分裂。The Kremlin is deeply split in its approach to foreign policy.克里姆林宫在对外政策的看法上严重分歧。They accused both radicals and conservatives of trying to provoke a split in the party.他们指责激进人士和保守人士都企图挑起党内分歧。...a split between what is thought and what is felt.…所想和所感之间的区别。The seat of his grey trousers split.他的那条灰色裤子的臀部裂开了。The plastic-covered seat has a few small splits around the corners.那个有塑料套的座位的角边周围有几处小裂缝。I would rather pay for a meal than watch nine friends pick over and split a bill.我宁愿付整顿饭钱而不愿看着9个朋友仔细算计、分摊账单。
spray  n. 喷雾，喷雾剂；喷雾器；水沫The moon was casting a rainbow through the spray from the waterfall.月亮在瀑布溅起的水雾中映出了一道彩虹。...hair spray.…头发喷剂A sprayer hooked to a tractor can spray five gallons onto ten acres.挂在拖拉机上的喷雾器用五加仑液量能喷洒十英亩地。Inmates threw bricks at prison officers who were spraying them with a hose.囚犯们朝那些用水管向他们喷水的狱警们抛掷砖头。A shower of mustard seeds sprayed into the air and fell into the grass.许多芥籽溅到空中，然后掉进草地里。The intensity of the blaze shattered windows, spraying glass on the streets below.熊熊烈焰烧碎了窗户，玻璃碎片飞溅到了下面的街道上。He ran to the top of the building, spraying bullets into shoppers below.他冲向楼顶，向下面的购物者扫射。The bare metal was sprayed with several coats of primer.裸露的金属被喷了几层底漆。He doesn't spray against pests or diseases.他没有喷农药来防治害虫或疾病。Confine the use of insecticides to the evening and do not spray plants that are in flower.只限晚间使用杀虫剂，并且不要对花期植物喷药。Farmers can use the spray to kill weeds without harming the soy crop.农民们能用喷雾器来除草而不伤大豆作物。
stale  adj. 陈腐的；不新鲜的Their daily diet consisted of a lump of stale bread, a bowl of rice, and stale water.他们的日常饮食包括一块不新鲜的面包、一碗米饭，还有不新鲜的水。...the smell of stale sweat.…汗臭味。Her relationship with Mark has become stale.她和马克的关系已变得乏味了。
stall  n. 货摊；畜栏；托辞The Social Democratic Party has vowed to try to stall the bill until the current session ends.该社会民主党已立誓设法暂停该议案直至当前会议结束。...but the peace process stalled.…但是和平进程暂停了。Thomas had spent all week stalling over his decision.托马斯花了整周的时间迟迟不做决定。The shop manager stalled the man until the police arrived.那个商场经理把那人拖住直到警察赶到。The engine stalled.发动机突然熄火了。...market stalls selling local fruits.…出售当地水果的市场摊位。With the balcony blocked off, patrons filled most of the stalls.楼厅包厢被封闭了，赞助人几乎坐满了舞台前方的座位。She went into the shower stall, turned on the water, and grabbed the soap.她走进淋浴间，打开水，抓起香皂。
staple  n. 主要产品；订书钉；主题；主食Rice is the staple food of more than half the world's population.大米是世界上半数以上人口的主食。The Chinese also eat a type of pasta as part of their staple diet.中国人也以一种面食作为他们的部分主食。Fish is a staple in the diet of many Africans.鱼是许多非洲人饮食中的主食。Political reporting has become a staple of American journalism.政治报道已经成为美国新闻业的一个重要内容。Staple some sheets of paper together into a book.用订书钉把一些纸张订成一本。

striking  adj. 显著的，突出的，惊人的；打击的；罢工的The most striking feature of those statistics is the high proportion of suicides.那些统计数据最显著的特征是高自杀率。He bears a striking resemblance to Lenin.他与列宁有着不同寻常的相似之处。In one respect, however, the men really were strikingly similar.然而，在一方面，这些男人的确惊人地相似。...a strikingly handsome man.…一个异乎寻常地英俊的男人。She was a striking woman with long blonde hair.她曾是一个留着金色长发的俊秀女子。

stroke  n. （游泳或划船的）划；中风；（打、击等的）一下；冲程；（成功的）举动；尝试；轻抚Carla, curled up on the sofa, was smoking a cigarette and stroking her cat.卡拉蜷曲在沙发上，抽着一支烟，轻抚着她的猫。He had a minor stroke in 1987, which left him partly paralysed.他在1987年患了轻度中风，这使他半身不遂了。Fill in gaps by using short, upward strokes of the pencil.用铅笔画出短的、向上的笔画来填空。I turned and swam a few strokes further out to sea.我转过身又向海里游了几下。She spent hours practising the breast stroke.她花了几个小时练习蛙泳。On the stroke of 12, fireworks suddenly exploded into the night.12点的钟声敲响时，焰火突然冲破了夜空。Compton was sending the ball here, there, and everywhere with each stroke.康普顿把球发到这儿，发到那儿，每一次击球都打到不同地方。It didn't rain, which turned out to be a stroke of luck.天没下雨，结果成为一次好运。At the time, his appointment seemed a stroke of genius.当时，他的任命似乎是天才之举。I never did a stroke of work in college.我在大学里从来不干一点儿活。
stubborn  adj. 顽固的；顽强的；难处理的He is a stubborn character used to getting his own way.他是一个固执的人，过去常常随心所欲。He stubbornly refused to tell her how he had come to be in such a state.他固执地拒绝告诉她自己是如何落到这种地步的。This treatment removes the most stubborn stains.这种处理去掉了最难以去除的污渍。Some interest rates have remained stubbornly high.一些利率仍然一直居高不下。
subordinate  n. 下属，下级；部属，属下Haig tended not to seek guidance from subordinates.黑格不想向下属们寻求指导。Sixty of his subordinate officers followed his example.他的60个下级官员都以他为榜样。It was an art in which words were subordinate to images.它是一种语言比图像次要的艺术。He was both willing and able to subordinate all else to this aim.他既愿意也能够让别的一切从属于这个目标。...the social subordination of women.…妇女们的社会从属地位。
subsequent  adj. 后来的，随后的...the increase of population in subsequent years.…随后几年中的人口增长。He subsequently worked on Boeing's 747, 767 and 737 jetliner programmes.他后来从事了波音747、767 和 737喷气式飞机的项目。
substitute  n. 代用品；代替者They were substituting violence for dialogue.他们那时在以暴力代替对话。He was substituting for the injured William Wales.他那时在代替受伤的威廉·威尔士。In my experience a straight substitution of carob for chocolate doesn't work.以我的经验，角豆直接代替巧克力不会奏效。She is seeking a substitute for the very man whose departure made her cry.他在寻找一个男人的替代者，这个男人的离去曾使她伤心落泪。The printed word is no substitute for personal discussion with a great thinker.印刷字无法替代与伟大思想家的当面交流。Jefferson entered as a substitute in the 60th minute.杰斐逊在第60分钟时作为替补队员上了场。
succession  n. 连续；继位；继承权；[生态] 演替Adams took a succession of jobs which have stood him in good stead.亚当斯做了一连串对他很有利的工作。She is now seventh in line of succession to the throne.她目前排在王位继任顺序的第7位。
sue  vt. 控告；请求Mr. Warren sued for libel over the remarks.沃伦先生对那些评论提起诽谤诉讼。The company could be sued for damages.该公司会因所造成的损失被起诉。
suicide  n. 自杀；自杀行为；自杀者She tried to commit suicide on several occasions.她曾几次试图进行自杀。...a case of attempted suicide.…一个自杀未遂的案子。
summon  vt. 召唤；召集；鼓起；振作Howe summoned a doctor and hurried over.豪叫了一位医生，匆忙赶过去了。Suddenly we were summoned to the interview room.突然我们被召唤进了面试室。It took her a full month to summon the courage to tell her mother.她用了整整一个月的时间才鼓起勇气告诉了母亲。Painfully shy, he finally summoned up courage to ask her to a game.尽管他非常腼腆，最终还是鼓起了勇气邀她去看一场比赛。

suspect  n. 嫌疑犯I suspect they were right.我觉得他们是正确的。The above complaints are, I suspect, just the tip of the iceberg.上述的这些抱怨，我觉得，不过是冰山的一角。He suspected that the woman staying in the flat above was using heroin.他怀疑住在楼上公寓里的那位女子在吸食海洛因。It was perfectly all right, he said, because the police had not suspected him of anything.一点儿没事，他说，因为警察对他没有任何怀疑。Police have arrested a suspect in a series of killings and sexual assaults in the city.警方逮捕了该城市一系列杀人强奸案件中的一名嫌疑犯。Delegates evacuated the building when a suspect package was found.一个可疑包裹被发现后，代表们撤离了这栋大楼。
