whirl  n. 旋转，回旋；昏乱；一连串的事；短暂的旅行Not receiving an answer, she whirled around.没有得到答复，她猛地转过身来。He was whirling Anne around the floor.他正与安妮旋转起舞。...the barely audible whirl of wheels.…几乎听不见的轮子转动声。In half an hour's whirl of activity she does it all.在半个小时马不停蹄的忙碌中，她做完了这一切。Why not give acupuncture a whirl?为什么不试试针灸？
withstand  vt. 抵挡；禁得起；反抗...armoured vehicles designed to withstand chemical attack.…设计来抵御化学攻击的装甲车。
wretched  adj. 可怜的；卑鄙的；令人苦恼或难受的Wretched woman, he thought, why the hell can't she wait?讨厌的女人，他想，她怎么就不能等等呢？I feel really confused and wretched.我真的感到迷惑和难过。
zone  n. 地带；地区；联防Many people have stayed behind in the potential war zone.许多人留在了可能交战的地带。The area has been declared a disaster zone.该地区已被宣布为灾难带。The land was not zoned for commercial purposes.这块地未被划为商业用地。...the use of zoning to preserve agricultural land.…使用分区制以保留农业用地。
abolish  vt. 废除，废止；取消，革除An Illinois House committee voted Thursday to abolish the death penalty.伊利诺伊州议院的一个委员会在星期四投票废除了死刑。
abrupt  adj. 生硬的；突然的；唐突的；陡峭的Rosie's idyllic world came to an abrupt end when her parents' marriage broke up.当她的父母婚姻破裂后，罗茜的田园诗一般的世界骤然结束了。He stopped abruptly and looked my way.他突然停住，向我看了过来。He was abrupt to the point of rudeness.他唐突到了无礼的地步。"Good night, then," she said abruptly.“那么，晚安”，她唐突地说道。
abuse  n. 滥用；虐待；辱骂；弊端；恶习，陋习...investigation of alleged child abuse.…对涉嫌虐待儿童的调查。...victims of sexual and physical abuse.…性虐待和肉体摧残的受害者们。I was left shouting abuse as the car sped off.当车加速离去时，我在那里破口大骂。What went on here was an abuse of power.这里发生的情况是职权的滥用。Janet had been abused by her father since she was eleven.詹妮特自从11岁起就被她的父亲虐待。...parents who feel they cannot cope or might abuse their children.…感到自己不能应付或可能虐待孩子的家长们。He alleged that he was verbally abused by other soldiers.他声称他被其他士兵们口头侮辱了。He showed how the rich and powerful can abuse their position.他揭露了有钱有势的人会如何滥用他们的地位。
accelerate  vt. 使……加快；使……增速Growth will accelerate to 2.9 percent next year.增长明年将加快到2.9%。Suddenly the car accelerated.突然车加速了。
accession  n. 增加；就职；到达...the anniversary of the king's accession to the throne.…国王继承王位周年纪念。
accessory  n. 配件；附件；[法] 从犯...an exclusive range of hand-made bedroom and bathroom accessories.…一个高档系列的手工制作的卧室及卫生间设备附件。It also has a good range of accessories, including sunglasses, handbags and belts.它还有多种配饰，包括墨镜、手包和皮带。She had been charged with being an accessory to the embezzlement of funds from a cooperative farm.她已被指控为挪用一个合作农场资金的一个从犯。
accord  n. 符合；一致；协议；自愿UNITA was legalized as a political party under the 1991 peace accords.根据1991年和平协议，安盟作为一个政党被合法化了。His predecessor was accorded an equally tumultuous welcome.他的前任受到了同样热烈的欢迎。On his return home, the government accorded him the rank of Colonel.在他回国时，该国政府授予他上校军衔。In many cases the disease will clear up of its own accord.在很多情况下这种疾病会自动地痊愈。He did not quit as France's prime minister of his own accord.他不是自愿地辞去法国总理一职的。
accountable  adj. 有责任的；有解释义务的；可解释的Public officials can finally be held accountable for their actions.政府官员最终是要对他们的行为负责任的。...a drive toward democracy and greater accountability.…一场促进民主和增强责任心的运动。
acquisition  n. 获得物，获得；收购...the acquisition of a profitable paper recycling company.对一家有利润的废纸回收公司的收购。How did you go about making this marvellous acquisition then?那么你是怎么着手进行这宗不可思议的购置的？...language acquisition.…语言习得。
actuality  n. 现状；现实；事实In actuality, Ted did not have a disorder but merely a difficult temperament.事实上，特德并没有什么异常而只是脾气不好。It exists in dreams rather than actuality.它于梦想而非实际中存在。
adhere  vi. 坚持；依附；粘着；追随All members of the association adhere to a strict code of practice.所有该协会的成员都遵守严格的业务守则。Small particles adhere to the seed.微小的粒子紧贴着种子。
adjoin  vi. 毗连，邻接The doctor's bedroom adjoined his wife's and the door between the rooms was always open.这位医生的卧室紧邻他妻子的卧室，两间房之间的门总是开着的。
admittance  n. 进入；入场权；通道We had not been able to gain admittance to the flat.我们还未能获得进入那所公寓的权利。
advantageous  adj. 有利的；有益的Free exchange of goods was advantageous to all.自由商品交易对大家都有利。
adventurous  adj. 爱冒险的；大胆的；充满危险的Warren was an adventurous businessman.沃伦是一位有冒险精神的商人。He had always wanted an adventurous life in the tropics.他一直都想要一种在热带丛林里的冒险生活。
aerial  adj. 空中的，航空的；空气的；空想的Weeks of aerial bombardment had destroyed factories and motorways.数周的空袭已经摧毁了各工厂和公路。Patterns that are invisible on the ground can be the most striking part of an aerial photograph.在地面上看不见的图案可能是空中照片中最为醒目的部分。
affirm  vt. 肯定；断言The court affirmed that the information can be made public under the Freedom of Information Act.法院公开肯定了此信息能依据《自由信息法案》公之于众。...a speech in which he affirmed a commitment to lower taxes.…在其中他公开肯定了减税承诺的一次演讲。The North Atlantic Treaty begins with the affirmation that its parties "reaffirm their faith in the purposes and principles of the Charter of the United Nations."《北大西洋公约》以公开肯定其成员“重申其对《联合国宪章》的目的以及原则的信念”开头。Everything I had accomplished seemed to affirm that opinion.我所做成的每件事似乎都证实了那个观点。The ruling was a welcome affirmation of the constitutional right to free speech.此裁决是对言论自由这一宪法权利的受人欢迎的肯定。
affix  vt. 粘上；署名；将罪责加之于
aggregate  vi. 集合；聚集；合计The rate of growth of GNP will depend upon the rate of growth of aggregate demand.国民生产总值的增长率将依赖于总需求的增长率。
airborne  adj. [航] 空运的；空气传播的；风媒的The pilot did manage to get airborne.这位飞行员的确使飞机升空了。The allies landed thousands of airborne troops.同盟国投下了成千上万的空降部队。Many people are allergic to airborne pollutants such as pollen.许多人对空气中花粉之类的污染物质过敏。
aisle  n. 通道，走道；侧廊...the frozen food aisle.…冷冻食品的货架通道。
allege  vt. 宣称，断言；提出…作为理由She alleged that there was rampant drug use among the male members of the group.她指称该组织中有大量的男性成员吸毒。The accused is alleged to have killed a man.该被告据称杀了一个男子。
alleviate  vt. 减轻，缓和Nowadays, a great deal can be done to alleviate back pain.如今，很多方法可以被用来减轻背部疼痛。Their energies were focused on the alleviation of the refugees' misery.他们把精力集中在了对难民苦难的减轻上。
alliance  n. 联盟，联合；联姻The two parties were still too much apart to form an alliance.这两个党派分歧大得还不能形成联盟。The Socialists' electoral strategy has been based on a tactical alliance with the Communists.社会党人的参选策略一直以和共产党人的战略性结盟为基础。
thermal  adj. 热的；热量的；保热的...thermal power stations.…热电站。Volcanic activity has created thermal springs and boiling mud pools.火山活动产生了温泉和沸腾的泥浆池。...thermal underwear.…保暖内衣My feet were like blocks of ice despite the thermal socks.我的双脚尽管穿着保暖袜，还是像冰块。Have you got your thermals on?你穿上保暖衣了吗？Birds use thermals to lift them through the air.鸟类利用上升的暖气流升空。
threshold  n. 入口；门槛；开始；极限；临界值He stopped at the threshold of the bedroom.他在卧室门口停了下来。Moss has a high threshold for pain and a history of fast healing.莫斯的忍痛力很强，而且有迅速愈合的经历。We are on the threshold of a new era in astronomy.我们将迈入天文学的新时代。
tick  vt. 标记号于；滴答地记录A wind-up clock ticked busily from the kitchen counter.一个上了发条的时钟在厨房案台上不停地嘀嗒作响。A grandfather clock ticked away in a corner.一个落地式大钟在墙角嘀嗒作响。...the endless ticking of clocks.…时钟没完没了的嘀嗒声。He sat listening to the tick of the grandfather clock.他坐着倾听那个落地式大钟的嘀嗒声。The company produces chemicals that destroy ticks and mites.该公司生产消灭壁虱和螨虫的化学品。To request your free gift, please tick the appropriate box below.需要免费礼品的，请在下面相关的框中打勾。
timely  adj. 及时的；适时的The recent outbreaks of cholera are a timely reminder that this disease is still a serious health hazard.最近几次爆发的霍乱是一个适时的提醒，该疾病依然是个严重的健康危害。
timid  adj. 胆小的；羞怯的A timid child, Isabella had learned obedience at an early age.伊莎贝拉是一个羞怯的孩子，很小的时候就已经学会了顺从。She doesn't ridicule my timidity.她不会嘲笑我的羞怯。
tone  n. 语气；色调；音调；音色Cross could hear him speaking in low tones to Sarah.克罗斯可以听到他在低声对萨拉说话。I still didn't like his tone of voice; he sounded angry and accusing.我仍然不喜欢他说话的语气；他的声音听起来好像是怒气冲冲地在指责人。The tone of the letter was very friendly.这封信的语气相当友好。There were no stores that would lower the tone of the area.没有一家商店会降低该地区的氛围。...stretch exercises that improve muscle tone.…提高肌肉结实度的伸展锻炼。This movement lengthens your spine and tones the spinal nerves.该运动能伸展你的脊柱，强健脊髓神经。Try these toning exercises before you start the day.试着在开始新的一天前练练这些健身操。Exercise tones up your body.运动强健身体。Each brick also varies slightly in tone, texture and size.每块砖在色调、质地和尺寸上也略有不同。I can't get a dial tone on this phone.我在这部电话上听不到拨号音。
trail  vt. 追踪；拖；蔓延；落后于He was following a trail through the trees.他正沿着一条崎岖小路穿过树林。...a large area of woodland with hiking and walking trails.…有徒步旅行和散步路线的大片林区。Everywhere in the house was a sticky trail of orange juice.房子里到处都是粘乎乎的橙汁印迹。Two detectives were trailing him.两个侦探正在跟踪他。During a recent speech on the campaign trail, he was interrupted by hecklers.在最近的一次竞选巡回演讲中，他被诘问者打断了。She came down the stairs slowly, trailing the coat behind her.她慢慢地走下楼梯，身后拖着大衣。The police were hot on his trail.警方正紧紧跟踪他。
transaction  n. 交易；事务；办理；会报，学报The transaction is completed by payment of the fee.交易在支付费用之后就完成了。
traverse  n. 穿过；横贯；横木I traversed the narrow pedestrian bridge.我走过了那座狭窄的步行桥。
tremendous  adj. 极大的，巨大的；惊人的；极好的I felt a tremendous pressure on my chest.我感到胸口有股巨大的压力。I thought they played tremendously well, didn't you?我认为他们表演得非常好，你不觉得吗？I thought it was absolutely tremendous.我觉得它绝对精彩。
tribute  n. 礼物；[税收] 贡物；颂词；（尤指对死者的）致敬，悼念，吊唁礼物The song is a tribute to Roy Orbison.这首歌是敬献给罗伊·奥比森的。His success has been a tribute to hard work, to professionalism.他的成功是辛勤工作和兢兢业业的结果。
trigger  vt. 引发，引起；触发A man pointed a gun at them and pulled the trigger.一个男人用枪指着他们，扣动了扳机。...trigger devices for nuclear weapons.…核武器的引爆装置。The thieves must have deliberately triggered the alarm and hidden inside the house.那些小偷一定是故意触发了报警器，然后藏在屋子里。...the incident which triggered the outbreak of the First World War.…引起第一次世界大战爆发的事件。It is still not clear what events triggered off the demonstrations.还不清楚是什么事件引发了示威。Stress may act as a trigger for these illnesses.压力也许是引发这些疾病的一个原因。
trivial  adj. 不重要的，琐碎的；琐细的The director tried to wave aside these issues as trivial details that could be settled later.那位主任对这些问题置之不理，视它们为可以后解决的无关紧要的细节。
tuck  vt. 卷起；挤进；用某物舒适地裹住；使有褶裥；收拢；大口吃；使隐藏He tried to tuck his flapping shirt inside his trousers.他试图把飘动的衬衫塞进他的裤子里。She'd undergone 13 operations, including a tummy tuck.她做过13次手术，包括1次腹部减脂。
turbulent  adj. 骚乱的，混乱的；狂暴的；吵闹的；激流的，湍流的They had been together for five or six turbulent years of break-ups and reconciliations.他们在一起度过了分分合合动荡不定的五六年。I had to have a boat that could handle turbulent seas.我必须有一条能应付汹涌海浪的船。
turnover  n. 翻覆；[贸易] 营业额；流通量；半圆卷饼；失误The company had a turnover of $3.8 million.那个公司拥有380万美元的营业额。Short-term contracts increase staff turnover.短期合同会增加员工的流动率。
underestimate  vt. 低估；看轻None of us should ever underestimate the degree of difficulty women face in career advancement.我们谁都不应低估妇女在职业发展中所面临的困难程度。I think a lot of people still underestimate him.我认为许多人仍然低估了他。
undertake  vt. 承担，保证；从事；同意；试图She undertook the task of monitoring the elections.她承担了监督选举的任务。He undertook to edit the text himself.他承诺亲自编辑正文。
underway  adj. 进行中的；起步的；航行中的An investigation is underway to find out how the disaster happened.一项调查正在进行，以查明这场灾难是如何发生的。It was a cold evening, winter well underway.那是个寒冷的夜晚，冬天早已来临。
update  vt. 更新；校正，修正；使现代化He was back in the office, updating the work schedule on the computer.他回到办公室，在计算机上更新了工作日程。Airlines would prefer to update rather than retrain crews.航空公司宁愿增添新机组人员而不愿对老的机组人员进行再培训。She had heard the newsflash on a TV channel's news update.她在电视频道的新闻快讯里听到了这条简短报道。...a weather update.…最新天气预报。We'll update you on the day's top news stories.我们将向你提供当天的头条新闻。
utilize  vt. 利用Sound engineers utilize a range of techniques to enhance the quality of the recordings.音响工程师利用一系列的技术来提高录音质量。...the utilization of human resources.…人力资源的利用。
vacant  adj. 空虚的；空的；空缺的；空闲的；茫然的Halfway down the bus was a vacant seat.这辆公共汽车中部有个空座。The position of chairman has been vacant for some time.主席的职位已经空缺一段时间了。She had a kind of vacant look on her face.在她脸上有一种茫然的表情。He looked vacantly out of the window.他茫然地望着窗外。
vain  adj. 徒劳的；自负的；无结果的；无用的The drafting committee worked through the night in a vain attempt to finish on schedule.起草委员会徒劳地通宵工作想按期完成工作。He hunted vainly through his pockets for a piece of paper.他徒劳地摸索着自己的口袋想找到一张纸。He married his fourth wife, Susan, in the vain hope that she would improve his health.他怀着她能改善自己健康的徒然希望娶了第4个妻子苏珊。He then set out for Virginia for what he vainly hoped would be a peaceful retirement.于是他出发前往弗吉尼亚，徒然地希望这会是一次平静的引退。He wasn't so vain as to think he was smarter than his boss.他还没有自负到以为他比自己的上司还精明。He stopped at the door, waiting in vain for her to acknowledge his presence.他停在门口，徒然地等着她跟自己打招呼。He wants the world to know his son did not die in vain.他想让世人知道他儿子的死不是毫无意义的。
valid  adj. 有效的；有根据的；合法的；正当的They put forward many valid reasons for not exporting.他们提出了许多有根据的理由来反对出口。The editorial says this argument has lost much of its validity.这篇社论说该论点已失去了其许多合理性。Most designers share the unspoken belief that fashion is a valid form of visual art.大多数设计师都有一种心照不宣的信念，即时尚是视觉艺术的一种重要形式。...the validity of making children wear bicycle helmets.…让孩子们戴自行车头盔的重要性。All tickets are valid for two months.所有的票在两个月内有效。
venture  vt. 敢于...a Russian-American joint venture.…一个俄美合资的风险项目。People are afraid to venture out for fear of sniper attacks.人们不敢冒险外出，害怕狙击手的袭击。"So you're Leo's girlfriend?" he ventured.“那么你就是利奥的女朋友了？”他小心地问道。He ventured that plants draw part of their nourishment from the air.他试探着提出了植物从空气中吸取它们的部分养分的观点。"Don't ask," he said, whenever Ginny ventured to raise the subject.每当金尼冒险提起这个话题时，他总是说∶“你不要问了。”He enjoyed little success when he ventured into business.他在冒险涉足生意时很少成功。
verbal  adj. 口头的；言语的；动词的；照字面的They were jostled and subjected to a torrent of verbal abuse.他们被推来搡去，并受到了潮水般的辱骂。Dave drank heavily and became verbally abusive.戴夫喝多了，嘴里脏话连篇。The test has scores for verbal skills, mathematical skills, and abstract reasoning skills.该项测试对文字表达技能、数学技能和抽象推理技能进行记分。...a verbal noun.…一个动名词。
verify  vt. 核实；查证I verified the source from which I had that information.我核实了我获知那条信息的来源。All charges against her are dropped pending the verification of her story.在她的陈述得到证实前，所有针对她的指控都被撤回。The government has not verified any of those reports.该政府尚未证实那些报道中的任何一个。
versatile  adj. 多才多艺的；通用的，万能的；多面手的He had been one of the game's most versatile athletes.他是这次运动会中最有才能的运动员之一。Aileen stands out for her incredible versatility as an actress.作为一名女演员，艾琳以其难以置信的多才多艺而出类拔萃。Never before has computing been so versatile.计算机技术从未像现在这样用途广泛。Velvet as a fabric is not known for its versatility.天鹅绒作为一种织物并非以其用途广泛而闻名。
versus  prep. 对；与...相对；对抗Only 18.8% of the class of 1982 had some kind of diploma four years after high school, versus 45% of the class of 1972.相对于1972届学生中有45%在中学毕业4年后获得了某种文凭来说，1982届学生的这一比例只有18.8%。Italy versus Japan is turning out to be a surprisingly well matched competition.意大利对日本队的比赛结果是一场出人意料地势均力敌的比赛。That case became known as Healey versus Jones.那起讼案被称作“希利诉琼斯案”。
violate  vt. 违反；侵犯，妨碍；亵渎They went to prison because they violated the law.他们因犯法而入狱。To deprive the boy of his education is a violation of state law.剥夺这个男孩的受教育权是一种违反州法律的行为。These men were violating her family's privacy.这些男人在侵犯她的家庭隐私。Detectives are still searching for those who violated the graveyard.侦探们还在查找那些亵渎了墓地的家伙。The violation of the graves is not the first such incident.亵渎墓地的事件这已不是第一回。
allotment  n. 分配；分配物；养家费；命运His meagre allotment of petrol had to be saved for emergencies.他的天然气的微薄份额必须省下以备急用。
aloft  adv. 在空中；在高处；在上面He held the trophy proudly aloft.他骄傲地把奖杯举向空中。
amend  vt. 修改；改善，改进The president agreed to amend the constitution and allow multi-party elections.总统同意了修正宪法并且允许多党选举。He wanted to make amends for causing their marriage to fail.他想为一手造成他们婚姻的破裂做出补偿。

animate  vt. 使有生气；使活泼；鼓舞；推动Natural philosophy involved the study of all aspects of the material world, animate and inanimate.自然哲学涉及到了对包括有生命体与无生命体的物质世界的全面研究。There was precious little about the cricket to animate the crowd.这场板球比赛极少有让观众兴奋的地方。
annoy  vt. 骚扰；惹恼；打搅Try making a note of the things that annoy you.试着把让你心烦的事记下来。It annoyed me that I didn't have time to do more ironing.没有时间熨更多的衣服让我心烦了。
anticipate  vt. 预期，期望；占先，抢先；提前使用At the time we couldn't have anticipated the result of our campaigning.当时我们不可能预期到我们活动的结果。It is anticipated that the equivalent of 192 full-time jobs will be lost.据预测相当于192个全职的工作将会丧失。What Jeff did was to anticipate my next question.杰夫所做的是预先准备我的下一个问题。
apparatus  n. 装置，设备；仪器；器官For many years, the country had been buried under the apparatus of the regime.多年来，该国一直处于这种政体的统治下。One of the boys had to be rescued by firemen wearing breathing apparatus.其中的一个男孩得由戴着呼吸设备的消防队员们营救。
apparent  adj. 显然的；表面上的I was a bit depressed by our apparent lack of progress.我对我们表面上的缺乏进展感到有点沮丧。It has been apparent that in other areas standards have held up well.显然在其他领域标准保持得良好。The person may become dizzy for no apparent reason.此人可能会莫名其妙地变得头晕目眩。

appoint  vt. 任命；指定；约定It made sense to appoint a banker to this job.任命一位银行家做这项工作是合理的。The president has appointed a civilian as defence secretary.总统任命了一位平民做国防部长。
appraisal  n. 评价；估价（尤指估价财产，以便征税）；估计What is needed in such cases is a calm appraisal of the situation.在此类情况下需要的是对形势的冷静估计。One of the most important tools for organizational improvement is the performance appraisal.组织改进的最重要手段之一是业绩评估。It may also be necessary to get a new appraisal of the property.可能还需要对该房产做个新的估价。
appreciate  vt. 欣赏；感激；领会；鉴别Anyone can appreciate our music.任何人都能欣赏我们的音乐。She never really appreciated the depth and bitterness of the family's conflict.她从未真正理解该家庭矛盾的深度与激烈程度。Peter stood by me when I most needed it. I'll always appreciate that.彼得在我最需要时支持了我。我对此将永远感激。They don't have any confidence that houses will appreciate in value.他们对房屋增值没有一点信心。
approximate  vt. 近似；使…接近；粗略估计The approximate cost varies from around $150 to $250.大致的费用在$150至$250之间不等。Approximately $150 million is to be spent on improvements.大概1.5亿美元将花在改进上。They did not have even an approximate idea what the Germans really wanted.他们对于德国人真正想要什么甚至没有一个大致概念。The mixture described below will approximate it, but is not exactly the same.下面所描述的混合物会与之近似，但不完全一样。

arch  n. 弓形，拱形；拱门When she passed under the arch leading out of the park, Mira whooped with delight.从通向公园外的拱门下走过时，米拉高兴地喊叫起来。...the arch of the fishing rods.…钓鱼竿的弧线。"Good girl," said Frank, winding the bandages around the arch of her foot.“好姑娘，”弗兰克说道，一边把绷带缠在她的足弓上。Don't arch your back, keep your spine straight.别弓着背，挺直脊梁。

assimilate  vt. 吸收；使同化；把…比作；使相似There is every sign that new Asian-Americans are just as willing to assimilate.各种迹象表明新的亚裔美籍人简直一样愿意被同化。His family tried to assimilate into the white and Hispanic communities.他的家人努力融入到白人和拉美人社区。They promote social integration and assimilation of minority ethnic groups into the culture.他们提倡少数民族团体与该文化的社会融合及同化。My mind could only assimilate one impossibility at a time.我的头脑一次只能吸纳一件不可能的事情。This technique brings life to instruction and eases assimilation of knowledge.这种技术给教学带来活力，并使知识的吸收更加容易。

cast  vt. 投，抛；计算；浇铸；投射（光、影、视线等）The show is very amusing and the cast is very good.表演非常有趣，演员都很优秀。The world premiere of Harold Pinter's new play casts Ian Holm in the lead role.哈罗德·品特新戏的首次全球公演选择伊恩·霍姆扮演主要角色。He was cast as a college professor.他被选扮演大学教授这个角色。He cast a stern glance at the two men.他严厉地瞪了那两名男子一眼。I cast my eyes down briefly.我往下瞅了瞅。The moon cast a bright light over the garden.月亮在院子里撒下清辉。Last night a top criminal psychologist cast doubt on the theory.昨晚，一位顶级的犯罪心理学家让人对该理论生疑。About ninety-five per cent of those who cast their votes approve the new constitution.95%的人投票赞成新宪法。Our door knocker is cast in solid brass.我们的门环是纯铜铸造的。An orthodontist took a cast of the inside of Billy's mouth to make a dental plate.正牙医师从比利的口腔内部取了模型来制作齿板。

choke  vt. 呛；使窒息；阻塞；抑制；扑灭A small child could choke on the doll's hair.小孩子可能会因玩具娃娃的头发而窒息。Dense smoke swirled and billowed, its rank fumes choking her.浓密的烟雾盘旋翻腾，刺鼻的烟味使她窒息。The girl choked to death after breathing in smoke.那位女孩吸入烟雾后窒息而亡。The men pushed him into the entrance of a nearby building, where they choked him with his tie.那些男人把他推进了附近一座大楼的入口处，然后在那里用他的领带将他勒死了。The village's roads are choked with traffic.那个村庄的道路被车辆阻塞住了。It is like driving your car with the choke out all the time.就像一直松着阻气门在开车一样。

contemporary  n. 同时代的人；同时期的东西She writes a lot of contemporary music for people like Whitney Houston.她为惠特尼·休斯敦等人创作大量当代音乐作品。...drawing upon official records and the reports of contemporary witnesses.…借助官方记录以及当时目击者的证言。Like most of my contemporaries, I grew up in a vastly different world.像我同时代的大多数人一样，我在一个非常不同的世界里长大。
contempt  n. 轻视，蔑视；耻辱He has contempt for those beyond his immediate family circle.他对自己直系亲属以外的人都心怀蔑视。
continuity  n. 连续性；一连串；分镜头剧本...a tank designed to ensure continuity of fuel supply during aerobatics.…为特技飞行中确保持续供油而设计的油箱。
convene  vt. 召集，集合；传唤Last August he convened a meeting of his closest advisers at Camp David.去年8月份，他在戴维营召集他最亲近的顾问开了一次会。
converge  vt. 使汇聚Hundreds of tractors will converge on the capital.成百上千的拖拉机将向首都聚集。As they flow south, the five rivers converge.这5条河向南流，最终汇合在一起。
convert  vt. 使转变；转换…；使…改变信仰The signal will be converted into digital code.信号将被转变成数字编码。...naturally occurring substances which the body can convert into vitamins.…可以在身体内转化成维生素的天然物质。By converting the attic, they were able to have two extra bedrooms.通过改建阁楼，他们又多出了两间卧室。...the entrepreneur who wants to convert County Hall into a hotel.…想把县政大厅改建成旅馆的企业家。Save money by converting your car to run on used vegetable oil.通过改装你的汽车使其燃烧用过的植物油来省钱。Converting metric measurements to U.S. equivalents is easy.把公制度量衡换算成美制度量衡很容易。If you try to convert him, you could find he just walks away.如果你想让他改变信仰，他会扭头就走。He was a major influence in converting Godwin to political radicalism.戈德温主要在他的影响下信仰了政治激进主义。She, too, was a convert to Roman Catholicism.她也改信罗马天主教了。As recent converts to vegetarianism and animal rights, they now live with a menagerie of stray animals.作为最近开始热衷素食主义和动物权利保护的人们，他们现在和一群流浪动物生活在一起。
convict  vt. 证明…有罪；宣告…有罪In 1977 he was convicted of murder and sentenced to life imprisonment.在1977年，他因谋杀被判处终生监禁。There was insufficient evidence to convict him.没有足够的证据证明他有罪。...Neil Jordan's tale of two escaped convicts who get mistaken for priests.…尼尔·乔丹的两个越狱囚犯被误认为是牧师的故事。
cord  n. 绳索；束缚The door had been tied shut with a length of nylon cord.这扇门已经被一段尼龙绳紧紧栓住了。...electrical cord.…电源接线。...an extension cord.…电源延长线。
cordial  adj. 热忱的，诚恳的；兴奋的He had never known him to be so chatty and cordial.他以前从来不知道他是这样一个健谈而友善的人。They all greeted me very cordially and were eager to talk about the new project.他们非常友善地和我打招呼，很想谈谈新项目。
corps  n. 军团；兵种；兵队；（德国大学的）学生联合会...the Army Medical Corps.…陆军医疗部队。...seventy-five men, all combat veterans, all members of The Corps' most exclusive unit.…75名士兵，全都是作战老手、海军陆战队最精锐部队的成员。...the diplomatic corps.…外交使团。
correlate  vi. 关联Obesity correlates with increased risk for hypertension and stroke.过度肥胖与高血压和中风的发病风险增加密切相关。The political opinions of spouses correlate more closely than their heights.与身高匹配相比，配偶之间的政治观点更为接近。Attempts to correlate specific language functions with particular parts of the brain have not advanced very far.试图把特定的语言功能和大脑特定区域相联系的努力还没有取得很大进展。
correspond  vi. 符合，一致；相应；通信Racegoers will be given a number which will correspond to a horse running in a race.观看赛马的观众将领到一个与参赛马匹相对应的号码。The two maps of the Rockies correspond closely.这两张落基山脉的地图极为相似。The rise in interest rates was not reflected in a corresponding rise in the dollar.利率上调没有反映在相应的美元增值上。She still corresponds with friends she met in Majorca nine years ago.她依然和9年前在马略卡岛遇到的朋友们通信。
corrode  vt. 侵蚀；损害He has devised a process for making gold wires which neither corrode nor oxidize.他发明了一种制造程序，使金线既不会腐蚀也不会氧化。Engineers found the structure had been corroded by moisture.工程师们发现这个构件已经被湿气腐蚀了。The investigators found that the underground pipes were badly corroded.调查人员发现地下管道已是严重腐蚀的。
corrupt  adj. 腐败的，贪污的；堕落的...to save the nation from corrupt politicians of both parties.…把国家从两党腐败的政客们手中解救出来。It is sad to see a man so corrupted by the desire for money and power.看到一个人被金钱和权力欲望所腐蚀很可悲。Power tends to corrupt.权力容易造成腐化。...warning that television will corrupt us all.…电视会使我们所有人堕落的警示。
costume  n. 服装，装束；戏装，剧装Even from a distance, the effect of his fox costume was stunning.即使从远处看，他的狐装造型也非常漂亮。The performers, in costume and makeup, were walking up and down backstage.演员们穿着戏服化着妆，在后台走来走去。...men and women in eighteenth-century costume.…身着18世纪服装的男男女女。...a lavish costume drama set in Ireland and the U.S. in the 1890s.…以19世纪90年代的爱尔兰和美国为背景的一部大型古装戏。

credible  adj. 可靠的，可信的Her claims seem credible to many.她的说法似乎在许多人看来是可信的。Mr. Robertson would be a credible candidate.罗伯逊先生将是一名有希望成功的候选人。
crossroads  n. 十字路口；交叉路口；聚会的中心地点（crossroad的复数形式）Turn right at the first crossroads.在第一个十字路口向右转。The company was clearly at a crossroads.这个公司显然正处于紧要关头。
diffuse  adj. 弥漫的；散开的Over time, however, the technology is diffused and adopted by other countries.然而，随着时间的推移，这项技术在其它国家得以传播并使用。...to diffuse new ideas obtained from elsewhere.…传播从别处获得的新思想。...the development and diffusion of ideas.…思想的发展和传播。The presidents will meet to try and diffuse the tensions that threaten to reignite the conflict.总统们将举行会晤以试图缓解可能重新引发冲突的紧张局面。Diffusing a light also reduces its power.使光线漫射也会减弱其能量。It allows nicotine to diffuse slowly and steadily into the bloodstream.它使尼古丁缓慢、稳步地扩散到血液当中。There are data on the rates of diffusion of molecules.有一些关于分子的扩散速率的数据。

dimension  n. 方面;[数] 维；尺寸；次元；容积 vt. 标出尺寸There is a political dimension to the accusations.这些指控含有政治因素。Drilling will continue on the site to assess the dimensions of the new oilfield.钻探还将继续在现场进行以估测新油田的大小。The dimensions of the market collapse, in terms of turnover and price, were certainly not anticipated.股市崩盘的规模，无论从成交量还是价格来看，都是出乎意料的。

discreet  adj. 谨慎的；小心的They were gossipy and not always discreet.他们爱说闲话，而且不总是言语谨慎。I took the phone, and she went discreetly into the living room.我拿了电话，她就谨慎地到客厅去了。We were very discreet about the romance.我们对这一段罗曼史守口如瓶。Everyone worked to make him welcome, and, more discreetly, to find out about him.大家都尽力使他受欢迎，且更为小心地去了解他。She is wearing a noticeably stylish, feminine dress, plus discreet jewellery.她穿着一条非常时髦、有女人味的连衣裙，配以小巧的首饰。...stately houses, discreetly hidden behind great avenues of sturdy trees.…那些豪宅，隐隐约约掩藏在茂密的林荫大道后面。

discriminate  vt. 歧视；区别；辨别He is incapable of discriminating between a good idea and a terrible one.他没能力在一个好主意和一个坏主意之间进行区分。They believe the law discriminates against women.他们认为这项法律歧视妇女。...legislation which would discriminate in favour of racial minorities.…会偏向少数民族的法规。
disgust  n. 厌恶，嫌恶He spoke of his disgust at the incident.他谈到了对此事的厌恶。He disgusted many with his boorish behaviour.他以其粗鲁的行为使许多人感到厌恶。
dispatch  n. 派遣；急件He had been continually dispatching scouts ahead.他一直不断地派遣侦察员到前面去。The dispatch of the task force is purely a contingency measure.派遣特遣队纯粹是应急措施。The victory inspired him to dispatch a gleeful telegram to Roosevelt.胜利鼓舞了他发喜电给罗斯福。We have 125 cases ready for dispatch.我们有125个待发的箱子。
dispense  vt. 分配，分发；免除；执行The union had already dispensed $60000 in grants.工会已经分发了6万美元的补助金。For two weeks, the cash machine spewed out receipts apologizing for its inability to dispense money.两周了，自动取款机就输出了一些因其无法提款而致歉的凭条。Health officials hope to begin dispensing anti-retroviral drugs on a wide scale at the beginning of next year.卫生官员们希望在明年年初开始大规模配发抗逆转录病毒药物。

distil  vi. 蒸馏；提炼；渗出The whisky had been distilled in 1926 and sat quietly maturing until 1987.这瓶威士忌是1926年被蒸馏的，存放至1987年酿造成熟。Any faults in the original cider stood out sharply after distillation.苹果酒原浆中的任何瑕疵蒸馏后就会突现出来。The oil is distilled from the berries of this small tree.这种油是从这种小树的浆果中提炼的。The distillation of rose petals to produce rosewater almost certainly originated in Ancient Persia.用玫瑰花瓣提炼制造玫瑰水几乎可以肯定是起源于古波斯。Reviews are distilled from articles previously published in the main column.评论文章荟萃了发表于各大专栏文章的精华。Eventually passion was distilled into the natural beauty of a balmy night.激情最终融入了芬芳夜晚的自然美之中。The material below is a distillation of his work.下面的材料是他著作的精萃。
distinct  adj. 明显的；独特的；清楚的；有区别的Engineering and technology are disciplines distinct from one another and from science.工程学和工艺学是互不相同的学科，也不同于理科。...a banking industry with two distinctly different sectors.…有两个截然不同部门的银行业。...to impart a distinct flavour with a minimum of cooking fat.…加入最少量的烹调油脂做出独特的风味。I distinctly heard the loudspeaker calling passengers for the Washington-Miami flight.我清楚地听到扩音器在呼叫由华盛顿飞往迈阿密的旅客。Now that Tony was no longer present, there was a distinct change in her attitude.现在托尼不在场了，她的态度就发生了明显变化。I distinctly remember wishing I had not got involved.我清楚地记得我巴不得自己没有参与进去。Being 6ft 3in tall has some distinct disadvantages!身高6英尺3英寸有明显的劣势！His government is looking distinctly shaky.他的政府看起来显然岌岌可危。There's a lot of evidence that oily fish, as distinct from fatty meat, has a beneficial effect.大量证据显示，含油的鱼与肥肉不同，具有益处。
diversion  n. 转移；消遣；分散注意力...armed robbers who escaped after throwing smoke bombs to create a diversion.…在扔出烟雾弹造成注意力分散之后逃跑的武装抢劫犯们。A slight diversion in the road is causing major headaches for businesses along El Camino Real.马路上的一小段绕行道让国王大道沿街的商家十分头疼。...the illegal diversion of profits from secret arms sales.…销售秘密武器所得收益的非法转移。
divine  adj. 神圣的；非凡的；天赐的；极好的He suggested that the civil war had been a divine punishment.他暗示此次内战是上天的惩罚。The law was divinely ordained.此法律为神授。Her carrot cake is divine.她的胡萝卜饼好吃极了。
dizzy  adj. 晕眩的；使人头晕的；昏乱的；心不在焉的；愚蠢的Her head still hurt, and she felt slightly dizzy and disoriented.她的头还在痛，感觉有些眩晕，分不清方向。His head injury causes dizziness and nausea.他头部受伤引起眩晕和呕吐。She is famed for playing dizzy blondes.她以扮演没头脑但招人喜爱的金发美女而闻名。I escalated to the dizzy heights of director's secretary.我逐渐升到了主任秘书这样的职位。
dodge  n. 躲闪；托词I dodged back into the alley and waited a minute.我往后一闪，躲进胡同里等了一会儿。He desperately dodged a speeding car trying to run him down.他拼命地闪身躲开一辆高速撞向自己的汽车。He boasts of dodging military service by feigning illness.他吹嘘说自己装病逃过了兵役。This was not just a tax dodge.这不仅仅是逃税的问题。

draft  n. 汇票；草稿；选派；（尤指房间、烟囱、炉子等供暖系统中的）（小股）气流I rewrote his rough draft, which was published under my name.我改写了他那篇以我的名义发表了的初稿。I faxed a first draft of this article to him.我把这篇文章的初稿传真给他。Payments must be made in U.S. dollars by a bank draft drawn to the order of the United Nations Postal Administration.付款必须用开给联合国邮政管理处的银行汇票，并以美元支付。Block drafts around doors and windows.挡住门窗周围的风。He drafted a letter to the editors.他草拟了一封给编辑的信。During the Second World War, he was drafted into the U.S. Army.第二次世界大战期间，他应征加入美国陆军。She hoped that Fox could be drafted to run the organization.她希望福克斯能够被选派来掌管这个组织。...his effort to avoid the draft.…他逃避兵役的努力。

dynamic  adj. 动态的；动力的；动力学的；有活力的He seemed a dynamic and energetic leader.他看来是个富有创新力与活力的领导。He's one of the most dynamically imaginative jazz pianists of our time.他是我们这个时代最具活跃想像力的爵士乐钢琴演奏家之一。South Asia continues to be the most dynamic economic region in the world.南亚仍然是世界上最具活力的经济区。...a dynamic, evolving worldwide epidemic.…一次不断变化发展的、世界范围内的疾疫流行。The dynamic of the market demands constant change and adjustment.市场的动力要求有不断的变化和调整。What is needed is insight into the dynamics of the social system.所需要的就是对社会制度反动力的洞悉。

elegant  adj. 高雅的，优雅的；讲究的；简炼的；简洁的Patricia looked beautiful and elegant as always.帕特丽夏看上去跟往常一样美丽优雅。The furniture managed to combine practicality with elegance.这家具结合了实用与优雅。The document impressed me with its elegant simplicity.这份文件以其精妙的简约给我留下了深刻的印象。...an elegantly simple idea.…一个精妙地简单的主意。
eloquent  adj. 意味深长的；雄辩的，有口才的；有说服力的；动人的I heard him make a very eloquent speech at that dinner.我听他在那次晚餐上做了一次很有说服力的演说。...the eloquence of his prose.…他散文的说服力。He was eloquent about his love of books.他善于谈论他对书籍的热爱。She can speak with an eloquence that is almost inspirational.她能用一种近乎激发灵感的口才发言。

fantastic  adj. 奇异的；空想的；异想天开的；古怪的；极好的，极出色的；不可思议的；不切实际的I have a fantastic social life.我有着极好的社交生活。...fantastic amounts of money.…几笔巨款。...a fantastically expensive restaurant.…一家极其昂贵的餐馆。
feast  vt. 享受；款待，宴请Lunch was a feast of meat and vegetables, cheese, yoghurt and fruit, with unlimited wine.午餐是一场盛宴，有肉、蔬菜、奶酪、酸奶和水果，以及不限量的葡萄酒。The fruit was often served at wedding feasts.婚宴上常有水果供应。The Jewish feast of Passover began last night.犹太人的宗教节日逾越节昨晚开始了。They feasted well into the afternoon on mutton and corn stew.他们尽情享用玉米炖羊肉，一直吃到下午。Only a few feet away, their captors feasted in the castle's banqueting hall.仅仅几英尺外，俘获他们的人在城堡的宴会厅里大吃大喝。The feasting, drinking, dancing and revelry continued for several days.宴会、畅饮、跳舞和狂欢持续了几天。She stood feasting her eyes on the view.她站着尽情欣赏着那片景色。
feat  n. 功绩，壮举；技艺表演A racing car is an extraordinary feat of engineering.赛车是工程学的一项非凡业绩。
fellowship  n. 团体；友谊；奖学金；研究员职位...the National Schizophrenia Fellowship.…全国精神分裂协会。He was offered a research fellowship at Yale.他得到了一个耶鲁大学的研究员职位。...a sense of community and fellowship.…一种社群归属感和友谊感。
fiction  n. 小说；虚构，编造；谎言Immigrant tales have always been popular themes in fiction.移民故事一直是小说的流行主题。The truth or fiction of this story has never been truly determined.这个故事是真实还是虚构，一直没有定论。Total recycling is a fiction.完全回收利用是假象。
fitting  n. 装配，装置；试穿，试衣...brass light fittings.…黄铜灯具配件。...industrial fittings for kitchen and bathroom.…工业化生产的厨卫配件。She lunched and shopped and went for fittings for clothes she didn't need.她吃过午饭就去购物，还试穿那些她根本不需要的衣服。...a detailed list of what fixtures and fittings are included in the purchase price.…哪些固定装置和可拆除装置包含在购价中的一份详细清单。A solitary man, it was perhaps fitting that he should have died alone.他是个独居的人，或许他本应该孤独地死去才合适。He closed out his career, fittingly, by hitting a home run.他以一记本垒打恰当地结束了自己的棒球生涯。
fixture  n. 设备；固定装置；固定于某处不大可能移动之物...a detailed list of what fixtures and fittings are included in the purchase price.…详细列出的室内设施与装备包括在购买价格中。
flap  n. 拍打，拍打声；神经紧张；[航] 襟翼Grey sheets flapped on the clothes line.灰色的床单在晾衣绳上飘动。The bird flapped its wings furiously.那只鸟儿使劲地拍打着翅膀。...a kid running and flapping her arms.…一个边跑边像小鸟一样上下扇动着双臂的小女孩。He drew back the tent flap and strode out into the blizzard.他拉开帐篷的门帘，大步走进了暴风雪中。...the sudden slowing as the flaps were lowered.…副翼降下时的突然减速。
flatter  vt. 奉承；谄媚；使高兴I knew she was just flattering me.我知道她只是在奉承我。I flatter myself that this campaign will put an end to the war.我自以为这次战役将结束这场战争。that dress flatters her
fling  vt. 掷，抛；嘲笑；使陷入；轻蔑地投射；猛动The woman flung the cup at him.那女人使劲把杯子朝他扔过去。He flung himself to the floor.他突然跳到了地板上。She flung her arms around my neck and kissed me.她猛地搂住我的脖子吻了我。The youth got him by the front of his shirt and flung him to the ground.那个年轻人抓住他的衬衫前襟把他推倒在地。Peter flung his shoes into the corner.彼得把他的鞋扔到了角落里。She flung herself into her career.她投身于自己的事业中。She claims she had a brief fling with him 30 years ago.她声称30年前曾跟他有过一段短暂的风流韵事。
flock  n. 群；棉束（等于floc）They kept a small flock of sheep.他们养了一小群绵羊。These cases all attracted flocks of famous writers.这些案例均吸引了大批知名作家。The public has flocked to the show.公众蜂拥而去看那场演出。The criticisms will not stop people flocking to see the film.这些批评阻止不了涌向看这部影片的人潮。
flourish  n. 兴旺；茂盛；挥舞；炫耀；华饰Business flourished and within six months they were earning 18,000 roubles a day.生意兴隆，6个月中他们每天挣18000卢布。Boston quickly became a flourishing port.波斯顿迅速成为一个繁荣的港口。The plant flourishes particularly well in slightly harsher climes.这种植物在较为恶劣一点的气候中长得特别茂盛。...a flourishing fox population.…不断繁衍的狐狸群。He flourished the glass to emphasize the point.他挥舞着杯子来强调这一点。He took his cap from under his arm with a flourish and pulled it low over his eyes.他挥手从腋下取出帽子，拉低帽檐盖住眼睛。
fluctuate  vi. 波动；涨落；动摇Body temperature can fluctuate if you are ill.如果你病了，体温会波动。Don't worry about tiny fluctuations in your weight.不用担心你体重的轻微波动。
foam  n. 泡沫；水沫；灭火泡沫The water curved round the rocks in great bursts of foam.水流卷绕着岩石产生大量的泡沫。...shaving foam.…剃须泡沫。...modern three-piece suites filled with foam rubber.…塞满海绵的现代3件套。
foil  vt. 衬托；阻止，挡开；挫败；贴箔于Pour cider around the meat and cover with foil.在肉的四周倒上苹果酒，然后盖上箔纸。A brave police chief foiled an armed robbery by grabbing the raider's shotgun.一个勇敢的警长夺过歹徒的猎枪，挫败了一起武装抢劫。
foremost  adj. 最重要的；最先的He was one of the world's foremost scholars of ancient Indian culture.他是世界上最优秀的古印度文化学者之一。It is first and foremost a trade agreement.它首先是一项贸易协定。
foresee  vt. 预见；预知He did not foresee any problems.他没有预见到任何问题。
fort  n. 堡垒；要塞；（美）边界贸易站His business partner is holding the fort while he is away.他的生意伙伴在他不在的时候代他处理事务。"I'll hold down the fort until he's back," Clark said.“在他回来之前我会代他处理事务，”克拉克说。
forthcoming  adj. 即将来临的...his opponents in the forthcoming elections.…他在即将到来的选举中的对手们。They promised that the money would be forthcoming.他们承诺说钱会到位的。One source predicts no major shift in policy will be forthcoming at the committee hearings.有一消息预言在委员会听证会上不会有政策上的重大变动。William, sadly, was not very forthcoming about any other names he might have, where he lived or what his phone number was.很遗憾，威廉在有关他可能有的其它名字、他的住处或者电话号码等方面不太愿意提供信息。
foul  adj. 犯规的；邪恶的；污秽的；淤塞的...foul polluted water.…污染了的、又脏又臭的水。The teachers had to deal with her foul language, disruptive behaviour, and low academic performance.老师们不得不应付她粗俗的语言、捣乱的行为和不良的学业成绩。Collins was in a foul mood even before the interviews began.柯林斯甚至在面试开始之前就处于暴躁情绪。No amount of foul weather, whether hail, wind, rain or snow, seems to deter them.不管天气有多恶劣，哪怕是冰雹、大风、雨还是雪，似乎都阻止不了他们。It is an offence to let your dog foul a footpath.让你的狗在人行道上拉屎是一种违法行为。Nowitzki fouled Mitchell early in the third quarter.在第三节早些时候，诺维斯基就对米切尔犯了规。Harridge was charged with a flagrant foul and ejected from the game.哈里基被指恶意犯规并被逐出了比赛。...a foul tackle.…一次犯规的阻截。He had fallen foul of the FBI.他已惹恼了联邦调查局。
fracture  n. 破裂，断裂；[外科] 骨折At least one-third of all women over ninety have sustained a hip fracture.90岁以上的妇女中至少有1/3遭受过髋骨骨折。You've fractured a rib, maybe more than one.你断了一根肋骨，也许不止一根。One strut had fractured and been crudely repaired in several places.一根支柱断裂了，好几处已做了粗略修补。His policy risks fracturing the coalition.他的政策有分裂联盟的危险。
fundamental  adj. 基本的，根本的Our constitution embodies all the fundamental principles of democracy.我们的宪法体现了民主的所有基本原则。A fundamental human right is being withheld from these people.这些人的一项基本人权正被剥夺。But on this question, the two leaders have very fundamental differences.但在这个问题上，这两位领导人有着极根本的分歧。He believes better relations with China are fundamental to the well-being of the area.他相信与中国的更好关系对这个地区的福祉是绝对必要的。The fundamental problem lies in their inability to distinguish between reality and invention.主要问题在于他们不能区分现实和虚构。
fury  n. 狂怒；暴怒；激怒者She screamed, her face distorted with fury and pain.她尖叫着，她的脸因愤怒和痛苦而扭曲了。
fuse  vi. 融合；熔化，熔融The fuse blew as he pressed the button to start the motor.保险丝在他按下按钮发动车子时烧断了。A bomb was deactivated at the last moment, after the fuse had been lit.一枚炸弹在导火线已被点燃后的最后一刻被解除。The skull bones fuse between the ages of fifteen and twenty-five.颅骨在15和25岁之间长合。Manufactured glass is made by fusing various types of sand.人造玻璃是通过熔合不同种类的沙子制造出来的。
fuss  vi. 小题大作；忙乱；焦燥；焦急；无事自扰I don't know what all the fuss is about.我不知道这一切无谓的忙乎是怎么回事。Carol fussed about getting me a drink.卡萝尔忙乎着给我弄杯饮料。My wife was fussing over the food and clothing we were going to take.我妻子在为我们要带的食物和衣服瞎操心。"Stop fussing," he snapped.“别瞎忙了，”他怒斥道。Auntie Hilda and Uncle Jack couldn't fuss over them enough.希尔达婶婶和杰克叔叔再宠爱他们不过了。I don't know why everybody makes such a fuss about a few mosquitoes.我不知道为什么所有人都为几只蚊子发这么大的牢骚。
gamble  vi. 赌博；孤注一掷；投机；打赌Yesterday, he named his cabinet and took a big gamble in the process.昨天他冒了很大的风险任命了他的内阁。Few firms will be willing to gamble on new products.很少有公司愿意在新产品上冒险。They are not prepared to gamble their careers on this matter.他们没准备为此事拿自己的事业来当赌注。Most people visit Las Vegas to gamble their hard-earned money.多数人去拉斯维加斯是为了用他们辛苦赚来的钱赌博。John gambled heavily on the horses.约翰在这几匹马上下了大赌注。
gasp  vi. 喘气；喘息；渴望An audible gasp went around the court as the jury announced the verdict.陪审团宣布判决的时候，法庭上听到倒抽了一口气的声音。She gasped for air and drew in a lungful of water.她倒吸气，吸了一大口水。...the last gasp of a dying system of censorship.…行将结束的审查制度的最后时刻。
gaze  vi. 凝视；注视...gazing at herself in the mirror.…凝视着镜中的她自己。Sitting in his wicker chair, he gazed reflectively at the fire.坐在他的柳条椅中，他若有所思地凝视着火焰。The Monsignor turned his gaze from the flames to meet the Colonel's.这位阁下把他凝视的目光从火焰上移开，与上校的目光相遇。She felt increasingly uncomfortable under the woman's steady gaze.她在那女人目不转睛的凝视下感到愈发不舒服。You won't find a couple more in the public gaze than Michael and Lizzie.你找不到比迈克尔和莉齐更受公众关注的夫妻了。
gear  n. 齿轮；装置，工具；传动装置On hills, he must use low gears.在山上，他必须用低速挡。The car was in fourth gear.那辆汽车处于第4挡。About 100 officers in riot gear were needed to break up the fight.大约需要100名配备防暴装备的警官来结束那场斗殴。...fishing gear.…钓鱼用具。I used to wear trendy gear but it just looked ridiculous.我过去常穿时髦服装，但那看起来简直滑稽。Colleges are not always geared to the needs of mature students.大学并不总是去适应成年学生的需要。My training was geared toward winning gold.我的训练是为赢得金牌去规划的。
generalize  vt. 概括；推广；使...一般化Critics love to generalize, to formulate trends into which all new work must be fitted, however contradictory.评论家喜欢概括，归纳出所有新作品都必须符合的趋势，不管它们是如何地不符。A child first labels the household pet cat as a "cat" and then generalizes this label to other animals that look like it.孩子先把家养的宠物猫称为“猫”，然后把这个称呼扩大到其他看起来像猫的动物。
homogeneous  adj. 均匀的；[数] 齐次的；同种的；同类的，同质的The unemployed are not a homogeneous group.失业者并不都是同一类人。
honorary  adj. 荣誉的；名誉的；道义上的Harvard awarded him an honorary degree.哈佛大学授予他荣誉学位。...the honorary secretary of the Beekeepers' Association.…养蜂人协会的名誉秘书。
hound  vt. 追猎；烦扰；激励Rainey's chief interest in life is hunting with hounds.雷尼一生中的主要嗜好是带着猎犬去打猎。an otterhounda deerhoundNewcomers are constantly hounding them for advice.新来的人老是缠着他们问这问那的。There is a general view around that he has been hounded out of office by the press.人们普遍认为是媒体迫使他离职的。
hurl  vt. 丢下；用力投掷；愤慨地说出Groups of angry youths hurled stones at police.一群群愤怒的年轻人朝着警察猛掷石块。Simon caught the grenade and hurled it back.西蒙接住手榴弹，把它掷了回去。How would you handle being locked in the back of a cab while the driver hurled abuse at you?如果你被锁在出租车后座又遭司机谩骂，你会怎么办？
illicit  adj. 违法的；不正当的Dante clearly condemns illicit love.但丁明确地谴责不正当的恋情。
illuminate  vt. 阐明，说明；照亮；使灿烂；用灯装饰No streetlights illuminated the street.一盏照亮街道的路灯也没有。Instead of formulas and charts, the two instructors use games and drawings to illuminate their subject.这两位教师用游戏和图画而不是公式和图表来阐明他们的题旨。It would be illuminating to hear the views of the club vice-chairman.听听俱乐部副主席的观点或许会有启发。
imitation  n. 模仿，仿造；仿制品...the most accurate imitation of Chinese architecture in Europe.…欧洲最逼真的仿中国建筑。They discussed important issues in imitation of their elders.他们模仿长辈的口气讨论重大问题。...a complete set of Dickens bound in imitation leather.…用人造革装帧的一整套《狄更斯全集》。One boy did an imitation of a soldier with a loudspeaker.一个男孩拿着扬声器学着士兵的样子。
immunize  vt. 使免疫；赋予免疫性We should require that every student is immunized against hepatitis B.我们应该要求每一位学生都注射乙肝疫苗。The monkeys used in those experiments had previously been immunized with a vaccine made from killed infected cells.这些实验中所用的猴子事先都已接种了由死亡的被感染细胞制成的疫苗。...universal immunization against childhood diseases.…为预防儿童疾病的普遍接种疫苗。
imperial  adj. 帝国的；皇帝的；至高无上的；威严的...the Imperial Palace in Tokyo.…东京的皇宫。
implicit  adj. 含蓄的；暗示的；盲从的...an implicit warning to the Moroccans not to continue or repeat the military actions they began a week ago.…叫摩洛哥人不要继续或重复一周前开始的军事行动的含蓄警告。The jury implicitly criticized the government by their verdict.陪审团通过他们的裁决含蓄地批评了政府。Trust is implicit in the system.信任是这种体制里内含的。He had implicit faith in the noble intentions of the Emperor.他对皇帝的崇高旨意笃信不疑。I trust him implicitly.我绝对信任他。
imprison  vt. 监禁；关押；使…下狱He was imprisoned for 18 months on charges of theft.他因盗窃指控而被监禁了18个月。
impromptu  n. 即兴曲；即席演出This afternoon the Palestinians held an impromptu press conference.今天下午巴勒斯坦人召开了一场临时记者招待会。
impulse  n. 冲动；[电子] 脉冲；刺激；神经冲动；推动力Unable to resist the impulse, he glanced at the sea again.他抑制不住冲动，又看了一眼大海。It works by sending a series of electrical impulses which are picked up by hi-tech sensors.它通过传输由高技术传感器收集的电脉冲而起作用。The curtains were an impulse buy.这窗帘是一时心血来潮买下的。Sean's a fast thinker, and he acts on impulse.肖恩是个思维敏捷、凭一时冲动行事的人。
inborn  adj. 天生的；先天的He had an inborn talent for languages.他有天生的语言才能。
inclusive  adj. 包括的，包含的The academy is far more inclusive now than it used to be.该学院如今比过去更为兼收并蓄。You are also invited to join us on our prayer days (this year, June 6 to June 14 inclusive).你也受邀加入我们的祷告日（今年从6月6日（含）至6月14日（含））。...all prices are inclusive of delivery.…所有价格包括运费。The outpatient programme costs $105 per day, all inclusive.门诊病人方案收费每人每天105美元，一切费用包括在内。
incompatible  adj. 不相容的；矛盾的；不能同时成立的They feel strongly that their religion is incompatible with the political system.他们强烈地感到他们的宗教信仰与政治体制格格不入。Incompatibility between the mother's and the baby's blood groups may cause jaundice.母亲和胎儿的血型不合有可能导致黄疸。This made its mini-computers incompatible with its mainframes.这使得它的微型电脑与其主机不兼容。
incorporate  vt. 包含，吸收；体现；把……合并The new cars will incorporate a number of major improvements.这种新型汽车将包含许多重大的改进。The agreement would allow the rebels to be incorporated into a new national police force.该协议将允许叛军并入一支新的国家警察部队。
incredible  adj. 难以置信的，惊人的；极好的The wildflowers will be incredible after this rain.这场雨过后，野花将开得非常好。Their father was incredibly good-looking.他们的父亲十分英俊。It seemed incredible that people would still want to play football during a war.在战争期间人们仍然想踢足球，这似乎不可思议。Incredibly, some people don't like the name.令人难以置信的是，有些人不喜欢这个名字。I work an incredible amount of hours.我工作的时间极长。It was incredibly hard work.那是个非常艰辛的工作。
index  n. 指标；指数；索引；指针...the consumer price index.…消费价格指数。There's even a special subject index.甚至有一个特别的主题索引。A quarter of this vast archive has been indexed and made accessible to researchers.这批数量巨大的档案的1/4都已编了索引，可供研究者查阅。Minimum benefits and wages are to be indexed to inflation.最低养老金和最低工资都要与通货膨胀挂钩。
indifferent  adj. 漠不关心的；无关紧要的；中性的，中立的People have become indifferent to the suffering of others.人们已经变得对别人的痛苦漠不关心。"Not that it matters," said Trujillo indifferently.“它倒不是那么重要”，特鲁希略漠然地说。She had starred in several very indifferent movies.她领衔主演过好几部非常平庸的电影。...a shoddy piece of work, poorly written, indifferently performed.…一部粗制滥造的作品，写得差劲，演得也蹩脚。
indignant  adj. 愤愤不平的；义愤的He is indignant at suggestions that they were secret agents.他对关于他们是特务的暗示很愤慨。He was indignant that his rival was offered the job.他对他的对手得到了那份工作感到愤愤不平。"That is not true," Erica said indignantly.“那不是真的，”埃丽卡气愤地说。
induce  vt. 诱导；引起；引诱；感应Doctors said surgery could induce a heart attack.医生们说手术可能导致心脏病。More than 4,000 teachers were induced to take early retirement.四千多名教师被劝说提前退休。
induction  n. [电磁] 感应；归纳法；感应现象；入门培训，入职仪式，就职；诱导...his induction as president.…他的总统就职仪式。
inductive  adj. [数] 归纳的；[电] 感应的；诱导的
infect  vt. 感染，传染A single mosquito can infect a large number of people.一只蚊子就能传染很多人。...objects used by an infected person.…一名感染者使用过的物品。...plants that are resistant to infection.…抗感染的植物。The birds infect the milk.鸟使牛奶受污染。For an instant I was infected by her fear.一瞬间，我被她的恐惧所感染。He thought they might infect others with their bourgeois ideas.他认为他们可能用中产阶级思想去影响别人。This virus infected thousands of computers across the U.S. and Europe within days.这种病毒几天之内就使美国和欧洲成千上万台电脑中毒。
infectious  adj. 传染的；传染性的；易传染的...infectious diseases such as measles.…像麻疹这样的传染病。She radiates an infectious enthusiasm for everything she does.她做的每件事都散发出一种有感染力的热情。
inferior  adj. 差的；自卑的；下级的，下等的The cassettes were of inferior quality.这些盒式磁带质量较差。This resulted in overpriced and often inferior products.这就导致产品标价过高而往往质量较次。He preferred the company of those who were intellectually inferior to himself.他喜欢与那些智力不如他的人为伍。It was a gentleman's duty always to be civil, even to his inferiors.一个绅士的责任是一直保持彬彬有礼，即使是对比自己地位低的人。I found it difficult to shake off a sense of social inferiority.我发现很难摆脱社会地位低下的自卑感。
ingredient  n. 原料；要素；组成部分Mix in the remaining ingredients.掺入剩下的原料。The meeting had all the ingredients of high political drama.这次会议拥有了极富戏剧性的政治紧张场面的全部要素。
inlet  n. 入口，进口；插入物；水湾A tiny fishing village by a rocky inlet.岩石嶙峋的水湾边上的一个小渔村。
inner  adj. 内部的；内心的；精神的She got up and went into an inner office.她起身走进里间办公室。Loving relationships that a child makes will give him an inner sense of security.儿童所建立的友爱关系会使他的内心有一种安全感。
innumerable  adj. 无数的，数不清的He has invented innumerable excuses, told endless lies.他编造了数不清的借口，说了无止尽的谎言。
insane  adj. 疯狂的；精神病的；极愚蠢的Some people simply can't take it and they just go insane.一些人就是接受不了，于是便变得精神错乱。He asked me what I thought and I said, "Listen, this is completely insane."他问我是怎么想的，我说，“听着，这十分愚蠢。”I would be insanely jealous if Bill left me for another woman.如果比尔为了另一个女人而离开我，我会妒忌得发疯的。
inspect  vt. 检查；视察；检阅Elaine went outside to inspect the playing field.伊莱恩到外边去检查运动场。"Excellent work," he said when he had completed his inspection of the painted doors.“干得好，”他在检查完刷过油漆的门之后说道。The Public Utilities Commission inspects us once a year.公用设施委员会每年到我们这里视察一次。Officers making a routine inspection of the vessel found fifty kilograms of cocaine.对船只做例行检查的警官们发现了50公斤可卡因。
instrumental  adj. 乐器的；有帮助的；仪器的，器械的In his first years as chairman he was instrumental in raising the company's wider profile.在刚担任董事长的头几年，他在提升公司形象方面发挥了作用。...a CD of vocal and instrumental music.…一张声乐和器乐光盘。After a couple of brief instrumentals, he puts his guitar down.演奏了几首简短的器乐曲之后，他放下了吉他。
intact  adj. 完整的；原封不动的；未受损伤的Customs men put dynamite in the water to destroy the cargo, but most of it was left intact.海关人员把炸药放入水中以摧毁货物，但大部分货物却完好无损。
intellect  n. 智力，理解力；知识分子；思维逻辑领悟力；智力高的人Do the emotions develop in parallel with the intellect?情感与智力同步发展吗？She is famed for her intellect.她因才智而出名。
interact  vt. 互相影响；互相作用While the other children interacted and played together, Ted ignored them.当其他孩子们相互交往、一起玩耍时，泰德却不理他们。...superficial interactions with other people.…和其他人的表面交往。...new, simplified ways of interacting with a computer.…与计算机互动的简化新方法。...experts on human-computer interaction.…人机互动专家。You have to understand how cells interact.你必须得了解细胞之间是如何相互作用的。...the interaction between physical and emotional illness.…生理疾病和心理疾病之间的相互作用。
interactive  adj. 交互式的；相互作用的This will make computer games more interactive than ever.这将使电脑游戏比以前更具交互性。...digital television, with more channels and interactivity.…有更多频道和交互功能的数字电视。There is little evidence that this encouraged flexible, interactive teaching in the classroom.几乎没有证据表明这促进灵活互动的课堂教学。
interfere  vi. 干涉；妨碍；打扰I wish everyone would stop interfering and just leave me alone.我希望所有人都不再干涉我，让我一个人静一静。Smoking and drinking interfere with your body's ability to process oxygen.吸烟和喝酒妨碍身体对氧的吸收能力。
interim  adj. 临时的，暂时的；中间的；间歇的She was sworn in as head of an interim government in March.她3月份宣誓出任临时政府首脑。But, in the interim, we obviously have a duty to maintain law and order.但是，在过渡时期我们显然有责任维持法律与秩序。
intermediate  vi. 起媒介作用Do you make any intermediate stops between your home and work?你在住所和工作地点之间停留吗？Students are categorized as novice, intermediate, or advanced.学生分为新生、中级生或高级生。The ski school coaches beginners, intermediates, and advanced skiers.滑雪学校训练初级、中级和高级水平的滑雪者。
internal  n. 内脏；本质The country stepped up internal security.该国加强了国内安全防卫。...Russia's Ministry of Internal Affairs.…俄罗斯内务部。The state is not a unified and internally coherent entity.这个国家不是一个内部凝聚的统一体。The doctor said the internal bleeding had been massive.医生说内出血的量很大。Evening primrose oil is used on the skin as well as taken internally.夜来香油可外用在皮肤上，也可内服。
intimate  adj. 亲密的；私人的；精通的；有性关系的I discussed with my intimate friends whether I would immediately have a baby.我和我的密友们商量我是不是该马上要孩子。He did not feel he had got to know them intimately.他觉得自己不必和他们亲密熟悉。...their intimate moments with their boyfriends.…她们和其男友们的私密时刻。You have to be willing to get to know yourself and your partner intimately.你必须乐意在私密方面逐渐了解自己和伴侣。He wrote about the intimate details of his family life.他写下了家庭生活中一些私人的细节。It was the first time they had attempted to talk intimately.这是他们第一次试图私下交谈。...an intimate candlelit dinner for two.…宁静怡人的一次二人烛光晚餐。...an intimate connection between madness and wisdom.…疯狂和睿智之间的一种密切联系。Scientific research and conservation are intimately connected.科学研究与环境保护联系密切。He surprised me with his intimate knowledge of Kierkegaard and Schopenhauer.他对克尔恺郭尔和叔本华的深刻了解令我感到惊奇。...a golden age of musicians whose work she knew intimately.…她熟知的那些音乐家们的一个黄金时代。He went on to intimate that he was indeed contemplating a shake-up of the company.他接着暗示他确实在考虑对公司进行一次改组。

intimidate  vt. 恐吓，威胁；胁迫Jones had set out to intimidate and dominate Paul.琼斯曾试图威胁并控制保罗。...an inquiry into allegations of intimidation during last week's vote.…一项对上周选举期间恐吓指控的调查。
intrinsic  adj. 本质的，固有的Diamonds have little intrinsic value and their price depends almost entirely on their scarcity.钻石没有多少内在价值，它们的价格几乎完全取决于其稀有程度。Sometimes I wonder if people are intrinsically evil.有时我怀疑人是否生来就是邪恶的。
invalid  adj. 无效的；有病的；残疾的I hate being treated as an invalid.我讨厌被当作病人对待。The trial was stopped and the results declared invalid.审判被终止了，其结果被宣布无效。We think that those arguments are rendered invalid by the facts.我们认为那些论点在事实面前站不住脚。
invariable  adj. 不变的；常数的There are no absolute, invariable moral rules.没有绝对的，不变的道德准则。
invisible  adj. 无形的，看不见的；无形的；不显眼的，暗藏的The lines were so finely etched as to be invisible from a distance.这些线条蚀刻得如此精细，离远点都看不出来。A thin coil of smoke rose almost invisibly into the sharp, bright sky.一缕轻烟几乎不见踪迹地升上了耀眼的晴空。All the time you are in doubt about the cause of your illness, you are fighting against an invisible enemy.一直以来你都在怀疑自己的病因，你是在和一个无形的敌人斗争。...the tradition that invisibly shapes things in the present.…这种无形地影响着现有事物的传统。It was strange, how invisible a clerk could feel.很奇怪一名职员会感到如此地受人忽视。She takes up the issue of the invisibility of women and women's concerns in society.她着手处理社会上对妇女及其所关注的事物的忽视问题。...The Invisible Man.…《隐身人》。The revenue from tourism is the biggest single item in the country's invisible earnings.旅游收入是该国非贸易性收益中最大的单项收入。
irrespective  adj. 无关的；不考虑的；不顾的...their commitment to a society based on equality for all citizens irrespective of ethnic origin.…他们为建设一个没有种族差别、全民平等的社会所做出的贡献。
irrigate  vt. 灌溉；冲洗；使清新None of the water from Lake Powell is used to irrigate the area.鲍威尔湖的水没有被用来灌溉这一地区。The agricultural land is hilly and the irrigation poor.这片农田多丘陵，而且灌溉条件很差。
jealous  adj. 妒忌的；猜疑的；唯恐失去的；戒备的She got insanely jealous and there was a terrible fight.她变得过分地猜忌，接着是一场激烈的打斗。The formula is jealously guarded.对该配方戒备森严。She was jealous of his wealth.她嫉妒他的富有。Gloria eyed them jealously.格洛丽亚当时嫉妒地看着他们。
jerk  n. 肌肉抽搐；性情古怪的人；蠢人；急拉Mr. Griffin jerked forward in his chair.格里芬先生在椅子上猛地向前一动。"This is Brady Coyne," said Sam, jerking his head in my direction.“这是布雷迪·科因”，萨姆说，他的头朝我这边甩了一下。He indicated the bedroom with a jerk of his head.他用头的猝然一动示意了卧室的方向。The guy is such a jerk! He only cares about himself.这家伙真是个蠢货！他只关心他自己。
jog  vt. 慢跑；轻推；蹒跚行进；使颠簸I got up early the next morning to jog.我次日清晨早起去慢跑了。He went for another early morning jog.他又去晨跑了。It isn't the walking and jogging that got his weight down.不是散步和慢跑使他体重下降了。Avoid jogging the camera.不要碰摄像机。Police have planned a reconstruction of the crime tomorrow in the hope that this will jog the memory of passersby.警方已计划明天再现犯罪过程，希望以此唤起过路人的记忆。
judicial  adj. 公正的，明断的；法庭的；审判上的...an independent judicial system.…一个独立的司法体系。...efforts to manipulate the judicial process.…操纵审判程序的努力。Even if the amendment is passed it can be defeated judicially.即使这项修正案获得了通过，它也有可能通过司法程序被否决。
kidnap  vt. 绑架；诱拐；拐骗Police in Brazil uncovered a plot to kidnap him.巴西警方侦破了一起要绑架他的阴谋。They were middle-class university students, intelligent and educated, yet they chose to kidnap and kill.他们是中产阶级大学生，聪明而且受过教育，却选择了绑架和谋杀。His kidnappers have threatened that they will kill him unless three militants are released from prison.绑架者威胁说，如果不释放3个武装分子出狱，他们就会杀了他。Stewart denies attempted murder and kidnap.斯图尔特否认有谋杀和绑架的企图。
knit  vi. 编织；结合；皱眉I had endless hours to knit and sew.我有无数的时间来缝缝织织。I have already started knitting baby clothes.我已经开始织婴儿的衣服了。Ferris wore a heavy knit sweater.菲立斯穿着一件织得厚厚的毛衣。The best thing about sports is that they knit the whole family close together.体育运动最大的好处就是将全家紧密连接在一起。...a closer-knit family.…一个连接更为紧密的家庭。The bone hasn't knitted together properly.骨头还没有完全愈合。
knot  n. （绳等的）结；节瘤，疙瘩；海里/小时（航速单位）One lace had broken and been tied in a knot.一根带子已经断了，被打成一个结。He knotted the laces securely together.他把带子牢牢地系在一起。He knotted the bandanna around his neck.他把印花大围巾系在他的脖子上。There was a knot of tension in his stomach.他心里一阵紧张。I felt my stomach knot with apprehension.我感到心里因为担心而揪紧。His forehead knotted in a frown.他的眉头紧皱。A carpenter often rejects half his wood because of knots or cracks.木匠常常因为有节疤或裂缝而把一半的木材都扔掉。They travel at speeds of up to 30 knots.他们以高达30节的航速行进。
lace  n. 花边；鞋带；饰带；少量烈酒She finally found the perfect gown, a beautiful creation trimmed with lace.她最终找到了那件完美的大衣，款式漂亮、饰有花边。Barry was sitting on the bed, tying the laces of an old pair of running shoes.巴里正坐在床上系一双旧跑鞋的鞋带。I have a good pair of skates, but no matter how tightly I lace them, my ankles wobble.我有一双很好的溜冰鞋，但是无论我把鞋带系得多么紧，我的脚踝还是在里面晃荡。He sat on the steps, and laced up his boots.他坐在台阶上系好靴子。She laced his food with sleeping pills.她在他的食物里加了安眠药。
lash  vt. 鞭打；冲击；摆动；扎捆；煽动；讽刺...sombre grey eyes, with unusually long lashes.…忧郁的灰眼睛，长着特长的睫毛。Secure the anchor by lashing it to the rail.把锚紧紧地捆在横木上。The shelter is built by lashing poles together to form a small dome.该掩蔽处是把杆子捆到一起形成一个小圆顶而搭建成。The worst winter storms of the century lashed the east coast of North America.本世纪最猛烈的暴风雪袭击了北美的东海岸。She went quiet for a moment while she summoned up the words to lash him.她沉默了一会儿，想了些话来怒斥他。The villagers sentenced one man to five lashes for stealing a ham from his neighbour.村民们判一个男人5下鞭刑，因为他偷了一个邻居的火腿。
lean  vi. 倾斜；倚靠；倾向；依赖Eileen leaned across and opened the passenger door.艾琳探过身来打开了乘客门。She was feeling tired and was glad to lean against him.她感到累了，乐意靠在他身上。Lean the plants against a wall and cover the roots with peat.把这些植物靠在墙上，用泥炭盖住根部。Like most athletes, she was lean and muscular.像大部分运动员一样，她清瘦而且肌肉强健。It is a beautiful meat, very lean and tender.这是一块好肉，又瘦又嫩。...reforms which turned us into a lean and competitive nation.…使我们成为高效率、竞争力强的国家的改革。My parents lived through the lean years of the 1930s.我的父母经历了20世纪30年代的萧条期。

legitimate  adj. 合法的；正当的；合理的；正统的The French government has condemned the coup in Haiti and has demanded the restoration of the legitimate government.法国政府已经谴责了海地的政变，并要求恢复合法政府。The opposition parties do not recognize the political legitimacy of his government.反对党不承认他的政府的政治合法性。That's a perfectly legitimate fear.那是种完全合乎逻辑的恐惧。Sampras beat Carl-Uwe Steeb by 6-1, 6-2, 6-1 to underline the legitimacy of his challenge for the title.桑普拉斯以6比1、6比2和6比1战胜了卡尔-尤韦·斯蒂布，证明了他挑战冠军头衔的合理性。

literal  adj. 文字的；逐字的；无夸张的In many cases, the people there are fighting, in a literal sense, for their homes.多数情况下，那里的人们实际上都是在为他们的家园而战斗。A literal translation of the name Tapies is "walls."名字的字面翻译是“墙”。
litter  n. 垃圾；轿，担架；一窝（动物的幼崽）；凌乱If you see litter in the corridor, pick it up.如果你看到走廊里有垃圾，就把它捡起来。Glass from broken bottles litters the sidewalk.碎瓶子的玻璃渣散落在人行道上。The entrance hall is littered with toys.入口大厅里散落着玩具。History is littered with men and women spurred into achievement by a father's disregard.历史上常有受父亲漠视的刺激而取得成就的男男女女。...a litter of pups.…一窝小狗。
locality  n. 所在；位置；地点Following the discovery of the explosives the president cancelled his visit to the locality.发现爆炸物之后总统取消了对该地区的访问。

log  vi. 伐木He dumped the logs on the big stone hearth.他把木柴扔进那个大石炉里。The family made an official complaint to a ship's officer, which was recorded in the log.这家人向一位高级船员提出过正式投诉，此事记入了航行日志。They log everyone and everything that comes in and out of here.他们把在这里出入的人和发生的事都记入日志。
lubricate  vi. 润滑；涂油；起润滑剂作用Mineral oils are used to lubricate machinery.矿物油被用来润滑机器。Use a touch of linseed oil for lubrication.用一点蓖麻油来润滑一下。
lump  n. 块，块状；肿块；瘤；很多；笨人The potter shaped and squeezed the lump of clay into a graceful shape.制陶工人把一块黏土塑形，压成漂亮的形状。...a lump of wood.…一块木头。I've got a lump on my shoulder.我的肩膀上有个肿块。...a nugget of rough gold about the size of a lump of sugar.…未加工的天然金块，约一块方糖大小。I stood there with a lump in my throat and tried to fight back tears.我站在那儿，喉咙哽咽，拼命忍住眼泪。
machinery  n. 机械；机器；机构；机械装置...quality tools and machinery.…优质工具和机械。The machinery of democracy could be created quickly.民主体制很快就能建立起来。
magistrate  n. 地方法官；文职官员；治安推事She will face a local magistrate on Tuesday.她将在星期二面见一位地方治安法官。
majesty  n. 威严；最高权威，王权；雄伟；权威His Majesty requests your presence in the royal chambers.国王陛下要求你在皇室受召见。...the majesty of the mainland mountains.…大陆山岳的壮美。
make  vt. 使得；进行；布置，准备，整理；制造；认为；获得；形成；安排；引起；构成I'd just like to make a comment.我只想做一下评论。I made a few phone calls.我打了几个电话。Apparently he made a mess of his audition.显然他把试演搞得一团糟。Mary made as if to protest, then hesitated.玛丽似乎要抗议，又犹豫了。Why make do with a copy if you can afford the genuine article?如果你买得起正品，为什么还拿复制品凑合呢？Dirt from the motorway made him cough.公路上的灰尘使他咳嗽起来。The white tips of his shirt collar made him look like a choirboy.他衬衣的白色领尖使他看起来像个唱诗班男童。You can't make me do anything.你不能强迫我做任何事。...James Bond, the role that made him a star.…詹姆斯·邦德，那个使他成为明星的角色。She made life very difficult for me.她使我的生活变得很艰难。They live in fantasy worlds which make Disneyland seem uninventive.他们生活在幻想世界里，那些幻想使迪斯尼乐园也显得毫无创意。He learned enough Spanish to make himself understood.他学的西班牙语足以让别人明白他。He made her a director in his numerous companies.他任命她为他数家公司的主管。We made it into a beautiful home.我们把它变成了一个漂亮的家。This makes the total cost of the bulb and energy $27.这使得灯泡和电量的总耗费升为$27。Lorenzo was a natural leader who made friends easily.洛伦佐是个天生的领导者，结交朋友容易。She made her own bread.她自己做了面包。Having curtains made professionally can be costly.找专业人员制作窗帘会很贵。Mr. Perry made a note in his book.佩里先生在他的书里做了批注。The police don't make the laws, they merely enforce them.警察不制定法律，只是执行法律。I think every business's goal is to make money.我想每笔生意的目的都是赚钱。You could certainly make a case for this point of view.你当然可以为这种观点做解释。The only car parked outside is a black Saab – a different make.停在外面的惟一一辆车是黑色的萨博–一个不同的牌子。She'll make a good actress, if she gets the right training.如果她得到恰当训练，她会成为一名好演员。You've a very good idea there. It will make a good book.你的那个绝妙观点会使之成为一本好书。A group of people made a circle around the Pentagon.一群人绕五角大楼围成了一个圈。Four twos make eight.4个2是8。The athletes are just happy to make the team.那些运动员很高兴加入该队。The engine is gulping two tons of fuel an hour in order to make New Orleans by nightfall.引擎每小时消耗两吨燃料以便在天黑之前赶到新奥尔良。So you did make it to America, after all.这样你终究成功到达了美国。...the hostages who never made it home.…始终没能回家的人质们。I believe I have the talent to make it.我相信我有获得成功的才干。He hadn't been able to make it to our dinner.他没能如约参加我们的晚宴。"How many shots has she got left?"—"I make it two."“她还剩几颗子弹？”–“我估计是两颗。”I make it nearly nine o'clock.我的表上快9:00了。
malicious  adj. 恶意的；恶毒的；蓄意的；怀恨的That might merely have been malicious gossip.那可能只是恶意闲言。...his maliciously accurate imitation of Hubert de Burgh.…他对休伯特·德·伯格的恶意精确模仿。
margin  n. 边缘；利润，余裕；页边的空白They could end up with a 50-point winning margin.他们最后可能会以50点的优势获胜。She added her comments in the margin.她在页边空白处加上了她的评语。The money is collected in a straightforward way with little margin for error.这笔钱是直接募集上来的, 几乎没有出错的余地。...the low coastal plain along the western margin.…沿着西部边缘地带的低洼海岸平原。Students have played an important role in the past, but for the moment, they're on the margins.学生们过去发挥了重要的作用，但现在，他们不再重要了。
massacre  vt. 残杀；彻底击败Maria lost her 62-year-old mother in the massacre.玛丽亚在大屠杀中失去了她62岁的母亲。300 civilians are believed to have been massacred by the rebels.据信300名平民被叛乱分子屠杀了。
massive  adj. 大量的；巨大的，厚重的；魁伟的There was evidence of massive fraud.有证据表明是巨额欺诈。...massive air attacks.…大规模的空袭。...a massively popular game.…一种非常受欢迎的游戏。He died six weeks later of a massive heart attack.他6周后死于一次严重的心脏病发作。
mastermind  vt. 策划There are many theories as to who masterminded the attacks.关于谁策划了这些攻击，有许多的猜测。He was the mastermind behind the plan to acquire the explosives.他是获取炸药计划的幕后操纵者。
melody  n. 旋律；歌曲；美妙的音乐I whistle melodies from Beethoven and Vivaldi and the more popular classical composers.我用口哨吹贝多芬、维瓦尔迪和更大众化一些的古典作曲家的曲子。
melt  vi. 熔化，溶解；渐混The snow had melted, but the lake was still frozen solid.雪已经融化了，但湖面仍然冻得结结实实。Meanwhile, melt the white chocolate in a bowl suspended over simmering water.同时，把碗架在快烧开的水上，融化碗里的白巧克力。His anxiety about the outcome melted, only to return later.他对结果的焦虑消失了，但过后又来了。When he heard these words, Scot felt his inner doubts melt away.听到这些话，斯科特觉得内心的疑虑消失了。The youths dispersed and melted into the darkness.年轻人们散开了，消失在夜色中。
memorial  n. 纪念碑，纪念馆；纪念仪式；纪念物Building a memorial to Columbus has been his lifelong dream.建一座哥伦布纪念碑一直是他一生的梦想。A memorial service is being held for her at St. Paul's Church.一场为她举行的纪念仪式正在圣保罗教堂举行。The museum will serve as a memorial to the millions who passed through Ellis Island.这个博物馆将成为曾经过埃利斯岛的数百万人的纪念馆。
memorize  vt. 记住，背熟；记忆He studied his map, trying to memorize the way to Rose's street.他研究了地图，努力记住去罗丝家那条街的路。
menace  n. 威胁；恐吓In my view, you are a menace to the public.在我看来，你对公众是一个威胁。You're a menace to my privacy, Kenton.你是个侵犯我隐私的讨厌的人，肯顿。There is a pervading sense of menace.有一种在蔓延的危险感。They seem determined to menace the United States and its allies.他们好像决心要威胁美国及其盟国。
migrate  vi. 移动；随季节而移居；移往People migrate to cities like Jakarta in search of work.人们移居到雅加达这样的城市找工作。...the migration of Soviet Jews to Israel.…苏联犹太人向以色列的迁移。Most birds have to fly long distances to migrate.大多数的鸟类不得不飞行很长的距离进行迁徙。...the migration of animals in the Serengeti.…塞伦盖蒂的动物迁徙。
militant  adj. 好战的Militant mine workers in the Ukraine have voted for a one-day stoppage next month.在乌克兰，激进的煤矿工人们已经投票决定在下个月进行一天的罢工。Even now we could not be sure that the militants would not find some new excuse to call a strike the following winter.即使到现在，我们也不能确定这些激进分子不会找到某个新的借口在下一年冬天号召一场罢工。...the rise of trade union militancy.…工会好战情绪的高涨。
moan  vi. 抱怨，悲叹；呻吟Tony moaned in his sleep and then turned over on his side.托尼在睡梦中呻吟了一下，然后转身侧躺。Suddenly she gave a low, choking moan and began to tremble violently.突然她发出了一声低沉、令人窒息的呻吟，身体开始剧烈地抖动。I used to moan if I didn't get at least six hours' sleep at night.我过去常常抱怨晚上睡不够6小时。...moaning about the weather.…抱怨天气。They have been listening to people's moans and praise.他们一直在倾听人民的抱怨与称赞。
mobilize  vt. 动员，调动；集合，组织；使…流通；使…松动The best hope is that we will mobilize international support and get down to action.最大的希望就是我们将动员国际社会的支持，开始行动。...the rapid mobilization of international opinion in support of the revolution.…对支持革命的国际舆论的迅速动员。If you could mobilize the resources, you could get it done.如果你能调动资源，你就能完成它。...the mobilization of resources for education.…调动教育资源。Sudan even threatened to mobilize in response to the ultimatums.苏丹甚至威胁说要动用军事力量来回应最后通牒。...a demand for full-scale mobilization to defend the republic.…全面动员来保卫共和国的命令。
mock  n. 英国模拟考试（mocks）I thought you were mocking me.我以为你在嘲笑我。"It's tragic!" swoons Jeffrey in mock horror.“太悲惨了！”杰弗里假装害怕得昏了过去。
modify  vt. 修改，修饰；更改The club members did agree to modify their recruitment policy.俱乐部成员确已同意修改他们的入会政策。Relatively minor modifications were required.需要相对较小的修改。
moist  adj. 潮湿的；多雨的；含泪的The soil is reasonably moist after the September rain.9月的雨水之后，土壤适度湿润。
